### [30] [Text-Graph Synergy: A Bidirectional Verification and Completion Framework for RAG](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05643v1)
*Jiarui Zhong,Hong Cai Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出文本-图双向校验补全的RAG框架，属于通用检索增强agent方法。

TL;DR: TGS-RAG通过双向文本-图协同增强机制解决信息孤岛问题，在多跳推理任务上超越现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RAG方法（文本或图）存在伪证据、剪枝丢失推理路径等问题，混合方法未能解决非对称推理流导致的信息孤岛问题。

Method: 提出TGS-RAG统一框架，包含图到文本通道（全局投票策略）和文本到图通道（记忆孤立实体桥接算法），实现双向协同增强。

Result: 在多个多跳推理基准上显著优于SOTA基线，在检索精度和计算效率之间取得更好平衡。

Conclusion: TGS-RAG有效解决信息孤岛问题，提升多跳推理性能，且无需额外数据库开销。

中文摘要：检索增强生成（RAG）已成为增强大语言模型（LLMs）事实基础和多跳推理的核心范式。传统的基于文本的RAG常常检索到逻辑不相关的伪证据，而基于图的RAG则常受限于搜索时剪枝，可能丢弃潜在有效的推理路径。现有的混合方法主要采用简单的证据拼接或单向增强，未能解决由非结构化文本与结构化图之间非对称推理流导致的根本性“信息孤岛”问题。我们提出TGS-RAG，一个用于文本-图协同增强的统一框架。TGS-RAG引入双向机制：（i）图到文本通道，采用从已访问图节点出发的全局投票策略，对文本证据进行重新排序和精炼，过滤语义噪声；（ii）文本到图通道，利用基于记忆的孤立实体桥接算法。该算法利用文本线索，主动从搜索历史中复活有效但先前被剪枝的推理路径，且无需额外数据库开销。在多个多跳推理基准上的实验结果表明，TGS-RAG显著优于最先进的基线，在检索精度和计算效率之间实现了优越的平衡。

Original abstract: Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) has become a core paradigm for enhancing factual grounding and multi-hop reasoning in Large Language Models (LLMs). Traditional text-based RAG often retrieves logically irrelevant pseudo-evidence, while graph-based RAG is frequently hindered by search-time pruning, which may discard potentially valid reasoning paths. Existing hybrid approaches primarily adopt simple evidence concatenation or unidirectional enhancement, which fails to address the fundamental "Information Island" problem caused by asymmetric reasoning flows between unstructured text and structured graphs. We propose \textbf{TGS-RAG}, a unified framework for \textbf{T}ext-\textbf{G}raph \textbf{S}ynergistic enhancement. TGS-RAG introduces a bidirectional mechanism: (i) a \textbf{Graph-to-Text} channel that employs a Global Voting strategy from visited graph nodes to re-rank and refine textual evidence, filtering out semantic noise; and (ii) a \textbf{Text-to-Graph} channel that utilizes the \textbf{Memory-based Orphan Entity Bridging} algorithm. This algorithm utilizes textual cues to proactively resurrect valid but previously pruned reasoning paths from the search history without additional database overhead. Experimental results on multiple multi-hop reasoning benchmarks demonstrate that TGS-RAG significantly outperforms state-of-the-art baselines, achieving a superior balance between retrieval precision and computational efficiency.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有系统选择编排拓扑时不考虑代码结构复杂度，导致路由问题。

Method: 从分层代码索引提取结构复杂度向量，据此选择拓扑；采用六维预算向量约束子智能体；结合复杂度条件路由与形式资源代数。

中文摘要：面向代码生成的多智能体LLM系统面临一个基本的路由问题：最优的编排拓扑取决于所修改代码的结构复杂度，然而现有系统在选择拓扑时并未咨询代码库。我们提出检索引导自适应编排（RGAO），一种通过从分层代码索引中提取结构复杂度向量后再选择编排拓扑来闭合此循环的架构。RGAO运行于Code-Agent框架内，该框架的子智能体受具有六维预算向量的正式契约约束。我们的主要贡献是将两个先前独立的工作——复杂度条件LLM路由与形式资源代数——组合起来，产生了一个两者单独都无法实现的特性：在检索条件动态拓扑选择下的可证明预算守恒。具体贡献包括：（1）一个复杂度条件拓扑路由器，将代理测量的误路由率从30.1%降低到8.2%；（2）一个带有结构归纳守恒定理的预算代数；（3）一个分层代码检索引擎。实证评估展示了亚毫秒级DAG构建和线性树索引可扩展性。

Original abstract: Multi-agent LLM systems for code generation face a fundamental routing problem: the optimal orchestration topology depends on the structural complexity of the code under modification, yet existing systems select topologies without consulting the codebase. We present Retrieval-Guided Adaptive Orchestration (RGAO), an architecture that closes this loop by extracting a structural complexity vector from a hierarchical code index before selecting the orchestration topology. RGAO operates within Code-Agent, a multi-agent framework whose sub-agents are governed by formal contracts with six-dimensional budget vectors. Our headline contribution is the composition of two previously separate lines of work -- complexity-conditioned LLM routing and formal resource algebras -- yielding a property neither admits alone: provable budget conservation under retrieval-conditioned dynamic topology selection. Concretely we contribute: (1) a complexity-conditioned topology router that reduces proxy-measured misrouting from 30.1% to 8.2%; (2) a budget algebra with a structural-induction conservation theorem; and (3) a hierarchical code retrieval engine. Empirical evaluation demonstrates sub-millisecond DAG construction and linear tree-index scalability.

### [32] [Chain of Risk: Safety Failures in Large Reasoning Models and Mitigation via Adaptive Multi-Principle Steering](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05678v1)
*Xiaomin Li,Jianheng Hou,Zheyuan Deng,Zhiwei Zhang,Taoran Li,Binghang Lu,Bing Hu,Yunhan Zhao,Yuexing Hao*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 研究推理模型安全失败并提出自适应多原则引导，涉及agent安全控制。

TL;DR: 大规模推理模型的推理轨迹会暴露最终答案中不存在的安全风险，提出自适应多原则引导方法可有效降低不安全内容，且保持高准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 最终答案的安全不能完全代表推理轨迹的安全，存在泄漏和逃避两种高风险失败模式，需全面评估推理过程。

Method: 基于20条安全原则对推理和答案分别评分，提出自适应多原则引导，为每条原则学习安全-不安全激活方向，在推理时选择性激活。

Result: 在15个模型上测试，推理轨迹揭示更多风险；自适应引导在三个模型上平均减少40.8%不安全计数，准确率保持97.7%。

Conclusion: LRM安全性应评估整个推理-答案轨迹，而不仅限于最终答案，自适应引导是一种有效的测试时缓解方法。

中文摘要：大规模推理模型（LRMs）日益将类思维链推理用于透明性、验证和深思熟虑的问题解决。这造成了一个安全盲点：即使最终答案看起来安全，推理轨迹中也可能出现有害或违反政策的内容。我们通过在一个统一的20条原则安全准则下对两个阶段进行评分，来测试最终答案安全是否足以代表整个推理-答案轨迹。使用来自七个公共危害和越狱来源的提示，加上四个分布外（OOD）来源，我们评估了15个开源权重和基于API的LRM，每个模型处理41K个提示。推理轨迹始终暴露出超出最终答案的额外安全风险，特别是在高严重性的阶段级失败中：泄漏情况（不安全推理后跟安全答案）和逃避情况（看似安全的推理后跟不安全答案）。原则级分析显示风险集中在错误信息、法律合规、歧视、身体伤害和心理伤害。我们进一步提出了自适应多原则引导，这是一种白盒测试时缓解方法，为每个安全原则学习一个从“不安全”到“安全”的激活方向，并仅激活那些当前隐藏状态更接近不安全质心而非安全质心的方向。在三个可引导的开放推理模型上，自适应引导在保留基准和OOD基准上的推理轨迹和最终答案中减少了不安全计数。DeepSeek-R1-Qwen-7B在BBH、GSM8K和MMLU上平均不安全计数减少40.8%，同时保留97.7%的宏观平均准确率。这些结果表明，LRM的安全性应该在整个暴露的推理-答案轨迹上进行评估和缓解，而不仅仅是在最终答案阶段。

Original abstract: Large reasoning models (LRMs) increasingly expose chain-of-thought-like reasoning for transparency, verification, and deliberate problem solving. This creates a safety blind spot: harmful or policy-violating content may appear in reasoning traces even when final answers appear safe. We test whether final-answer safety is a sufficient proxy for the full reasoning-answer trajectory by scoring both stages under a unified twenty-principle safety rubric. Using prompts from seven public harmfulness and jailbreak sources, plus four out-of-distribution (OOD) sources, we evaluate 15 open-weight and API-based LRMs across 41K prompts per model. Reasoning traces consistently reveal additional safety risks beyond final answers, especially in high-severity stage-wise failures: leak cases, where unsafe reasoning precedes a safe-looking answer, and escape cases, where benign-looking reasoning precedes an unsafe final response. Principle-level analysis shows that risk concentrates in misinformation, legal compliance, discrimination, physical harm, and psychological harm. We further propose adaptive multi-principle steering, a white-box test-time mitigation that learns one unsafe-to-safe activation direction per safety principle and activates only directions whose current hidden state is closer to the unsafe than safe centroid. On three steerable open reasoning models, adaptive steering reduces unsafe counts in both reasoning traces and final answers on held-out and OOD benchmarks. DeepSeek-R1-Qwen-7B achieves a 40.8% average unsafe-count reduction while retaining 97.7% macro-averaged accuracy on BBH, GSM8K, and MMLU. These results suggest that LRM safety should be evaluated and mitigated over the full exposed reasoning-answer trajectory, not only at the final-answer stage.

</details>


### [33] [Inference-Time Budget Control for LLM Search Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05701v1)
*Zhengru Fang,Senkang Forest Hu,Zhonghao Chang,Yu Guo,Yihang Tao,Hongyao Liu,Mengzhe Ruan,Jun Huang,Yuguang Fang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 直接研究LLM搜索agent推理预算控制，提出价值导向的预算分配方法

TL;DR: 本文提出两阶段推理时预算控制方法，通过信息价值分数指导搜索预算分配，并通过选择性答案改写提升多跳问答性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM搜索代理受限于工具调用和生成令牌的双重预算，缺乏对搜索动作和答案提交的细粒度控制，导致效率低下。

Method: 提出两阶段预算控制：搜索时根据信息价值（VOI）分数选择动作（检索、分解或提交）；搜索后通过证据驱动的最终处理器选择性改写答案。

Result: 在四个多跳QA基准上，使用三个LLM骨干和四个预算水平，该方法在严格双重预算下优于四个基线，消融显示搜索时预算控制（特别是预算依赖惩罚）贡献最大。

Conclusion: 推理时预算控制应同时管理搜索中的预算使用和最终答案的提交方式，以提升LLM搜索代理的性能。

中文摘要：LLM搜索代理在推理时越来越依赖工具，但它们的轨迹通常受到工具调用和生成令牌的严格限制。在这种双重预算下，更好的答案不仅需要更强的模型，还需要明确控制哪个搜索动作应该接收下一个预算单位，以及累积的证据何时足以确定最终答案。我们在多跳问答（QA）中研究这个问题，并将其形式化为两阶段的推理时预算控制。在搜索阶段，我们的控制器为每个可行动作分配一个任务级别的信息价值（VOI）分数，定义为在当前搜索状态和剩余双重预算下每单位预算的边际任务价值的操作估计，并使用该分数在检索、分解和答案提交中进行选择。搜索后，一个选择性的基于证据的最终处理器将轨迹答案与改进的候选答案进行比较，并且仅在残余误差似乎是低风险的答案形式错误时才重写。在四个多跳QA基准、三个LLM骨干和四个预算水平上，该方法在相同的严格双重预算协议下，相对于四个审计基线产生了正的总体收益。消融实验表明，搜索时预算控制（尤其是依赖于预算的惩罚）提供了主要的性能提升，而答案时控制主要在有足够检索路径时有所帮助。这些结果表明，LLM搜索代理的推理时预算控制应该同时管理搜索过程中预算的使用方式以及最终答案的提交方式。

Original abstract: LLM search agents increasingly rely on tools at inference time, but their trajectories are often constrained by hard limits on both tool calls and generated tokens. Under such dual budgets, better answers require not only stronger models, but also explicit control over which search action should receive the next budget unit and when the accumulated evidence is sufficient to commit a final answer. We study this problem in multi-hop question answering (QA) and formulate it as two-stage inference-time budget control. At search time, our controller assigns each feasible action a task-level Value-of-Information (VOI) score, defined as an operational estimate of marginal task value per unit budget under the current search state and remaining dual budget, and uses this score to choose among retrieval, decomposition, and answer commitment. After search, a selective evidence-grounded finalizer compares the trajectory answer with a refined candidate and rewrites only when the residual error appears to be a low-risk answer-form error. Across four multi-hop QA benchmarks, three LLM backbones, and four budget levels, the method yields positive aggregate gains over four audited baselines under the same hard dual-budget protocol. Ablations show that search-time budget control, especially budget-dependent penalty, provides the main performance gain, while answer-time control helps mainly when the retrieval path is already adequate. These results suggest that inference-time budget control for LLM search agents should govern both how budget is spent during search and how the final answer is committed.

</details>


### [34] [Knowledge-Graph Paths as Intermediate Supervision for Self-Evolving Search Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05702v1)
*Huyu Wu,Jun Liu,Xiaochi Wei,Yan Gao,Yi Wu,Yao Hu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 自演化搜索agent利用知识图谱路径作为过程监督，提升自我改进能力

TL;DR: 通过重用知识图谱路径作为中间监督，解决SSP框架中问题构建和奖励稀疏的瓶颈，提升多跳QA性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: SSP框架中提议者因缺乏关系上下文生成无效问题，求解器仅接收二元奖励丢失部分正确轨迹信息，限制自我进化搜索代理的效果。

Method: 利用LLM引导的知识图谱子图进行问题构建，并提出路标覆盖奖励（WCR）基于构建路径实体覆盖度给予部分学分。

Result: 在七个QA基准和九种模型配置中，改方法在所有配置中平均分数优于标准SSP，尤其在多跳QA任务上有显著提升。

Conclusion: 知识图谱路径可作为轻量级中间监督，无需额外人工标注即可提供关系指导和过程反馈，有效提升搜索代理的自我进化能力。

中文摘要：自我进化的搜索代理通过生成和解决自己的搜索任务，减少了对人工编写训练问题的依赖。我们基于搜索自我对弈（SSP）框架，这是一种代表性的提议者和求解器框架，其中问题通过多步搜索和推理被生成和回答。然而，在实践中，SSP面临两个瓶颈：提议者从孤立的答案实体构建问题，缺乏关系上下文，导致在早期自我对弈训练中产生许多无效或不可验证的问题；而求解器仅接收二元结果奖励，丢弃了部分正确搜索轨迹中的有用信号。我们通过重用知识图谱路径作为构建派生的中间监督来解决这两个瓶颈，既用于问题构建也用于奖励塑造。首先，我们将问题构建基于LLM引导的知识图谱子图，为提议者提供关系上下文。其次，我们观察到构建和解决一个多跳问题可能涉及重叠的中间实体：用于构建问题的事实桥可能为解决它提供近似路标。利用这种重叠，我们引入了路标覆盖奖励（WCR），该奖励根据错误求解器轨迹对构建路径上实体的覆盖程度给予分级部分学分，同时保持对正确答案的完整奖励。在七个QA基准测试和九种模型配置中，我们的方法在所有配置中都比标准SSP提高了平均分数，包括在多跳QA任务上的显著提升。这些结果表明，知识图谱路径可以重用为轻量级中间监督，不需要额外的任务特定人工注释或手动标记的过程步骤即可提供关系指导和过程反馈。

Original abstract: Self-evolving search agents reduce reliance on human-written training questions by generating and solving their own search tasks. We build on Search Self-Play (SSP), a representative Proposer and Solver framework in which questions are generated and answered via multi-step search and reasoning. In practice, however, SSP faces two bottlenecks: the Proposer constructs questions from isolated answer entities without relational context, yielding many invalid or unverifiable questions in early self-play training, while the Solver receives only a binary outcome reward that discards useful signal from partially on-track search trajectories. We address both bottlenecks by reusing knowledge-graph paths as construction-derived intermediate supervision for both question construction and reward shaping. First, we ground question construction in LLM-guided knowledge-graph subgraphs, providing relational context for the Proposer. Second, we observe that constructing and solving a multi-hop question can involve overlapping intermediate entities: the factual bridges used to formulate the question may provide approximate waypoints for answering it. Exploiting this overlap, we introduce Waypoint Coverage Reward (WCR), which grants graded partial credit to incorrect Solver trajectories according to their coverage of entities on the construction path, while preserving full reward for correct answers. Across seven QA benchmarks and nine model configurations, our approach improves the average score over standard SSP in all configurations, including notable gains on multi-hop QA tasks. These results suggest that knowledge-graph paths can be reused as lightweight intermediate supervision, providing both relational guidance and process feedback without additional task-specific human annotations or manually labeled process steps.

</details>


### [35] [More Is Not Always Better: Cross-Component Interference in LLM Agent Scaffolding](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05716v1)
*Ming Liu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 系统研究LLM agent组件间的干扰，揭示全组件组合非最优，对agent设计有直接指导价值

TL;DR: 通过全因子实验发现，LLM智能体系统中堆叠更多组件反而因跨组件干扰导致性能下降，最优子集通常小于全包含，且组件间存在复杂交互。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 挑战LLM智能体系统中“越多组件越好”的默认假设，研究组件间破坏性交互（CCI）对性能的影响。

Method: 在HotpotQA和GSM8K数据集上，使用Llama-3.1-8B/70B模型，对规划、工具、记忆、自我反思、检索五种组件的所有32个子集进行全因子实验（共96个条件，最多10种子），并采用主效应回归、Shapley值和次模性分析量化组件交互。

Result: 全包含系统始终非最优：HotpotQA上单工具优于全包含32%，GSM8K上3组件子集优于全包含79%。最优组件数（1-4）因任务和模型规模而异。发现56.3%的次模性违反，表明贪婪选择不可靠。工具使用、自我反思和检索间存在三体协同效应（+0.175）。CCI在Qwen2.5和提示改写下稳健。

Conclusion: 应摒弃最大装备的智能体默认设置，采用基于交互感知分析的任务特定子集选择，以最大化性能。

中文摘要：LLM智能体系统通过堆叠脚手架组件（规划、工具、记忆、自我反思、检索）构建，假设越多越好。我们研究了跨组件干扰（CCI）：组件间破坏性交互导致的性能下降。我们在HotpotQA和GSM8K上，使用Llama-3.1-8B/70B（96个条件，最多10个种子）对所有2^5=32个五组件子集进行了全因子实验。全包含系统始终是次优的：在HotpotQA上，单工具智能体比全包含系统高出32%（F1 0.233 vs 0.177，p=0.023）；在GSM8K上，一个3组件子集比全包含系统高出79%（0.43 vs 0.24，p=0.010）。最优组件数量取决于任务（k*=1-4）且对规模敏感：在70B下，在8B上造成伤害的组合反而带来收益，尽管全包含系统仍落后于最佳子集。我们拟合了主效应回归（R^2=0.916，adj-R^2=0.899，LOOCV=0.872），计算了精确的Shapley值，并发现183/325个次模性违反（56.3%），表明贪婪选择不可靠。作为探索性分析，我们报告了工具使用、自我反思和检索之间的三体协同效应（INT_3=+0.175，95%置信区间[+0.003,+0.351]）。CCI在不同模型系列（Qwen2.5）中复现，且对提示改写鲁棒。我们的发现表明，最大装备的智能体默认设置应被通过交互感知分析的任务特定子集选择所取代。

Original abstract: LLM agent systems are built by stacking scaffolding components (planning, tools, memory, self-reflection, retrieval) assuming more is better. We study cross-component interference (CCI): degradation when components interact destructively. We run a full factorial experiment over all 2^5=32 subsets of five components on HotpotQA and GSM8K with Llama-3.1-8B/70B (96 conditions, up to 10 seeds). The All-In system is consistently suboptimal: on HotpotQA, a single-tool agent surpasses All-In by 32% (F1 0.233 vs 0.177, p=0.023); on GSM8K, a 3-component subset beats All-In by 79% (0.43 vs 0.24, p=0.010). Optimal component count is task-dependent (k*=1-4) and scale-sensitive: at 70B, combinations that hurt at 8B provide gains, though All-In still trails the best subset. We fit a main-effects regression (R^2=0.916, adj-R^2=0.899, LOOCV=0.872), compute exact Shapley values, and find 183/325 submodularity violations (56.3%), showing greedy selection is unreliable. A three-body synergy among Tool Use, Self-Reflection, and Retrieval (INT_3=+0.175, 95% CI [+0.003,+0.351]) is reported as exploratory. CCI replicates across model families (Qwen2.5) and is robust to prompt paraphrasing. Our findings suggest maximally-equipped agent defaults should be replaced by task-specific subset selection via interaction-aware analysis.

</details>


### [36] [Detecting Time Series Anomalies Like an Expert: A Multi-Agent LLM Framework with Specialized Analyzers](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05725v1)
*Hyeongwon Kang,Jeongseob Kim,Jinwoo Park,Pilsung Kang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 多agent框架用于时间序列异常检测，分解分析+证据融合机制对通用agent设计有参考价值

TL;DR: SAGE是一个多智能体框架，通过分解异常诊断任务并使用多个专门分析器和证据整合，显著提高了时间序列异常检测的可控性、可解释性和可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法依赖单一通用模型直接推断异常，导致对复杂异常模式的可控性、可解释性和可靠性不足。

Method: SAGE将异常分析分解为四个专门分析器（点、结构、季节性和模式异常），每个使用家族特定工具和可视化生成证据，然后由证据检测器整合为置信度分数的异常记录，最后监督器生成诊断报告；并通过合成正常参考片段构建上下文示例。

Result: 在三个基准测试中，SAGE在ML/DL和语言模型基线中取得最佳平均性能；消融和人工评估表明检测可靠性和诊断有用性提升。

Conclusion: SAGE通过多智能体分解和证据整合，有效提升了时间序列异常检测的可靠性、可控性和可解释性，具有实际应用价值。

中文摘要：最近的研究探索了将大语言模型用于时间序列异常检测，然而现有方法通常依赖单一的通用模型直接推断异常指标或区间，限制了对复杂异常模式的可控性、可解释性和可靠性。我们提出了SAGE（专业分析器组实现类似专家的检测），一个用于单变量时间序列结构化异常诊断的多智能体框架。它将异常分析分解为四个专门的分析器：点异常、结构异常、季节性异常和模式异常。每个分析器应用特定家族的数值工具和诊断可视化生成证据，而一个基于证据的检测器将证据整合为带有置信度分数的异常记录，包括区间和候选类型。然后，一个监督器将这些结构化记录转换为面向分析师诊断报告。SAGE进一步从正常参考训练片段构建合成的上下文示例，而不使用真实的异常片段或异常类型标签作为上下文示例。在三个基准测试中，SAGE在强大的ML/DL和基于语言模型的基线中取得了最佳平均性能。消融研究和人工评估进一步表明，所提出的框架提高了检测可靠性和诊断输出的实际有用性。

Original abstract: Recent studies have explored large language models for time-series anomaly detection, yet existing approaches often rely on a single general-purpose model to directly infer anomaly indices or intervals, limiting controllability, interpretability, and reliability for complex anomaly patterns. We propose SAGE (Specialized Analyzer Group for Expert-like Detection), a multi-agent framework for structured anomaly diagnosis in univariate time series. It decomposes anomaly analysis into four specialized Analyzers for point, structural, seasonal, and pattern anomalies. Each Analyzer applies family-specific numerical tools and diagnostic visualizations to generate evidence, while an evidence-grounded Detector consolidates the evidence into confidence-scored anomaly records with intervals and candidate types. A Supervisor then converts these structured records into analyst-facing diagnostic reports. SAGE further constructs synthetic in-context examples from normal-reference training segments, without using real anomalous segments or anomaly-type labels as in-context examples. Across three benchmarks, SAGE achieves the best average performance among strong ML/DL and language-model-based baselines. Ablation studies and human evaluation further show that the proposed framework improves detection reliability and the practical usefulness of diagnostic outputs.

</details>


### [37] [SkillRet: A Large-Scale Benchmark for Skill Retrieval in LLM Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05726v1)
*Hongcheol Cho,Ryangkyung Kang,Youngeun Kim*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 构建大规模技能检索基准，直接服务于LLM agent技能选择与检索研究

TL;DR: 提出SkillRet，一个大规模技能检索基准，包含17,810个技能和63,259个训练样本，发现现有检索器表现不佳，微调可显著提升性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有技能检索研究不足，缺乏大规模基准和对现实技能库检索行为的理解。

Method: 构建SkillRet基准，包含17,810个公共代理技能、结构化标签和两层级分类，提供训练和评估数据；对多种检索器进行评测并进行任务特定微调。

Result: 微调后在NDCG@10上比最强先前检索器高13.1点，比最强现成检索器高16.9点，增益来自更好聚焦于长查询中的技能相关信号。

Conclusion: SkillRet作为大规模代理系统中技能检索的强基准和基础，揭示了当前方法的不足并展示了微调的有效性。

中文摘要：随着LLM代理越来越多地部署有大量可重用技能库，为用户请求选择正确的技能已成为一个关键的系统挑战。在小规模库中，用户可以通过名称显式调用技能，但随着技能生态系统在紧张的上下文和延迟预算下增长，这一假设不再成立。尽管具有实际重要性，技能检索仍然研究不足，基准测试有限，且对现实技能库上的检索行为了解甚少。为弥补这一差距，我们引入了SkillRet，一个用于LLM代理中技能检索的大规模基准。SkillRet包含17,810个公共代理技能，组织有结构化语义标签和两层级分类法，涵盖6个主要类别和18个子类别。它提供了63,259个训练样本和4,997个具有不重叠技能池的评估查询，支持基准测试和面向检索的训练。在一系列不同的检索器上，我们发现技能检索远未解决：现成模型在现实大规模技能库上表现不佳，先前的技能检索模型仍有很大提升空间。在SkillRet上进行任务特定微调显著提升了性能，在NDCG@10上比最强先前检索器提高了13.1点，比最强现成检索器提高了16.9点。我们的进一步分析表明，这些提升是因为微调模型能更好地关注长且嘈杂查询中的少量技能相关信号。这些结果确立了SkillRet作为大规模代理系统中检索研究的强大基准和基础。

Original abstract: As LLM agents are increasingly deployed with large libraries of reusable skills, selecting the right skill for a user request has become a critical systems challenge. In small libraries, users may invoke skills explicitly by name, but this assumption breaks down as skill ecosystems grow under tight context and latency budgets. Despite its practical importance, skill retrieval remains underexplored, with limited benchmarks and little understanding of retrieval behavior on realistic skill libraries. To address this gap, we introduce SkillRet, a large-scale benchmark for skill retrieval in LLM agents. SkillRet contains 17,810 public agent skills, organized with structured semantic tags and a two-level taxonomy spanning 6 major categories and 18 sub-categories. It provides 63,259 training samples and 4,997 evaluation queries with disjoint skill pools, enabling both benchmarking and retrieval-oriented training. Across a diverse set of retrievers, we find that skill retrieval remains far from solved: off-the-shelf models struggle on realistic large-scale skill libraries, and prior skill-retrieval models still leave substantial headroom. Task-specific fine-tuning on SkillRet substantially improves performance, improving NDCG@10 by +13.1 points over the strongest prior retriever and by +16.9 points over the strongest off-the-shelf retriever. Our analysis further suggests that these gains arise because fine-tuned models better focus on the small skill-relevant signals within long and noisy queries. These results establish SkillRet as a strong benchmark and foundation for future research on retrieval in large-scale agent systems.

### [38] [ReFlect: An Effective Harness System for Complex Long-Horizon LLM Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05737v1)
*Fan Huang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出推理harness系统用于错误检测与恢复，提升长程任务成功率，可迁移至agent可靠性

TL;DR: 提出ReFlect，一种模型无关、无需训练的推理封装系统，通过独立错误检测与恢复显著提升LLM在长时程任务上的成功率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有推理范式（CoT、ReAct、自我批评）在长时程多阶段任务中因错误累积而失败，且自我批评效果差（90%无问题、76%接受错误答案），需要自动检测和恢复错误的推理系统。

Method: 设计ReFlect作为确定性封装，包含独立的错误检测和恢复逻辑；在6个推理领域进行受控实验，比较Direct CoT、自我批评和ReFlect；评估6种模型；尝试添加结构化状态和操作符但发现小规模模型无法可靠使用。

Result: ReFlect在6个模型上任务成功率提升7-29个百分点；SWE-bench补丁质量从0%提升至82-87%；Harness增益与基线成功率成反比（斜率-1.69）；结构化状态方法在70B模型上效果有限（15-18.7%）。

Conclusion: ReFlect是一种简单有效的推理增强方法，模型无关、无需训练，通过直接错误检测和恢复机制显著改善LLM在复杂推理任务上的表现，且增益与模型原有能力负相关。

中文摘要：当前的LLM推理范式包括思维链、ReAct和事后自我批评。这些范式依赖于两个在长时程、多阶段任务中失败的假设。因此，错误在推理步骤中默默累积，留下一个开放性问题：推理系统能否有效检测并从自身故障中恢复？我们提出了ReFlect，一个用于LLM推理的harness系统，它创建了独立的错误检测和恢复逻辑，作为模型的确定性封装。在6个推理领域的受控实验表明，提示级别的自我批评会产生公式化的模板，在100个审核的反思块中有90个未标记问题，并且所研究的LLM在至少76%的情况下错误地接受了错误答案。我们的ReFlect harness在跨越小规模和前沿规模的六个模型上实现了从gpt-4o-mini的41%到Claude Sonnet 4.5的56%的任务成功率，相对于Direct CoT的每个模型提升从Qwen2.5-72B的+7个百分点到Claude Sonnet 4.5的+29个百分点，并且还将SWE-bench补丁结构质量从0%（Direct CoT）提高到82%（Qwen2.5-72B）到87%（GPT-4o）。值得注意的是，harness增益与模型的Direct CoT任务成功率成反比（拟合斜率为-1.69，r=-0.76）：基线成功率每损失一个百分点，harness增益就机械地恢复1.69个百分点。我们注意到，添加结构化推理状态和操作符在Llama-3.3-70B和Qwen2.5-72B上仅产生15.0-18.7%的配对平均值，因为这种规模的模型无法可靠地填充其操作符所需的状态。ReFlect是模型无关的、无需训练的，并且完全在推理时运行。

Original abstract: Current reasoning paradigms for LLMs include chain-of-thought, ReAct, and post-hoc self-critique. These paradigms rely on two assumptions that fail on long-horizon, multi-stage tasks. As a result, errors accumulate silently across reasoning steps, leaving an open question: can a reasoning system effectively detect and recover from its own failures? We present ReFlect, a \emph{harness} system for LLM reasoning that creates standalone error detection and recovery logic as a deterministic wrapper around the model. Controlled experiments across 6 reasoning domains show that prompt-level self-critique produces formulaic templates that flag no issues in 90 of 100 audited reflection blocks, and the investigated LLMs wrongly accept a wrong answer in at least 76\% of cases. Our ReFlect harness achieves task success rates ranging from 41\% on gpt-4o-mini to 56\% on Claude Sonnet 4.5 across six models spanning small and frontier scale, with per-model gains over Direct CoT ranging from +7 pp on Qwen2.5-72B to +29 pp on Claude Sonnet 4.5, and additionally raises SWE-bench patch-structural quality from 0\% (Direct CoT) to between 82\% (Qwen2.5-72B) and 87\% (GPT-4o). Notably, the harness gain is inversely proportional to the model's Direct CoT task success rate (the fitted slope is -1.69 with r=-0.76): each pp lost in baseline success rate is mechanically recovered by 1.69 pp of harness gain. We spot that adding structured reasoning state and operators yields only 15.0--18.7\% pair-mean on Llama-3.3-70B and Qwen2.5-72B because models at this scale cannot reliably populate the state its operators require. ReFlect is model-agnostic, training-free, and operates entirely at inference time.

</details>


### [39] [Long-Horizon Q-Learning: Accurate Value Learning via n-Step Inequalities](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05812v2)
*Armaan A. Abraham,Lucy Xiaoyang Shi,Chelsea Finn*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出长视界Q-learning方法稳定值函数学习，可改善agent长程任务中的训练稳定性

TL;DR: 提出长时域Q学习（LQL），通过铰链损失惩罚最优性收紧界限的违反，在不增加计算开销的情况下稳定Q学习，在多个基准上优于传统TD方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准Q学习中的自举导致长时域下估计误差向后传播并累积，使得学习不稳定。

Method: LQL基于最优性收紧不等式，使用铰链损失惩罚违背该不等式的行为，且仅利用TD误差已有的网络输出计算惩罚，无需额外网络或前向传播。

Result: 在在线和离线到在线基准测试中，与多种最先进方法结合，LQL在相似运行时间下始终优于1步TD和n步TD学习。

Conclusion: LQL提供了一种稳定Q学习的有效机制，能显著减少长时域下的误差累积，且计算开销低。

中文摘要：离策略的、基于值的强化学习方法（如Q学习）因其可以从任意经验（包括由较旧策略或其他智能体收集的数据）中学习而具有吸引力。然而，在实践中，自举使得长时域学习变得脆弱：后期状态的估计误差通过时间差分（TD）更新向后传播，并可能随时间累积。我们提出了长时域Q学习（LQL），该方法在学习最优动作价值函数时引入了一种原则性的防止误差累积的机制。LQL建立在先前的“最优性收紧”观察之上：任何实际执行的动作序列都构成了最优策略在期望上所能达到的下界，因此，较早地采取最优行动不应比遵循观察到的动作若干步后再切换到最优行为更差。我们的贡献是将这一不等式转化为Q学习的实用稳定机制，通过使用铰链损失来惩罚对这些界限的违反。重要的是，LQL使用已经为TD误差产生的网络输出来计算这些惩罚，与Q学习相比，不需要辅助网络，也不需要额外的前向传播。当与多种最先进方法结合，在一系列在线和离线到在线基准测试中，LQL在相似运行时间下始终优于1步TD和n步TD学习。

Original abstract: Off-policy, value-based reinforcement learning methods such as Q-learning are appealing because they can learn from arbitrary experience, including data collected by older policies or other agents. In practice, however, bootstrapping makes long-horizon learning brittle: estimation errors at later states propagate backward through temporal-difference (TD) updates and can compound over time. We propose long-horizon Q-learning (LQL), which introduces a principled backstop against compounding error when learning the optimal action-value function. LQL builds on a prior optimality tightening observation: any realized action sequence lower-bounds what the optimal policy can achieve in expectation, so acting optimally earlier should not be worse than following the observed actions for several steps before switching to optimal behavior. Our contribution is to turn this inequality into a practical stabilization mechanism for Q-learning by using a hinge loss to penalize violations of these bounds. Importantly, LQL computes these penalties using network outputs already produced for the TD error, requiring no auxiliary networks and no additional forward passes relative to Q-learning. When combined with multiple state-of-the-art methods on a range of online and offline-to-online benchmarks, LQL consistently outperforms both 1-step TD and n-step TD learning at similar runtime.

</details>


### [40] [SANEmerg: An Emergent Communication Framework for Semantic-aware Agentic AI Networking](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05861v1)
*Yong Xiao,Haoran Zhou,Yujie Zhou,Marwan Krunz*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出多agent协作中通信协议涌现的框架，涉及语义通信与带宽自适应，可迁移至agent协作。

TL;DR: 提出了SANEmerg框架，通过带宽自适应重要性过滤和MDL复杂度正则化，实现多代理涌现通信，在带宽受限下提升任务准确率并降低开销。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统网络通信与计算解耦导致AgentNet低效，现有涌现通信未充分考虑计算限制和带宽约束。

Method: 提出SANEmerg，包含带宽自适应重要性过滤和基于MDL的复杂度正则化，促进计算受限信令涌现。

Result: 在AgentNet原型上实验，SANEmerg显著优于现有方案，任务准确率更高，带宽和计算开销更低。

Conclusion: SANEmerg有效解决带宽和计算约束下的多代理涌现通信问题。

中文摘要：未来网络系统被设想为将成为代理型人工智能原生生态系统的一部分，在该生态系统中，大量异构且专业化的AI代理无缝协作，实时满足复杂的用户需求。然而，传统网络范式的特点是通信与计算严格解耦，这通常导致大规模代理型AI网络（AgentNet）系统效率低下。涌现通信提供了一种新颖的解决方案，通过使自主代理支持任务特定的信令协议进行信息交换和协作协调。在本文中，我们考虑了一个多代理涌现通信框架，专为语义感知的AgentNet系统量身定制，该系统可以自动检测、推断用户的语义意图，并将其链接到一组子任务，分配给一组代理。我们研究了在严格带宽约束下，具有计算受限智能的协作代理之间如何涌现通信和信令协议。我们提出的框架称为SANEmerg，旨在促进协作任务完成过程中通信的涌现，同时遵守AgentNet的物理限制。SANEmerg包含一个带宽可适应的重要性过滤器，该过滤器动态优先传输贡献更高的消息维度，确保在带宽受限环境中的鲁棒性能。此外，SANEmerg集成了一个基于最小描述长度（MDL）原则的复杂度正则化器，以促进计算受限信令的涌现。通过AgentNet原型和大量实验评估，SANEmerg在任务准确性上取得了显著提升，同时大幅降低了带宽和计算开销，优于现有最先进的解决方案。

Original abstract: Future networking systems are envisioned to become part of an agentic AI-native ecosystem in which a vast number of heterogeneous and specialized AI agents cooperate seamlessly to fulfill complex user requirements in real time. However, traditional networking paradigms are characterized by a rigid decoupling of communication and computation, which often leads to significant inefficiencies in large-scale agentic AI networking (AgentNet) systems. Emergent communication offers a novel solution by enabling autonomous agents that support task-specific signaling protocols for information exchange and collaborative coordination. In this paper, we consider a multi-agent emergent communication framework, tailored for semantic-aware AgentNet systems in which the user's semantic intent can be automatically detected, inferred, and linked to a set of sub-tasks to be assigned to a set of agents. We investigate how communication and signaling protocols can emerge among collaborative agents with computationally bounded intelligence under stringent bandwidth constraints. Our proposed framework, called SANEmerg, is designed to facilitate the emergence of communication for collaborative task fulfillment while adhering to the physical limits of AgentNet. SANEmerg incorporates a bandwidth-adaptable importance-filter that dynamically prioritizes the transmission of higher-contribution message dimensions, ensuring robust performance in bandwidth-limited environments. Furthermore, SANEmerg integrates a complexity-regularizer grounded in the Minimum Description Length (MDL) principle to facilitate the emergence of computationally bounded signaling. Evaluated via an AgentNet prototype and extensive experimentation, SANEmerg demonstrates significant performance improvements over state-of-the-art solutions, achieving superior task accuracy while significantly reducing bandwidth and computational overhead.

Original abstract: The Internet of Value (IoV) is a heterogeneous, partially-trusted network in which the dominant marginal risk is composite (route, sentiment, liquidity, and the policy a system is willing to commit to) rather than a property of any single chain. We argue that a risk primitive adequate for this regime is a composition of five engines: a prediction engine over price, liquidity, volatility, and route health; a Bittensor verification subnet that decentralises and economically scores prediction outputs; a sentiment-fusion engine over text, on-chain flow, and grey-literature feeds; an agentic engine under constitutional, role-bound action constraints; and an API-risk and scenario engine that converts forecasts into pre-committed action programs in the sense of Monte-Carlo scenario generation. We anchor the architecture in two empirical artefacts: a 27-hour policy-constrained liquidity stress-response experiment on Solana, and a 168-hour prediction-router calibration arc reported with explicit class-imbalance honesty. The case study supports deployability; the validator-loss decomposition is stated formally and is falsifiable.

### [42] [Intentmaking and Sensemaking: Human Interaction with AI-Guided Mathematical Discovery](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05921v1)

TL;DR: 本研究通过11位数学家使用AlphaEvolve的用户研究，发现了一种名为'意图构建'的工作流程，即通过迭代交互定义实验目标，并建议AI工具应作为协作工具而非黑箱助手。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 进行了一项形成性用户研究，11位专家数学家使用AlphaEvolve进化编码代理解决高级问题，通过观察和访谈识别工作模式。

Result: 识别并描述了'意图构建'（intentmaking）这一迭代过程，用户通过与系统互动不断定义和更新实验目标，并与意义构建（sensemaking）循环交替。

Original abstract: Artificial intelligence offers powerful new tools for scientific discovery, but the interaction paradigms required to effectively harness these systems remain underexplored. In this paper, we present findings from a formative user study with 11 expert mathematicians who used AlphaEvolve, an evolutionary coding agent, to tackle advanced problems in their fields of expertise. We identify and characterize a distinct workflow we term intentmaking, the iterative process of discovering, defining, and refining one's experimental goals through active system interaction. We frame this as a natural extension to sensemaking, the cognitive process of building an understanding of complex or novel data. We suggest that users enter a cycle of intentmaking (defining and updating their experiment) and sensemaking (interpreting the results) which repeats many times during the course of an investigation. Our documentation of these themes suggests an approach to designing AI tools for scientific discovery that goes beyond the existing question/answer model of many current systems, treating them as collaborative instruments rather than opaque black-box assistants.

### [43] [MAS-Algorithm: A Workflow for Solving Algorithmic Programming Problems with a Multi-Agent System](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05949v2)
*Yuliang Xu,Xiang Xu,Yao Wan,Hu Wei,Tong Jia*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出MAS-Algorithm，一种受竞争性程序员启发的多智能体工作流，在算法推理任务上实现显著性能提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法成本高、可解释性有限或碎片化，缺乏统一框架，亟需一种系统性的多智能体方法。

Method: MAS-Algorithm将端到端求解分解为模块化阶段，支持结构化推理、工具集成和智能体协调。

Result: 在自建基准上接受率平均提升6.48%，LiveCodeBench-Pro上提升4.72%，单个智能体贡献高达27.7%。

Conclusion: MAS-Algorithm在推进AI驱动的算法推理方面具有巨大潜力，且优于参数高效微调等方法。

中文摘要：算法问题求解是评估AI编程系统中结构化推理的严格测试床，因为它直接反映了模型在复杂场景下执行结构化推理的能力。现有方法主要依赖于以模型为中心的策略，例如架构修改和数据扩展，这些策略成本高昂且可解释性有限。利用外部工具或提示技术（如思维链）的替代方法往往是零散的，缺乏统一的框架。在本文中，我们提出了MAS-Algorithm，这是一种受竞争性程序员和算法工程师实践启发的系统性多智能体工作流，用于算法问题求解。我们的框架将端到端的求解过程分解为模块化阶段，实现了结构化推理、工具集成和智能体之间的灵活协调。该设计强调严谨性和可扩展性，使其能够泛化到各种问题类型。在自建基准上的实验结果表明，在多个Qwen系列模型上均取得了一致的改进，接受率平均提高了6.48%。相比之下，在相同数据上进行参数高效微调仅获得0.89%的微小改进。我们进一步在LiveCodeBench-Pro上观察到了4.72%的提升，同时在额外的准确性和效率指标上也取得了一致的改进。除了性能提升，我们还进行了全面分析，以更好地理解工作流中的推理过程，包括错误模式和跨场景行为。我们还进行了定制替换和消融研究，以探索框架的上限，表明单个智能体可以贡献高达27.7%的改进。这些结果凸显了MAS-Algorithm在推进AI驱动的算法推理方面的巨大潜力。

Original abstract: Algorithmic problem solving serves as a rigorous testbed for evaluating structured reasoning in AI coding systems, as it directly reflects a model's ability to perform structured reasoning in complex scenarios. Existing approaches predominantly rely on model-centric strategies, such as architectural modifications and data scaling, which are costly and offer limited interpretability. Alternative methods leveraging external tools or prompting techniques (e.g., chain-of-thought) are often fragmented and lack a unified framework. In this paper, we propose MAS-Algorithm, a systematic multi-agent workflow for algorithmic problem solving inspired by the practices of competitive programmers and algorithm engineers. Our framework decomposes the end-to-end solving process into modular stages, enabling structured reasoning, tool integration, and flexible coordination among agents. The design emphasizes both rigor and extensibility, allowing it to generalize across diverse problem types. Experimental results on a self-constructed benchmark demonstrate consistent improvements across multiple Qwen series models, achieving an average gain of 6.48% in acceptance rate. In contrast, parameter-efficient fine-tuning on the same data yields only a marginal improvement of 0.89%. We further observe a 4.72% gain on LiveCodeBench-Pro, along with consistent improvements across additional accuracy and efficiency metrics. Beyond performance gains, we conduct comprehensive analyses to better understand the reasoning process within the workflow, including error patterns and cross-scenario behaviors. We further perform customized replacement and ablation studies to explore the upper bound of the framework, showing that individual agents can contribute improvements of up to 27.7%. These results highlight the strong potential of MAS-Algorithm for advancing AI-driven algorithmic reasoning.

### [44] [HaM-World: Soft-Hamiltonian World Models with Selective Memory for Planning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05951v1)
*Haoyun Tang,Haodong Cui,Keyao Xu,Kun Wang,Zhandong Mei*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出基于哈密顿动力学和选择性记忆的世界模型，用于agent规划，可迁移到coding agent的长期规划。

TL;DR: 提出HaM-World，通过引入历史条件记忆和哈密顿几何结构，解决了世界模型长时域推演不稳定的问题，在多项任务上显著提升规划性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有世界模型在长时域规划和分布外推演时不稳定，原因在于潜在表示缺乏历史条件记忆和几何组织。

Method: 将潜在状态分解为规范子空间(q,p)和上下文子空间c，使用Mamba记忆作为历史条件输入，并采用能量导出的哈密顿向量场加上可学习残差/控制动力学。

Result: 在DeepMind Control Suite上平均AUC提升9.5%，长时域推演误差降至45%，OOD条件下回报增益10.2%-13.6%。

Conclusion: HaM-World通过结构化潜在状态和哈密顿动力学有效提升了世界模型的长期规划稳定性和泛化能力。

中文摘要：世界模型通过学习到的潜在动力学实现基于模型的规划，但随着规划范围的增长或动力学分布的变化，想象推演变得不稳定。我们认为，这种不稳定性反映了面向规划器的潜在表示中缺失两种结构：用于近似马尔可夫完备性的历史条件记忆，以及分离配置、动量和任务语义的几何组织。我们提出 HaM-World (HMW)，一种结构化世界模型，将潜在状态分解为规范 (q, p) 子空间和上下文子空间 c，同时使用 Mamba 选择性状态空间记忆作为同一潜在动力学的历史条件输入。在此接口内，(q, p) 通过能量导出的哈密顿向量场加上可学习的残差/控制动力学演化，而 c 捕获语义、耗散和非保守因素。这为规划器提供了一个单一的潜在状态，用于动力学预测、奖励/价值估计、想象推演和 CEM 动作搜索。在四个 DeepMind Control Suite 任务上，HaM-World 达到了最高的平均 AUC（117.9，+9.5%），将长时域推演误差降低到强基线模型的 45%，并在 {3,5,7} MSE 单元中赢得 11/12 的胜率。在 12 种涵盖动力学变化、动作延迟和观测遮挡的 OOD 扰动下，HaM-World 在每种条件下都获得了最高的回报，在 Finger Spin 和 Reacher Easy 上平均 OOD 回报增益分别为 10.2% 和 13.6%。机制诊断进一步显示，无动作哈密顿能量漂移有界，策略推演下能量变化有结构，以及控制引起的能量转移具有一致性，支持了所设计的软哈密顿动力学。

Original abstract: World models enable model-based planning through learned latent dynamics, but imagined rollouts become unstable as the planning horizon grows or the dynamics distribution shifts. We argue that this instability reflects two missing structures in planner-facing latents: history-conditioned memory for approximate Markov completeness, and geometric organization that separates configuration, momentum, and task semantics. We propose HaM-World (HMW), a structured world model that decomposes the latent state into a canonical (q, p) subspace and a context subspace c, while using Mamba selective state-space memory as the history-conditioned input to the same latent dynamics. Within this interface, (q, p) evolves through an energy-derived Hamiltonian vector field plus learnable residual/control dynamics, while c captures semantic, dissipative, and non-conservative factors. This gives the planner a single latent state shared by dynamics prediction, reward/value estimation, imagined rollouts, and CEM action search. On four DeepMind Control Suite tasks, HaM-World reaches the highest Avg. AUC (117.9, +9.5%), reduces long-horizon rollout error to 45% of a strong baseline model, and wins 11/12 k in {3,5,7} MSE cells. Under 12 OOD perturbations spanning dynamics shifts, action delay, and observation masking, HaM-World achieves the highest return in every condition, with average OOD-return gains of 10.2% on Finger Spin and 13.6% on Reacher Easy. Mechanism diagnostics further show bounded action-free Hamiltonian-energy drift, structured energy variation under policy rollouts, and coherent control-induced energy transfer, supporting the intended Soft-Hamiltonian dynamics design.

### [45] [TheraAgent: Self-Improving Therapeutic Agent for Precise and Comprehensive Treatment Planning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05963v1)
*Junkai Li,Yunghwei Lai,Tianyi Zhu,Zheng Long Lee,Weizhi Ma,Yang Liu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出治疗计划agent，采用generate-judge-refine迭代框架，属于通用agent方法，可迁移到代码优化agent的自我改进。

TL;DR: 提出TheraAgent框架，通过迭代生成-判断-优化流程，将大型语言模型的一次性治疗计划生成改进为逐步优化，并在HealthBench和专家评估中取得最佳结果，安全性显著提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLMs依赖一次性输出且缺乏验证，导致治疗计划粗糙、不完整且存在安全风险。

Method: 提出TheraAgent智能体框架，包含迭代的生成-判断-优化流程，并引入治疗专用评估模块TheraJudge强制执行临床标准。

Result: 在HealthBench上取得SOTA结果（Accuracy和Completeness领先），专家评估中86%胜率超过医生，靶向性和危害控制优秀；TheraJudge与HealthBench评估高度一致。

Conclusion: 迭代优化框架能有效生成更精确、全面、安全的治疗方案，且内置评估模块可靠。

中文摘要：制定治疗计划本质上是一项复杂的推理和优化任务，而非简单的生成问题。然而，现有的大型语言模型主要依赖一次性输出且缺乏明确验证，可能导致治疗计划粗糙、不完整且存在潜在安全风险。为解决这些局限，我们提出TheraAgent，一个智能体框架，用迭代的生成-判断-优化流程取代一次性生成。通过模仿人类专家迭代修订治疗计划的真实推理过程，我们的框架逐步将粗糙、不完整的草稿转化为精确、全面且更安全的治疗方案。为促进关键判断组件，我们引入TheraJudge，一个集成到推理循环中的治疗专用评估模块，以强制执行临床标准。实验表明，TheraAgent在HealthBench上取得了最先进的结果，在准确性和完整性上领先。在专家评估中，它针对医生取得了86%的胜率，在靶向性和危害控制方面表现优异。此外，TheraJudge与HealthBench评估的高度一致性证实了我们框架的可靠性。

Original abstract: Formulating a treatment plan is inherently a complex reasoning and refinement task rather than a simple generation problem. However, existing large language models (LLMs) mainly rely on one-shot output without explicit verification, which may result in rough, incomplete, and potentially unsafe treatment plans. To address these limitations, we propose TheraAgent, an agentic framework that replaces one-shot generation with an iterative generate-judge-refine pipeline. By mirroring the actual reasoning process of human experts who iteratively revise treatment plans, our framework progressively transforms coarse and incomplete drafts into precise, comprehensive, and safer therapeutic regimens. To facilitate the critical judge component, we introduce TheraJudge, a treatment-specific evaluation module integrated into the inference loop to enforce clinical standards. Experiments show TheraAgent achieves state-of-the-art results on HealthBench, leading in Accuracy and Completeness. In expert evaluations, it attains an 86% win rate against physicians, with superior Targeting and Harm Control. Moreover, the highly agreement between TheraJudge and HealthBench evaluations confirms the reliability of our framework.

### [46] [TACT: Mitigating Overthinking and Overacting in Coding Agents via Activation Steering](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05980v1)
*Yuan Sui,Yulin Chen,Yibo Li,Xue Jiang,Yufei He,Yihong Dong,Xiaoxin He,Tianyu Gao,Bryan Hooi*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 针对coding agent的过度思考与过度行动问题，提出激活引导方法，直接相关于agent长程任务可靠性。

TL;DR: 提出TACT方法，通过激活引导来校准智能体的思考与行动，在长轨迹中检测并缓解overthinking和overacting漂移，提升解决率并减少步骤。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 语言模型智能体在处理复杂软件工程任务时，长轨迹中常出现overthinking和overacting两种漂移，导致性能退化。

Method: 标记轨迹步骤为overthinking、overacting或calibrated，发现隐藏状态可沿两个漂移轴线性分离（AUC≈0.9）；测试时，将步骤激活投影到轴上，并将漂移的激活拉回校准区域。

Result: 在SWE-bench Verified、Terminal-Bench 2.0和CLAW-Eval上，TACT相比未引导基线，解决率分别提升+5.8pp（Qwen3.5-27B）和+4.8pp（Gemma-4-26B-A4B-it），解决步骤减少高达26%。

Conclusion: agent drift是残差流中的可引导方向，TACT为构建可靠长程智能体提供了有效手段。

中文摘要：当语言模型智能体处理复杂的软件工程任务时，它们经常在长轨迹中退化，我们将其定义为*智能体漂移*。我们关注两种反复出现的失败模式：*过度思考*和*过度行动*，即智能体反复推理它已有的信息，以及智能体发出工具调用但没有整合最近的观察或获取新证据。在本文中，我们引入了TACT（通过激活引导的思考-行动校准），以在残差流中检测并缓解智能体漂移，在其表现为行为失败之前。具体来说，我们将轨迹步骤标记为过度思考、过度行动或校准，并发现它们的隐藏状态可以沿两条*漂移轴*线性分离，从校准行为指向每种失败模式（AUC≈0.9）。为了缓解智能体漂移，我们在测试时将每个步骤的激活投射到这些轴上，并将漂移的激活拉回校准区域。实验表明，TACT在SWE-bench Verified、Terminal-Bench 2.0和CLAW-Eval上均优于未引导的基线，在Qwen3.5-27B上平均解决率提升+5.8个百分点，在Gemma-4-26B-A4B-it上提升+4.8个百分点，同时将解决步骤减少高达26%。这些增益将智能体漂移视为残差流中的一个可引导方向，并将TACT定位为可靠长程智能体的一个可行手段。

Original abstract: When language model agents tackle complex software engineering tasks, they often degrade over long trajectories, which we define as *agent drift*. We focus on two recurring failure modes *overthinking* and *overacting*, i.e., where the agent repeatedly reasons over information it already has, and where it issues tool calls without integrating recent observations or acquiring new evidence. In this paper, we introduce TACT (Think-Act Calibration via activation Steering), to detect and mitigate agent drift in the residual stream before it surfaces as a behavioral failure. In specific, we label trajectory steps as overthinking, overacting, or calibrated, and find that their hidden states can separate linearly along two *drift axes*, pointing from calibrated behavior toward each failure mode (AUC $\approx$ 0.9). To mitigate agent drift, we project each step's activation onto these axes at test time and pull drifted ones back toward the calibrated region. Experiments show that TACT outperforms unsteered baselines across SWE-bench Verified, Terminal-Bench 2.0, and CLAW-Eval, lifting average resolve rate by $+5.8$ pp on Qwen3.5-27B and $+4.8$ pp on Gemma-4-26B-A4B-it while cutting steps-to-resolve by up to $26\%$. These gains frame agent drift as a steerable direction in the residual stream, and position TACT as a viable handle for reliable long-horizon agents.

</details>

*Remigiusz Kinas,Joanna Krawczyk,Rafał Powalski,Przemysław Pietrzak,Agnieszka Kowalewska,Krzysztof Kolmus,Maciej Sypetkowski,Łukasz Smoliński,Tomasz Jetka*

Conclusion: 该系统在单元级、开放性和端到端临床评估中展现出广泛且具有竞争力的性能，适合转化医学证据综合。

中文摘要：转化医学将未明确的发展目标转化为证据综合，必须结合文献、试验、专利和定量多组学分析，同时保留标识符、不确定性和可检索的出处。通用基础模型和现成的工具增强或多智能体系统并非为此而构建：它们倾向于产生一次性答案或无限期运行，并且在异构生物医学来源所需的可审计、情景特定工作流程方面存在不足。本文介绍了Ingenix BioResearcher，一个情景引导的多智能体系统，它将查询映射到版本化的研究手册，委托给30多个工具和机器学习端点的专门子智能体，将结构化数据库访问与沙盒代码相结合用于基因组规模分析，并在编辑汇编之前应用声明级多模型调和。我们在单元级能力、开放性生物医学推理和端到端临床发现上评估了BioResearcher。它在109个单步测试中领先基线（通过率83.49%，平均分0.892），在生物医学基准测试中表现强劲（BixBench-Verified-50上89.33%，BaisBench Scientific Discovery上前0.758平均分），并在30个查询的临床端到端基准测试中领先，具有最高的阳性命中率（74.7%±3.3%）和阴性清除率（96.8%±0.2%）。这些结果表明在单元级、开放性和端到端临床评估中具有广泛、有竞争力的性能。

Original abstract: Translational medicine turns underspecified development goals into evidence synthesis that must combine literature, trials, patents, and quantitative multi-omics analysis while preserving identifiers, uncertainty, and retrievable provenance. General-purpose foundation models and off-the-shelf tool-augmented or multi-agent systems are not built for this: they tend to produce single-shot answers or run open-endedly, and fall short on the auditable, scenario-specific workflows that heterogeneous biomedical sources demand.
  This paper introduces Ingenix BioResearcher, a scenario-guided multi-agent system that maps queries to versioned research playbooks, delegates to specialized subagents over 30+ tools and machine-learning endpoints, mixes structured database access with sandboxed code for genome-scale analyses, and applies claim-level multi-model reconciliation before editorial assembly.
  We evaluate BioResearcher across unit-level capabilities, open-ended biomedical reasoning, and end-to-end clinical discovery. It leads evaluated baselines on 109 single-step tests (83.49% pass rate; 0.892 average score), achieves strong biomedical benchmark performance (89.33% on BixBench-Verified-50 and the top 0.758 mean score on BaisBench Scientific Discovery), and leads on a 30-query clinical end-to-end benchmark with the highest positive hit rate (74.7% $\pm$ 3.3%) and negative clear rate (96.8% $\pm$ 0.2%). ### [48] [Strat-LLM: Stratified Strategy Alignment for LLM-based Stock Trading with Real-time Multi-Source Signals](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06024v1)
*Wenliang Huang,Zengyi Yu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出LLM交易agent的策略对齐框架，可迁移到agent行为一致性控制。

TL;DR: 提出Strat-LLM框架，通过分层策略对齐和实时前向设置揭示不同规模和模式下LLM在交易中的表现差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准忽视架构推理与策略一致性相互作用，缺乏对LLM交易代理的全面评估。

Method: 基于分层策略对齐的Strat-LLM框架，在2025年实时前向设置中整合价格、新闻和年报数据，消除前瞻偏差，并在A股和美国市场进行压力测试。

Result: 四个发现：推理模型在自由模式最优，标准模型需严格模式；对齐效用依赖市场体制；中等规模模型(35B)在严格约束下保真度好，超大规模模型(122B)在引导模式有溢价；标准LLM陷入高胜率陷阱。

Conclusion: 深层次推理或严格外部护栏是缓解标准LLM高胜率陷阱的关键。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）正在演变为自主交易代理，但现有的基准测试往往忽视了架构推理与策略一致性之间的相互作用。我们提出了Strat-LLM，一个基于分层策略对齐（Stratified Strategy Alignment）的框架。在2025年全年的实时向前设置中运行，它整合了包括顺序价格、实时新闻和年度报告在内的异构数据，以消除前瞻偏差。在A股和美国市场上进行的大量压力测试显示：（1）推理密集型模型在自由模式下通过内部逻辑达到峰值效用，而标准模型则需要严格模式作为关键风险锚；（2）对齐效用具有体制依赖性，自由模式和引导模式在上升趋势市场中捕捉动量，而严格模式在下降趋势中减少回撤；（3）中等规模模型（35B）在严格约束下表现出最佳保真度，而超大规模模型（122B）在刚性规则下受到对齐税的影响，但在引导模式下获得性能溢价；（4）标准LLM常常陷入高胜率陷阱，优化小收益而牺牲总回报，只有通过深度推理或严格的外部护栏才能缓解。项目详情请访问https://Strat-LLM.github.io。

Original abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) are evolving into autonomous trading agents, yet existing benchmarks often overlook the interplay between architectural reasoning and strategy consistency. We propose Strat-LLM, a framework grounded in Stratified Strategy Alignment. Operating in a live-forward setting throughout 2025, it integrates heterogeneous data including sequential prices, real-time news, and annual reports to eliminate look-ahead bias. Extensive stress tests on A-share and U.S. markets reveal: (1) reasoning-heavy models achieve peak utility in Free Mode via internal logic, whereas standard models require Strict Mode as a vital risk anchor; (2) alignment utility is regime-dependent, with Free and Guided modes capturing momentum in uptrending markets, while Strict Mode mitigates drawdowns in downtrends; (3) mid-scale models (35B) show optimal fidelity under strict constraints, whereas ultra-large models (122B) suffer an alignment tax under rigid rules but gain a performance premium in Guided Mode; (4) standard LLMs often fall into a high win-rate trap, optimizing for small gains at the expense of total returns, which can only be mitigated through deep reasoning or strict external guardrails. Project details are available at https://Strat-LLM.github.io.

### [49] [Novelty-based Tree-of-Thought Search for LLM Reasoning and Planning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06040v1)
*Leon Hamm,Zlatan Ajanovic*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 基于新颖性的思维树搜索改进LLM推理规划，属于agent规划方法创新。

TL;DR: 提出一种基于新颖性度量的剪枝方法，通过评估节点独特性减少树状思维搜索规模，从而降低LLM推理的令牌成本并在多个基准上验证有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM推理方法（如链式思维、树状思维、强化学习）虽然提升了性能，但仍脆弱且成本高昂，受宽度搜索中新颖性思想的启发，旨在将新颖性概念引入语言领域以改进树状思维推理的效率。

Method: 定义可测量的新颖性概念，通过提示LLM并利用预训练知识估计新节点相对于已访问节点的独特性，据此进行分支剪枝以缩小搜索树规模。

Result: 在多个基于语言的规划和一般推理基准测试中，该方法尽管增加了每状态的提示次数，但通过剪枝显著降低了总体令牌成本，并保持了性能。

Conclusion: 新颖性剪枝是一种有效的树状思维优化策略，能在减少计算开销的同时保持推理质量，为未来LLM推理的轻量化提供了新思路。

中文摘要：尽管链式思维、树状思维或强化学习等进步提高了LLM在推理和规划任务中的表现，但它们仍然脆弱，在许多领域尚未达到人类水平，并且常常面临高时间和令牌成本的问题。受宽度优先搜索在规划中成功的启发，我们探索了如何将新颖性概念转移到语言领域，以及如何改进树状思维推理。树状思维依赖于构建连续想法或思维的潜在“路径”。这些路径通过反复提示LLM生成。在本文中，我们提出了一种可测量的新颖性概念，用于描述新节点（思维）与搜索树中先前看到的节点相比的独特性。新颖性通过提示LLM并利用预训练中的嵌入通用知识来估计。然后，该指标可用于剪枝分支并缩小搜索范围。尽管这种方法在每个状态引入了更多提示，但通过剪枝和缩小整体树大小，可以降低总令牌成本。该过程在基于语言的规划和一般推理的多个基准测试中进行了测试和比较。

Original abstract: Although advances such as chain-of-thought, tree-of-thought or reinforcement learning have improved the performance of LLMs in reasoning and planning tasks, they are still brittle and have not achieved human-level performance in many domains, and often suffer from high time and token costs. Inspired by the success of width-based search in planning, we explore how the concept of novelty can be transferred to language domains and how it can improve tree-of-thought reasoning. A tree of thoughts relies on building possible "paths" of consecutive ideas or thoughts. These are generated by repeatedly prompting an LLM. In our paper, a measurable concept of novelty is proposed that describes the uniqueness of a new node (thought) in comparison to nodes previously seen in the search tree. Novelty is estimated by prompting an LLM and making use of embedded general knowledge from pre-training. This metric can then be used to prune branches and reduce the scope of the search. Although this method introduces more prompts per state, the overall token cost can be reduced by pruning and reducing the overall tree size. This procedure is tested and compared using several benchmarks in language-based planning and general reasoning.

</details>


### [50] [VibeServe: Can AI Agents Build Bespoke LLM Serving Systems?](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06068v1)
*Keisuke Kamahori,Shihang Li,Simon Peter,Baris Kasikci*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 多agent循环自动合成LLM服务系统，直接相关coding agent与自动代码生成。

TL;DR: VibeServe通过多智能体循环自动生成针对特定场景优化的LLM服务系统，在标准场景中与vLLM性能相当，在非标准场景中超越现有系统。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统LLM服务系统采用单一通用堆栈，需要大量手动调优且难以适应多样化场景，因此需要自动合成专用服务系统。

Method: 提出VibeServe，使用外循环搜索系统设计空间，内循环实现候选方案、验证正确性并测量性能，端到端生成定制化服务堆栈。

Result: 在标准部署中与高度优化的vLLM竞争力持平；在六种非标准场景（如非标准模型架构、工作负载知识、硬件特定优化）中，VibeServe显著优于现有通用系统。

Conclusion: 生成时特化而非运行时通用是基础设施软件设计的新方向，可兼顾性能与场景适应性。

中文摘要：多年来，我们构建LLM服务系统就像构建任何其他关键基础设施一样：一个单一的通用堆栈，经过多年工程师的手动调优，旨在支持每个模型和工作负载。在本文中，我们采取了相反的赌注：一个多智能体循环，自动为不同的使用场景综合定制服务系统。我们提出了VibeServe，这是第一个端到端生成完整LLM服务堆栈的智能体循环。VibeServe使用外循环来规划和跟踪系统设计的搜索，使用内循环来实现候选方案、检查正确性并在目标基准上测量性能。在标准部署环境中，现有堆栈已经高度优化，VibeServe与vLLM保持竞争力，表明生成时特化不需要以牺牲性能为代价。更有趣的是，在非标准场景中，VibeServe通过利用通用系统错失的机会，在涉及非标准模型架构、工作负载知识和硬件特定优化的六种场景中超越了现有系统。总之，这些结果表明了基础设施软件设计空间中的一个不同点：生成时特化而非运行时通用。代码可在https://github.com/uw-syfi/vibe-serve获取。

Original abstract: For years, we have built LLM serving systems like any other critical infrastructure: a single general-purpose stack, hand-tuned over many engineer-years, meant to support every model and workload. In this paper, we take the opposite bet: a multi-agent loop that automatically synthesizes bespoke serving systems for different usage scenarios. We propose VibeServe, the first agentic loop that generates entire LLM serving stacks end-to-end. VibeServe uses an outer loop to plan and track the search over system designs, and an inner loop to implement candidates, check correctness, and measure performance on the target benchmark. In the standard deployment setting, where existing stacks are highly optimized, VibeServe remains competitive with vLLM, showing that generation-time specialization need not come at the cost of performance. More interestingly, in non-standard scenarios, VibeServe outperforms existing systems by exploiting opportunities that generic systems miss in six scenarios involving non-standard model architectures, workload knowledge, and hardware-specific optimizations. Together, these results suggest a different point in the design space for infrastructure software: generation-time specialization rather than runtime generality. Code is available at https://github.com/uw-syfi/vibe-serve.

</details>


### [51] [On Time, Within Budget: Constraint-Driven Online Resource Allocation for Agentic Workflows](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06110v2)
*Xinglin Wang,Zishen Liu,Shaoxiong Feng,Peiwen Yuan,Yiwei Li,Jiayi Shi,Yueqi Zhang,Chuyi Tan,Ji Zhang,Boyuan Pan,Yao Hu,Kan Li*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 约束驱动在线资源分配用于agent工作流，提出MCPP规划器。

TL;DR: 提出MCPP，一种轻量级闭环规划器，通过模拟执行和重新规划来最大化在预算和截止日期约束下智能体工作流成功完成的概率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实际部署中工作流必须在指定预算和截止日期内完成，现有方法只优化平均效率，无法满足此类硬约束需求。

Method: 将资源分配问题建模为有限时域随机在线分配问题，提出MCPP，利用模拟工作流执行估计约束完成概率，并基于实时观测进行闭环重新规划。

Result: 在CodeFlow和ProofFlow基准上，MCPP在多种预算-截止日期组合下持续优于基线方法，提升约束完成概率。

Conclusion: MCPP能有效应对预算和截止日期约束，提高智能体工作流成功完成的可靠性。

中文摘要：智能体系统越来越多地通过执行编排的工作流来解决复杂的用户请求，其中子任务被分配给专门的模型或工具，并根据它们的依赖关系进行协调。虽然最近的工作通过优化性能-成本-延迟前沿来提高智能体效率，但实际部署通常有具体的要求：工作流必须在指定的预算内并在指定的截止日期前完成。这使目标从平均效率优化转向在明确的预算和截止日期约束下最大化整个工作流成功完成的概率。我们研究面向智能体工作流的约束驱动在线资源分配。给定一个具有依赖结构的工作流以及每个子任务-模型对的成功率和生成长度的估计，执行器动态地在可同时执行的子任务之间分配模型和并行样本，同时管理剩余的预算和时间。我们将此设置形式化为一个有限时域随机在线分配问题，并提出蒙特卡洛组合规划（MCPP），一个轻量级的闭环规划器，通过模拟工作流执行直接估计受约束的完成概率，并在观察到结果后重新规划。在CodeFlow和ProofFlow上的实验表明，MCPP在广泛的预算-截止日期约束下，始终提高了受约束的完成概率，优于强基线。

Original abstract: Agentic systems increasingly solve complex user requests by executing orchestrated workflows, where subtasks are assigned to specialized models or tools and coordinated according to their dependencies. While recent work improves agent efficiency by optimizing the performance--cost--latency frontier, real deployments often impose concrete requirements: a workflow must be completed within a specified budget and before a specified deadline. This shifts the goal from average efficiency optimization to maximizing the probability that the entire workflow completes successfully under explicit budget and deadline constraints. We study \emph{constraint-driven online resource allocation for agentic workflows}. Given a dependency-structured workflow and estimates of success rates and generation lengths for each subtask--model pair, the executor dynamically allocates models and parallel samples across simultaneously executable subtasks while managing the remaining budget and time. We formulate this setting as a finite-horizon stochastic online allocation problem and propose \emph{Monte Carlo Portfolio Planning} (MCPP), a lightweight closed-loop planner that directly estimates constrained completion probability through simulated workflow executions and replans after observed outcomes. Experiments on CodeFlow and ProofFlow demonstrate that MCPP consistently improves constrained completion probability over strong baselines across a wide range of budget--deadline constraints.

### [52] [Policy-Guided Stepwise Model Routing for Cost-Effective Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06116v1)
*Wenwen Si,Insup Lee,Osbert Bastani*

Selection reason: 通过RL训练策略进行逐步模型路由，方法可迁移到agent决策。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有步进模型路由方法依赖手工设计的策略或训练大型过程奖励模型，前者性能受限，后者计算成本高且可能不可行。

Method: 将步进模型路由形式化为约束决策问题，使用强化学习训练一个小型控制策略，并结合阈值校准来调节性能-效率权衡。

Result: 在三个数学基准上，方法比手工策略有更好的精度-成本权衡，且与需要训练大型过程奖励模型的方法性能相当。

中文摘要：推理时计算极大地增强了大型语言模型（LLMs）在具有挑战性的推理任务上的性能，但这种策略可能会产生高昂的推理成本。一种解决方案是将中间思维链（CoT）状态路由到不同规模的语言模型；然而，现有方法依赖于手工设计的路由策略从而限制了性能，或者依赖于训练大型过程奖励模型，这在许多应用中可能不可行。我们将步进模型路由形式化为一个约束决策问题，通过使用强化学习训练一个小型控制策略并结合阈值校准来调节性能-效率权衡来解决该问题。我们在三个数学基准测试（GSM8K、MATH500和OmniMath）上使用开放和封闭模型验证了我们的方法。与手工设计的方法相比，我们的方法始终改善了精度-成本权衡，同时实现了与需要训练大型过程奖励模型的方法相当的权衡。

Original abstract: Inference-time computation has greatly enhanced the performance of large language models (LLMs) on challenging reasoning tasks, but this strategy can incur high inference costs. One solution is to route intermediate chain-of-thought (CoT) states to language models of different sizes; however, existing approaches rely on handcrafted routing strategies that limit performance, or on training large process reward models that may be infeasible in many applications. We formulate stepwise model routing as a constrained decision-making problem, which we solve by training a small control policy using reinforcement learning in conjunction with threshold calibration to tune the performance-efficiency tradeoff. We validate our method on three math benchmarks (GSM8K, MATH500, and OmniMath) on both open and closed models. Our method consistently improves the accuracy-cost tradeoff compared to handcrafted approaches, while achieving a comparable tradeoff to methods that require training large process reward models.

### [53] [Back to the Beginning of Heuristic Design: Bridging Code and Knowledge with LLMs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06123v1)
*Nguyen Viet Tuan Kiet,Bui Dinh Pham,Dao Van Tung,Tran Cong Dao,Huynh Thi Thanh Binh*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 知识优先的LLM自动启发式设计，可迁移到自动代码优化与agent。

TL;DR: 提出从代码中心向知识优先的范式转变，通过统计学习视角形式化失真-压缩权衡，并证明知识优先搜索在组合优化中能提高发现效率、迁移和泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自动启发式设计方法主要采用自底向上的代码中心范式，从底层实现迭代提炼高层原则，但缺乏对可重用知识的明确追求。本文旨在补全这一视角，引入知识优先的自顶向下范式，使所学知识显式化并跨问题可复用。

Method: 通过统计学习视角形式化知识搜索中的失真-压缩权衡，并在基于种群和基于树的AHD框架中实例化知识优先搜索；将知识作为主要搜索对象，代码作为实例化工具，结合两种范式进行对比实验。

Result: 知识优先搜索在组合优化及其他任务中优于代码中心管道，提高了发现效率、迁移性和泛化能力；将两者结合能进一步提升性能。

Conclusion: 自动启发式设计的进展依赖于迭代构建和演化具有长期价值的可解释假设，知识优先范式是实现这一目标的关键方向。

中文摘要：大语言模型最近推动了组合优化（CO）中自动启发式设计（AHD）的进展，其中候选启发式通过迭代提议、评估和优化得以改进。现有方法大多搜索可执行程序，并从执行反馈中提炼见解以引导后续迭代。由于这一过程从底层实现转向高层原则，我们称之为自底向上范式。我们认为这种观点是不完整的，并引入了一种互补的自顶向下视角：知识成为主要搜索对象，而代码仅用于实例化和测试它，从而使所学内容明确且在问题和轨迹间可复用。我们通过统计学习视角形式化了这一转变，该视角揭示了失真-压缩权衡，并在基于种群和基于树的AHD框架中实例化了它。在组合优化及其他任务中，知识优先的搜索提高了发现效率、迁移性和泛化能力，通常优于以代码为中心的管道，而结合两种策略则能带来进一步的增益。我们的结果表明，AHD的进展依赖于迭代构建和演化可解释的假设，这些假设在单次搜索轨迹之外仍保留价值。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have recently advanced automatic heuristic design (AHD) for combinatorial optimization (CO), where candidate heuristics are iteratively proposed, evaluated, and refined. Most existing approaches search over executable programs and distill insights from execution feedback to guide later iterations. Because this process moves from low-level implementations to high-level principles, we refer to it as a bottom-up paradigm. We argue that this view is incomplete and introduce a complementary top-down perspective: knowledge becomes the primary search object and code merely instantiates and tests it, making what is learned explicit and reusable across problems and trajectories. We formalize this shift through a statistical-learning view that exposes a distortion--compression trade-off, and instantiate it in both population-based and tree-based AHD frameworks. Across CO and tasks beyond it, knowledge-first search improves discovery efficiency, transfer, and generalization, often outperforming code-centric pipelines, while combining both strategies yields further gains. Our results suggest that progress in AHD depends on iteratively constructing and evolving interpretable hypotheses that retain value beyond a single search trajectory.

### [54] [Skill1: Unified Evolution of Skill-Augmented Agents via Reinforcement Learning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06130v3)
*Yaorui Shi,Yuxin Chen,Zhengxi Lu,Yuchun Miao,Shugui Liu,Qi GU,Xunliang Cai,Xiang Wang,An Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 统一演化技能增强agent，优化技能选择、利用和蒸馏。

TL;DR: 提出Skill1框架，通过单一任务结果信号共同进化技能选择、利用和提炼，在ALFWorld和WebShop上超越基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法孤立优化或使用不同奖励源导致部分冲突进化。

Method: 训练单一策略，生成查询搜索库、重排候选、基于选定技能解决问题、从轨迹提炼新技能，所有学习来自单一任务结果信号。

Result: 在ALFWorld和WebShop上超越基线，训练动态显示共同进化，消融证明信号重要性。

Conclusion: Skill1有效实现三种能力的共同进化。

中文摘要：一个持久的技能库允许语言模型代理在任务间复用成功的策略。维护这样一个库需要三个耦合的能力：代理选择相关技能，在执行中利用它，并从经验中提炼新技能。现有方法孤立地优化这些能力，或者使用不同的奖励来源，导致部分且冲突的进化。我们提出Skill1，一个框架，训练单一策略以共同进化技能选择、利用和提炼，朝向共享的任务结果目标。该策略生成一个查询来搜索技能库，对候选进行重新排序以选择一个，在给定该技能的条件下解决任务，并从轨迹中提炼一个新技能。所有学习都来自单一的任务结果信号。其低频趋势归因于选择，高频变化归因于提炼。在ALFWorld和WebShop上的实验表明，Skill1优于先前的基于技能和强化学习的基线。训练动态证实了三种能力的共同进化，消融实验表明，去除任何归因信号都会降低进化。

Original abstract: A persistent skill library allows language model agents to reuse successful strategies across tasks. Maintaining such a library requires three coupled capabilities. The agent selects a relevant skill, utilizes it during execution, and distills new skills from experience. Existing methods optimize these capabilities in isolation or with separate reward sources, resulting in partial and conflicting evolution. We propose Skill1, a framework that trains a single policy to co-evolve skill selection, utilization, and distillation toward a shared task-outcome objective. The policy generates a query to search the skill library, re-ranks candidates to select one, solves the task conditioned on it, and distills a new skill from the trajectory. All learning derives from a single task-outcome signal. Its low-frequency trend credits selection and its high-frequency variation credits distillation. Experiments on ALFWorld and WebShop show that Skill1 outperforms prior skill-based and reinforcement learning baselines. Training dynamics confirm the co-evolution of the three capabilities, and ablations show that removing any credit signal degrades the evolution.

</details>


### [55] [Beyond Accuracy: Policy Invariance as a Reliability Test for LLM Safety Judges](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06161v1)
*Shihao Weng,Yang Feng,Xiaofei Xie*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 现有LLM作为评判员的评估器缺乏策略不变性，评估策略的微小变化可导致判决大幅翻转，论文提出压力测试协议和不变性分数来暴露这一问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准将LLM评判员的判定视为真实代理，未检查其是否依赖于评估策略的措辞，缺乏对裁判可靠性的基本保证。

Method: 将策略不变性操作化为三个可测试原则，并实例化为压力测试协议，在ASSEBench和R-Judge轨迹上测试四个代理类评判员。

Result: 评判员对有意义规范转变和无意义结构重写反应强度相似；内容保持重写导致9.1%的额外翻转，其中18-43%发生在无歧义案例；安全分数混淆了代理行为与评估提示。

Conclusion: 贡献策略不变性分数和法官卡报告协议，揭示排行榜无法显示的可靠性差异，并发布协议和代码以推动评估器审计。

中文摘要：LLM作为评判员的管道已成为代理安全的事实上的评估器，然而现有基准将其判定视为真实代理，而不检查这些判定是否取决于代理的行为，或者仅仅取决于评估策略的措辞。我们认为，任何可信赖的安全评判员必须满足我们称之为策略不变性的基本属性，并将其操作化为三个可测试原则：在认证等价重写下的评分准则语义不变性，在有意识地从严格到宽容转变下的评分准则阈值不变性，以及歧义感知校准，使得判定不稳定性集中在真正有歧义的案例上。将这些原则实例化为一个压力测试协议，对来自ASSEBench和R-Judge的轨迹上的四个代理类评判员，我们发现了一个以前未被测量的失败模式：当今的评判员对有意义规范转变和无意义结构重写具有相当的反应强度，并且无法区分两者。内容保持的策略重写使得高达9.1%的判定翻转为超出基线抖动，在这种重写下，所有观察到的翻转中有18-43%发生在无歧义的案例上，因此现有的安全分数混淆了代理的行为与评估器被提示的方式。除了诊断，我们还贡献了策略不变性分数和评判员卡报告协议，这些揭示了评判员可靠性上数量级的差异，而仅凭准确率的排行榜无法看到这些差异。我们发布该协议和代码，以便未来的代理安全基准可以审计自己的评估器，而不是默认信任它们。

Original abstract: LLM-as-a-Judge pipelines have become the de facto evaluator for agent safety, yet existing benchmarks treat their verdicts as ground-truth proxies without checking whether the verdicts depend on the agent's behavior or merely on how the evaluation policy happens to be worded. We argue that any trustworthy safety judge must satisfy a basic property we call policy invariance, and we operationalize it as three testable principles: rubric-semantics invariance under certified-equivalent rewrites, rubric-threshold invariance under intentional strict-to-lenient shifts, and ambiguity-aware calibration so that verdict instability concentrates on genuinely ambiguous cases. Instantiating these principles as a stress-test protocol with four agent-class judges on trajectories drawn from ASSEBench and R-Judge, we surface a previously unmeasured failure mode: today's judges respond to meaningful normative shifts and to meaningless structural rewrites with comparable strength, and cannot tell the two apart. Content-preserving policy rewrites flip up to 9.1% of verdicts above baseline jitter, and 18-43% of all observed flips occur on unambiguous cases under such rewrites, so existing safety scores conflate what the agent did with how the evaluator was prompted. Beyond the diagnosis, we contribute the Policy Invariance Score and the Judge Card reporting protocol, which expose an order-of-magnitude spread in judge reliability that is invisible to accuracy-only leaderboards. We release the protocol and code so that future agent-safety benchmarks can audit their own evaluators rather than trust them by default.

</details>


### [56] [BioMedArena: An Open-source Toolkit for Building and Evaluating Biomedical Deep Research Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06177v2)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出BioMedArena，解耦注入、工具暴露、工具选择、框架模式、上下文管理和评分六个评估层，提供166个基准和75个工具，支持快速添加新模型/基准/工具，并附带6种框架和6种上下文管理策略。

Result: 装备最佳组件后，所有12个骨干模型性能显著提升，在8个代表性生物医学基准上平均超越先前最先进水平15.01个百分点。

Conclusion: BioMedArena通过开源工具包和标准化评估环境，有效缓解了深度研究智能体的可复现性问题，并展示了组件通用性带来的性能提升。

中文摘要：如今，复现和比较深度研究智能体非常困难：由于基准测试框架和工具注册表的不同，相同的骨干模型在相同基准上评估时，不同论文可能报告不同的准确率；将新模型整合到可比较的评估环境中需要花费数周的模型特定工程。这些都是深度研究智能体研究中更广泛可复现性问题的症状。在此，我们介绍BioMedArena，这是一个开源工具包，旨在解决这一可复现性差距，并提供一个在共享评估环境下比较深度研究智能体的竞技场。BioMedArena将生物医学智能体评估的六个层次解耦——基准加载、工具暴露、工具选择、框架模式、上下文管理和评分——并提供了涵盖9个功能家族的166个生物医学基准和75个生物医学工具。添加新模型、基准或工具只需几行提供者适配器代码。除了评估基础设施外，BioMedArena还附带了一个高质量参考组件库：6个智能体框架（包括我们提出的Mutual-Evolve）和6个上下文管理策略，其中任何一个都可以装备在任何骨干模型上。装备这些组件显著提升了所有12个骨干模型；在8个代表性生物医学基准上，装备最佳的骨干模型平均超过先前最先进水平15.01个百分点。工具包、配置和每任务轨迹可在https://github.com/AI-in-Health/BioMedArena获取。

Original abstract: Reproducing and comparing deep research agents today is hard: the same backbone evaluated on the same benchmark can report different accuracies across papers because the harness and tool registry differ, and integrating a new model into a comparable evaluation surface costs weeks of model-specific engineering. These are symptoms of a broader reproducibility problem in deep research agent research. Here, we introduce BioMedArena, an open-source toolkit that addresses this reproducibility gap and provides an arena for comparing deep research agents under a shared evaluation environment. BioMedArena decouples six layers of biomedical agent evaluation -- benchmark loading, tool exposure, tool selection, harness mode, context management, and scoring -- and exposes 166 biomedical benchmarks and 75 biomedical tools across 9 functional families. Adding a new model, benchmark, or tool can be accomplished with a few-line provider adapter. Beyond evaluation infrastructure, BioMedArena ships a library of high-quality reference components: 6 agent harnesses (including our proposed Mutual-Evolve) and 6 context-management strategies, any of which can be equipped on any backbone. Equipping these components substantially improves all 12 backbones; on each of 8 representative biomedical benchmarks, the best equipped backbone surpasses prior state-of-the-art (SOTA), by 15.01 percentage points on average. The toolkit, configurations, and per-task traces are available at https://github.com/AI-in-Health/BioMedArena.

### [57] [Event-Causal RAG: A Retrieval-Augmented Generation Framework for Long Video Reasoning in Complex Scenarios](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06185v1)
*Peizheng Yan,Yu Zhao,Liang Xie,Juntong Qi,Mingming Wang,Erwei Yin*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 长视频推理RAG框架，用因果图组织记忆，对agent长期记忆与检索有启发

TL;DR: 提出 Event-Causal RAG，通过将视频分割成语义事件并构建状态-事件-状态图，结合双向检索和双存储记忆，有效解决了超长视频推理中的记忆和因果建模问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大视觉语言模型在超长视频推理中记忆不连贯、因果建模弱，且端到端方法受自注意力复杂度限制，RAG方法碎片化且成本高。

Method: 将流式视频分割为语义事件，每个事件表示为状态-事件-状态图，合并为全局事件知识图并存入双存储记忆，采用双向检索策略获取因果链和视频证据，供视频基础模型生成答案。

Result: 在长视频理解基准上持续优于基于片段的检索方法和长上下文视频模型，尤其在多事件集成和跨时间间隔因果推理任务上表现突出，同时提升了记忆效率和流式性能。

Conclusion: Event-Causal RAG 是一种高效、轻量的超长视频推理框架，能有效解决现有方法的记忆和因果建模缺陷，并在多项指标上达到更优性能。

中文摘要：近期的大型视觉语言模型在短到中等长度视频理解上取得了强大性能，但在超长甚至无限视频推理方面仍然不足，因为模型必须在长时间跨度内保持连贯记忆，并推断时间上遥远事件之间的因果依赖关系。现有的端到端视频理解方法从根本上受到自注意力机制 O(n²) 复杂度的限制，而最近的检索增强生成（RAG）方法仍然存在片段级记忆碎片化、时间和因果结构建模薄弱以及存储和在线推理成本高的问题。我们提出了 Event-Causal RAG，一种轻量级的检索增强框架，用于无限长视频推理。我们的方法不是索引固定长度的片段，而是将流式视频分割成语义连贯的事件，并将每个事件表示为结构化的状态-事件-状态（SES）图，捕获事件及其周围的状态转换。这些图合并成一个全局事件知识图，并存储在双存储记忆系统中，支持语义匹配和因果拓扑检索。在此记忆基础上，我们设计了一种双向检索策略，以高效识别最相关的事件因果链，并将其连同相关视频证据一起提供给骨干视频基础模型以生成答案。在长视频理解基准上的实验表明，Event-Causal RAG 持续优于强基线（基于片段的检索方法和长上下文视频模型），特别是在需要多事件集成和跨长时间间隔因果推理的问题上，同时实现了更高的记忆效率和稳健的流式处理性能。

Original abstract: Recent large vision-language models have achieved strong performance on short- and medium-length video understanding, yet they remain inadequate for ultra-long or even infinite video reasoning, where models must preserve coherent memory over extended durations and infer causal dependencies across temporally distant events. Existing end-to-end video understanding methods are fundamentally limited by the $O(n^2)$ complexity of self-attention, while recent retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) approaches still suffer from fragmented clip-level memory, weak modeling of temporal and causal structure, and high storage and online inference costs. We present Event-Causal RAG, a lightweight retrieval-augmented framework for infinite long-video reasoning. Instead of indexing fixed-length clips, our method segments streaming videos into semantically coherent events and represents each event as a structured State-Event-State (SES) graph, capturing the event together with its surrounding state transitions. These graphs are merged into a global Event Knowledge Graph and stored in a dual-store memory that supports both semantic matching and causal-topological retrieval. On top of this memory, we design a bidirectional retrieval strategy to efficiently identify the most relevant event causal chains and provide them, together with the associated video evidence, to a backbone video foundation model for answer generation. Experiments on long-video understanding benchmarks demonstrate that Event-Causal RAG consistently outperforms strong clip-based retrieval baselines and long-context video models, particularly on questions requiring multi-event integration and causal inference across long temporal gaps, while also achieving improved memory efficiency and robust streaming performance.

</details>


### [58] [Beyond Fixed Benchmarks and Worst-Case Attacks: Dynamic Boundary Evaluation for Language Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06213v2)
*Haoxiang Wang,Da Yu,Huishuai Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 动态边界评估方法，可迁移至agent能力评估

TL;DR: 提出动态边界评估（DBE），通过主动定位模型边界并置于统一难度尺度，克服固定基准的天花板和地板效应，实现无饱和的模型评估。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有固定基准对所有模型应用相同测试项，导致天花板和地板效应，掩盖了能力差距；最具信息量的评估信号应在每个提示通过概率接近0.5的边界处。

Method: 提出动态边界评估（DBE），包括：(i) 经过9个参考LLM验证的校准题库（覆盖安全、能力、真实性）；(ii) 技能引导边界搜索（SGBS）算法，仅用API查询即可为目标模型找到边界项；(iii) 评估协议，将新模型置于统一能力尺度，并在超出题库时自适应扩展。

Result: 在有害请求拒绝、过度拒绝、约束性指令遵循和多轮谄媚抵抗四个类别上实例化，评估覆盖了更广的模型谱且无饱和，同时与现有数据集兼容。

Conclusion: 动态边界评估提供了更具信息量的评估信号，通过主动定位边界和统一难度尺度，有效避免了基准测试的饱和问题，并能兼容现有数据集。

中文摘要：如今，评估大型语言模型（LLM）依赖于固定基准，这些基准对任何模型都应用相同的测试项，从而产生掩盖能力差距的天花板和地板效应。我们认为，最具信息量的评估信号位于边界附近，即在随机采样解码下，每个提示的通过概率接近0.5。为此，我们提出动态边界评估（DBE），该方法主动定位每个模型的边界，并将其置于全局可比较的难度尺度上。DBE提供三个成果：（i）一个经过校准的题库，涵盖安全性、能力和真实性，其中每项的难度标签经过9个参考LLM的验证；（ii）技能引导边界搜索（SGBS），一种仅通过API级查询访问即可为目标LLM找到边界项的搜索算法；（iii）一个评估协议，将新LLM置于统一的能力尺度上，并在目标超出题库覆盖范围时自适应地扩展评估集。我们在四个类别上实例化DBE，涵盖安全性（有害请求拒绝和过度拒绝）、能力（约束性指令遵循）和真实性（多轮谄媚抵抗）。由此产生的评估覆盖了更广泛的模型谱，且无饱和现象，同时与现有数据集保持兼容。

Original abstract: Evaluating large language models (LLMs) today rests on fixed benchmarks that apply the same set of items to any model, producing ceiling and floor effects that mask capability gaps. We argue that the most informative evaluation signal lies at the boundary, where the per-prompt pass probability is near $0.5$ under random-sampling decoding, and propose Dynamic Boundary Evaluation (DBE), which actively locates each model's boundary and places it on a globally comparable difficulty scale. DBE delivers three artifacts: (i) a calibrated item bank covering safety, capability, and truthfulness, with per-item difficulty labels validated across $9$ reference LLMs; (ii) Skill-Guided Boundary Search (SGBS), a search algorithm that finds boundary items for a given target LLM using only API-level query access; and (iii) an evaluation protocol that places a new LLM on a unified ability scale and grows the evaluation set adaptively when the target falls outside the bank's coverage. We instantiate DBE on four categories spanning safety (harmful request refusal and over-refusal), capability (constrained instruction following), and truthfulness (multi-turn sycophancy resistance). The resulting evaluation covers a broader model spectrum without saturation while remaining compatible with existing datasets.

### [59] [Joint Consistency: A Unified Test-Time Aggregation Framework via Energy Minimization](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06219v1)
*Yunzhen Yao,Hongye Wang,Yahong Wang,Michael C. Gastpar,Bo Jiang,Lie He*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 测试时推理聚合框架，可用于agent答案验证与自洽性

TL;DR: 提出联合一致性（JC）方法，通过考虑候选轨迹间的比较交互（而非孤立信号）来改进测试时聚合，实验表明优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有测试时聚合方法忽略了候选轨迹间的比较交互，仅依赖孤立评估信号或答案频率，导致聚合效果不佳。

Method: 将测试时聚合形式化为约束Ising型能量最小化问题，其中独立评估信号为外部场，成对比较为交互；利用LLM-as-a-judge构建交互矩阵，并开发高效近似策略。

Result: 在数学和代码推理基准上，JC在多种任务、评判模型、轨迹预算和轨迹生成设置中一致优于现有基线。

Conclusion: JC提供了一个统一的测试时聚合框架，通过考虑比较交互显著提升了聚合性能。

中文摘要：本文研究了测试时聚合，一种生成多个推理轨迹并将它们聚合成最终答案的方法。现有大多数方法依赖于从候选轨迹中孤立地收集评估信号或答案频率，而忽略了候选之间的比较交互。我们提出了联合一致性（JC），将其形式化为一个约束的Ising型能量最小化问题，其中独立评估信号充当外部场，成对比较充当交互。JC提供了一个统一的测试时聚合框架，将现有的投票和加权聚合方法作为特例。我们的交互矩阵构建利用了LLM-as-a-judge比较，并在答案级同质性假设下具有理论解释。此外，我们开发了一种高效的近似策略，使交互建模对于大规模测试时聚合是可行的。在数学和代码推理基准上的实验表明，JC在任务、评判模型、轨迹预算和轨迹生成设置中始终优于现有基线。

Original abstract: This paper studies test-time aggregation, an approach that generates multiple reasoning traces and aggregates them into a final answer. Most existing methods rely on evaluation signals collected from candidate traces in isolation or answer frequencies, while ignoring comparative interactions among candidates. We propose Joint Consistency (JC), formulated as a constrained Ising-type energy minimization problem, where independent evaluation signals act as external fields and pairwise comparisons act as interactions. JC provides a unified framework for test-time aggregation that subsumes existing voting and weighted aggregation methods as special cases. Our construction of the interaction matrix leverages LLM-as-a-judge comparisons, and admits a theoretical interpretation under answer-level homogeneity assumptions. Moreover, we develop an efficient approximation strategy that makes interaction modeling practical for large-scale test-time aggregation. Experiments on math and code reasoning benchmarks show that JC consistently outperforms existing baselines across tasks, judge models, trace budgets, and trace-generation settings.

### [60] [ProCompNav: Proactive Instance Navigation with Comparative Judgment for Ambiguous User Queries](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06223v3)
*Junhyuk Kwon,Seungjoon Lee,Hyejin Park,Kyle Min,Jungseul Ok*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 主动询问与比较判断消歧方法，可用于agent交互与主动学习

TL;DR: 提出ProCompNav框架，通过主动比较判断来区分目标与干扰物，提升导航成功率并减少用户响应长度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在初始请求不唯一时难以有效区分目标，常导致过早决策或冗长对话。

Method: 两阶段框架：先构建候选池，再通过每轮提取属性-值对询问二元问题，剪除不一致候选，实现池级别判别性询问。

Result: 在CoIN-Bench上提升成功率并减少响应长度，在TextNav上达到最先进成功率。

Conclusion: 比较判断在实例级导航中广泛有效，可提升系统主动询问的效率。

中文摘要：在初始用户请求未唯一指定目标实例的情况下，自然语言实例导航变得具有挑战性。一个实用的智能体应通过主动仅询问区分目标与相似干扰物所需的信息来减轻用户负担，而不是要求事先提供详细描述。现有方法往往无法实现这一目标：它们可能在充分探索替代方案之前就停留在第一个看似合理的候选项上，或者，即使在收集了多个候选项后，它们询问的是基于单个候选目标属性的问题，而不是选择能够区分候选池中目标的问题。结果，尽管进行了对话，智能体仍可能无法将目标与干扰物区分开，导致过早决策和冗长的用户响应。我们提出了一种名为ProCompNav的主动比较判断实例导航框架，这是一个两阶段框架，首先构建候选池，然后通过比较判断识别目标。在每一轮中，ProCompNav提取一个能够分割当前池的属性-值对，询问一个二元是/否问题，并立即剪除所有不一致的候选。这将消歧从开放式目标描述重新定义为池级别的判别性询问，其中每个问题都被选择来缩小候选集。在CoIN-Bench上，ProCompNav在相同最小输入下相比交互式基线以及具有详细描述的非交互式基线提高了成功率，同时大幅减少了响应长度。ProCompNav还在TextNav上取得了最先进成功率，表明比较判断在类似干扰物之间的实例级导航中具有广泛适用性。代码可在https://github.com/tree-jhk/procompnav获取。

Original abstract: Natural-language instance navigation becomes challenging when the initial user request does not uniquely specify the target instance. A practical agent should reduce the user's burden by actively asking only the information needed to distinguish the target from similar distractors, rather than requiring a detailed description upfront. Existing approaches often fall short of this goal: they may stop at the first plausible candidate before sufficiently exploring alternatives, or, even after collecting multiple candidates, ask about the target's attributes derived from individual candidates rather than questions selected to distinguish candidates in the pool. As a result, despite the dialogue, the agent may still fail to distinguish the target from distractors, leading to premature decisions and lengthy user responses. We propose Proactive Instance Navigation with Comparative Judgment (ProCompNav), a two-stage framework that first constructs a candidate pool and then identifies the target through comparative judgment. At each round, ProCompNav extracts an attribute-value pair that splits the current pool, asks a binary yes/no question, and prunes all inconsistent candidates at once. This reframes disambiguation from open-ended target description to pool-level discriminative questioning, where each question is chosen to narrow the candidate set. On CoIN-Bench, ProCompNav improves Success Rate over interactive baselines with the same minimal input and non-interactive baselines with detailed descriptions, while substantially reducing Response Length. ProCompNav also achieves state-of-the-art Success Rate on TextNav, suggesting that comparative judgment is broadly useful for instance-level navigation among similar distractors. Code is available at https://github.com/tree-jhk/procompnav.

</details>

中文摘要：随着大型模型从对话助手演变为自主代理，长期决策、工具使用和真实环境交互带来的挑战日益增多。现有的代理基础设施在评估、数据管理和代理演化方面仍然支离破碎，使得难以系统地发现风险并在持续闭环中改进模型。在本报告中，我们提出了	extbf{Safactory}，一个用于可信自主智能的可扩展代理工厂。Safactory集成了三个紧密耦合的平台：用于轨迹生成的	extbf{并行模拟平台}、用于轨迹存储和经验提取的	extbf{可信数据平台}，以及用于异步强化学习和在策略蒸馏的	extbf{自主演化平台}。据我们所知，Safactory是第一个为下一代可信自主智能提出统一演化管道的框架。

Original abstract: As large models evolve from conversational assistants into autonomous agents, challenges increasingly arise from long-horizon decision making, tool use, and real environment interaction. Existing agenticinfrastructure remain fragmented across evaluation, data management, and agent evolution, making it difficult to discover risks systematically and improve models in a continuous closed loop. In this report, we present \textbf{Safactory}, a scalable agent factory for trustworthy autonomous intelligence. Safactory integrates three tightly coupled platforms: a \textbf{Parallel Simulation Platform} for trajectory generation, a \textbf{Trustworthy Data Platform} for trajectory storage and experience extraction, and an \textbf{Autonomous Evolution Platform} for asynchronous reinforcement learning and on-policy distillation. As far as we know, Safactory is the first framework to propose a unified evolutionary pipeline for next-generation trustworthy autonomous intelligence.
