### [62] [Measuring Black-Box Confidence via Reasoning Trajectories: Geometry, Coverage, and Verbalization](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06308v1)
*Marc Boubnovski Martell,Josefa Lia Stoisser,Kaspar Märtens,Jialin Yu,Robert Kitchen,Philip Torr,Jesper Ferkinghoff-Borg*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 通过推理轨迹进行黑盒置信度估计，可直接用于agent自我评估与反思机制。

TL;DR: 提出一种黑盒轨迹置信度分数，通过滑动窗口和单参数softmax衡量CoT轨迹收敛性，在多个基准上优于自我一致性，且融合三个通道（覆盖率、几何结构、口头化）效果更佳。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有黑盒置信度方法（如自我一致性）线性昂贵且忽略轨迹几何结构，需要更高效且利用轨迹结构的置信度估计。

Method: 将CoT嵌入为滑动窗口轨迹，用单参数softmax测量其与外部答案锚点的收敛性，融合覆盖率、几何结构和口头化置信度三个通道。

Result: 在6/6设置中，融合方法（K=4）优于自我一致性（K=8），中位AUC从0.71提升至0.78；几何结构在倒数第二个窗口峰值；融合在17/18设置中优于单通道。

Conclusion: 黑盒轨迹置信度分数有效且高效，几何结构提供关键信号，融合多通道可显著提升置信度估计性能。

中文摘要：可靠的置信度估计使得通过纯文本API安全部署链式思维(CoT)推理成为可能。然而，主流的黑盒基线方法——基于K个样本的自我一致性——在计算上呈线性增长且忽略了轨迹的几何结构。我们提出了一种黑盒轨迹置信度分数：将CoT嵌入为滑动窗口轨迹，并通过单参数softmax测量其与外部答案锚点的收敛性。该方法无需logits、隐藏状态或有监督校准器。在MedQA-USMLE、GPQA Diamond和MMLUP-Pro上，使用Gemini 3.1 Pro和Claude Sonnet 4.6的六个（基准，推理器）设置中，将该分数与覆盖率和口头化置信度通道融合（K=4），在6/6的设置中实现了对K=8自我一致性的Pareto改进（中位数AUC 0.78 vs 0.71，deltaAUC=+0.075）。固定选择控制（+0.060）和E5交叉嵌入器复制排除了答案切换和单一供应商伪影。几何结构在所有基准和推理器的倒数第二个窗口中达到峰值，并在GPQA Diamond的终端窗口上反转。三种无脚手架机制将黑盒置信度分离为法官中介的覆盖率先验(C)、轨迹内几何结构(G)和条件性口头化通道(V)。在18个基准×推理器×提议者设置中，C和G分别在18/18和16/18中提供独立信号，而V在6/18中贡献残余信号。将法官从GPT-5-mini更换为Claude Sonnet 4.6，G-only AUC保持不变（|delta|<=0.013），C-only AUC最多变化+/-0.02（kappa=0.82）。融合在17/18的设置中优于最佳单一通道（中位数AUC 0.78，最大0.92）。

Original abstract: Reliable confidence estimation enables safe deployment of chain-of-thought (CoT) reasoning through text-only APIs. Yet the dominant black-box baseline, self-consistency over K samples, is linearly expensive and ignores the geometry of the trace. We propose a black-box trajectory-confidence score: we embed a CoT as a sliding-window trajectory and measure its convergence to external answer anchors with a one-parameter softmax. The method needs no logits, hidden states, or supervised calibrators. Across six (benchmark, reasoner) settings on MedQA-USMLE, GPQA Diamond, and MMLU-Pro with Gemini 3.1 Pro and Claude Sonnet 4.6, fusing this score with coverage and verbalized-confidence channels at K=4 yields Pareto improvements over self-consistency at K=8 in 6/6 settings (median AUC 0.78 vs 0.71, deltaAUC=+0.075). A fixed-pick control (+0.060) and E5 cross-embedder replication rule out answer switching and single-vendor artifacts. Geometry peaks in the penultimate window across benchmarks and reasoners, and inverts at the terminal window on GPQA Diamond. Three unscaffolded regimes separate black-box confidence into a judge-mediated Coverage prior (C), within-trace Geometry (G), and a conditional Verbalization channel (V). Across 18 benchmark x reasoner x proposer settings, C and G provide independent signal in 18/18 and 16/18, while V contributes residual signal in 6/18. Swapping the judge from GPT-5-mini to Claude Sonnet 4.6 leaves G-only AUC unchanged (|delta|<=0.013) and shifts C-only AUC by at most +/-0.02 (kappa=0.82). Fusion beats the best single channel in 17/18 settings (median AUC 0.78, max 0.92).

</details>


### [63] [A Regime Theory of Controller Class Selection for LLM Action Decisions](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06339v1)
*Zhaoyang Jiang,Zhizhong Fu,Yunsoo Kim,Jiacong Mi,Zicheng Li,Xuanqi Peng,Honghan Wu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出LLM行动决策的控制器类选择理论，可迁移至coding agent的retrieve/defer/abstain策略。

TL;DR: 本文提出一种机制理论，通过三个数据可估计的瓶颈选择最优控制器类别，解决了有限样本下不同控制器偏好不一致的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有直觉认为更大的每输入表达能力总是有益，但在有限样本下不同基准偏好不同控制器类别，需要理论指导如何选择。

Method: 将控制器组织为固定动作、分区路由器、实例级控制器和先验门控控制器的嵌套格，基于三个可估计瓶颈（超越固定动作的改进潜力、实例级决策的样本充足性、分区路由器的恢复能力）推导伯恩斯坦紧致阈值和严格嵌套交叉验证来类别选择。

Result: 在SMS-Spam、HallusionBench、A-OKVQA和FOLIO上，预测类别与经验赢家一致；在TextVQA上先验门控控制器获胜。

Conclusion: 提出的机制理论和选择方法有效，可指导实际部署中控制器类别的选择。

中文摘要：部署的语言和视觉-语言模型必须在每个输入上决定是直接回答、检索证据、延迟到更强的模型还是弃权。与常见的单调性直觉相反，在有限样本中，更大的每输入表达能力并不总是有益的：在相同的严格交叉验证下，不同的基准偏好不同的控制器类别。这反映了实例级不确定性信号的有限样本局限性，这种局限性在依赖于分布尺度上可能会被耗尽。我们将控制器组织成一个嵌套的四类格：固定动作、分区路由器、实例级控制器和先验门控控制器，按复杂度排序。我们证明了一个机制理论，将三个可数据估计的瓶颈转化为类别选择：超越最佳固定动作可能带来多少改进，是否有足够的样本使实例级控制器做出可靠决策，以及当实例级信号不可靠时，粗分区路由器可以恢复多少改进。由此产生的伯恩斯坦紧致阈值具有匹配的信息论下界，并且严格的嵌套交叉验证可证明选择接近最优的类别。在SMS-Spam、HallusionBench、A-OKVQA和FOLIO上，预测的类别与经验赢家匹配；当OCR令牌提供无标签的预测时先验时，先验门控控制器在TextVQA上获胜。代码可在https://github.com/Anonymous-Awesome-Submissions/Regime-Theory获取。

Original abstract: Deployed language and vision-language models must decide, on each input, whether to answer directly, retrieve evidence, defer to a stronger model, or abstain. Contrary to the common monotonicity intuition, greater per-input expressivity is not uniformly beneficial in finite samples: under identical strict cross-validation, different benchmarks prefer different controller classes. This reflects a finite-sample limitation of instance-level uncertainty signals, which can be exhausted at a distribution-dependent scale. We organize controllers into a nested lattice of four classes: fixed actions, partition routers, instance-level controllers, and prior-gated controllers, ordered by complexity. We prove a regime theory that turns three data-estimable bottlenecks into a class choice: how much improvement is possible beyond the best fixed action, whether there are enough samples for instance-level controllers to make reliable decisions, and how much improvement a coarse partition router can recover when instance-level signal is unreliable. The resulting Bernstein-tight threshold has a matching information-theoretic lower bound, and strict nested cross-validation provably selects a near-best class. Across SMS-Spam, HallusionBench, A-OKVQA, and FOLIO, the predicted class matches the empirical winner; the prior-gated controller wins on TextVQA when OCR tokens supply a label-free prediction-time prior. Code is available at https://github.com/Anonymous-Awesome-Submissions/Regime-Theory.

</details>


### [64] [More Than Can Be Said: A Benchmark and Framework for Pre-Question Scientific Ideation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06345v1)
*Jie Yu,Song Qiu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 多agent框架将隐式理解显式化，可启发coding agent的规划与假设验证。

TL;DR: 提出了InciteResearch多智能体框架，将研究者的隐性理解显性化，通过苏格拉底式提问分解和因果推理，显著提升了AI研究辅助的创新能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有AI研究助手需要清晰明确的输入，但人类研究常始于模糊的隐性摩擦，缺乏将隐含知识转化为可操作问题的能力。

Method: 构建了InciteResearch框架，包含三个步骤：1) 从模糊输入提取五维研究者画像；2) 通过最大化可行性-新颖性乘积和七步因果推导违反隐藏假设；3) 验证方法是否为重构洞察的必要结果。同时提出了TF-Bench基准。

Result: 在TF-Bench上，InciteResearch相比基线将新颖性从3.671提升至4.250，影响力从3.806提升至4.397，生成的提案从重组式转变为架构洞察式。

Conclusion: AI可以作为思维本身的延伸，而不仅仅是自动执行工具，实现了从隐性到显性的研究辅助跨越。

中文摘要：AI研究助手在自动化文献检索和手稿优化方面显示出强大潜力，但大多数助手假设输入清晰且可操作，仅在研究问题明确后运行。相比之下，人类研究往往从隐性摩擦开始，即在问题形成之前的一种错位感。我们提出了InciteResearch，一个多智能体框架，旨在使研究者的隐含理解变得明确、可检查和可操作。InciteResearch将苏格拉底式提问的逻辑链分解并分布到整个流程中：（1）从模糊甚至与领域无关的输入中，引出由特定摩擦点锚定的结构化五维研究者画像状态；（2）通过最大化可行性-新颖性乘积并强制执行七阶段因果推导轨迹，违反隐藏假设；（3）检查所提出的方法是否是重构洞察的必要结果。我们还引入了TF-Bench，这是第一个隐性到显性研究辅助的基准，它区分了四种科学模式下与领域相关和与领域无关的灵感。在TF-Bench上，InciteResearch相比基于提示的基线取得了跨越式提升（新颖性/影响力从3.671/3.806提高到4.250/4.397），将生成的提案从重组转变为架构洞察。我们的工作表明，AI可以作为思维本身的延伸，而不仅仅是自动化下游执行。

Original abstract: AI research agents have shown strong potential in automating literature search and manuscript refinement, yet most assume a clear and actionable initial input, operating only after a research question has been made explicit. In contrast, human research often begins with tacit friction, a sense of misalignment before a question can be formed. We introduce InciteResearch, a multi-agent framework designed to make a researcher's implicit understanding explicit, inspectable, and actionable. InciteResearch decomposes the logical chain of Socratic questioning and distributes it across the entire pipeline that: (1) Elicits a structured five-dimensional researcher profile state anchored by specific friction points from vague, even domain-unrelated inputs; (2) Violates hidden assumptions by maximizing the feasibility-novelty product with enforcing a 7-stage causal derivation trace; and (3) check whether the proposed method is a Necessary consequence of the reframed insight. We further introduce TF-Bench, the first benchmark for tacit-to-explicit research assistance that distinguishes domain-related from domain-unrelated inspirations across four scientific modes. On TF-Bench, InciteResearch achieves leapfrogging gains over a prompt-based baseline (novelty/impact from 3.671/3.806 to 4.250/4.397), shifting generated proposals from recombination to architectural insight. Our work demonstrates that AI can serve as an extension of thinking itself, rather than merely automating downstream execution.

### [65] [Prediction and Empowerment: A Theory of Agency through Bridge Interfaces](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06346v1)
*Richard Csaky*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出agent设计原则区分识别与控制，对agent架构有理论启发。

TL;DR: 在确定性部分可观测环境下，代理的预测、压缩和赋能可分离；预测可通过识别隐藏商数或覆盖控制实现，赋能不足；接口细化和目标条件赋能是关键；结果建议AI设计应区分不同目标成分。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究在确定性世界中部分可观测性下代理的预测、压缩和赋能之间的关系，为设计更有效的AI系统提供理论基础。

Method: 构建确定性POMDP模型，通过桥接接口将感知和驱动分为代理控制和环境控制部分，利用信息论和因果推理证明分离定理，并通过比特串特化展示权衡。

Result: 证明完美预测可通过识别或覆盖控制实现，赋能不足；接口细化和目标条件赋能有助于减少不确定性；识别需要内部容量，覆盖需要终端动作容量。

Conclusion: AI设计应区分隐藏状态识别、接口细化、任务相关可控性和干扰控制，人机对齐是接口设计问题。

中文摘要：我们研究了在确定性物理或模拟世界中部分可观测条件下的代理问题，其中表观随机性源于对初始条件、固定法则位和展开的外生噪声的不确定性。我们将感知和驱动建模为在代理控制参数与环境控制的通道状态之间分割的桥接接口，通过潜在微观状态上的先验和一对多的观测粗化，导出一个确定性POMDP。在此框架内，我们证明了预测、压缩和赋能之间的分离。完美预测可以通过识别与目标家族相关的隐藏商数或通过覆盖控制使未来目标由动作决定来实现；仅靠高赋能是不够的。在可细化接口和足够记忆的条件下，动作条件观测压缩进展减少了关于潜在商数的后验不确定性，而当细化需要引导世界侧通道条件时，这产生了目标条件接口赋能。一个具有保守信息预算的比特串特化使得由此产生的权衡显式化：通过识别进行预测需要至少相关潜在熵的内部容量，而通过覆盖控制则需要针对受控商数的终端动作容量。对于现代AI代理，结果建议了一个设计原则而非必然性定理：目标应区分隐藏状态识别、接口细化、任务相关可控性以及单纯的覆盖或干扰控制。人机对齐部分是一个接口设计问题，相关桥梁位于人类意图、代理内部状态、外部工具和世界侧通道条件之间。这是一份工作草案：欢迎反馈和批评。

Original abstract: We study agency under partial observability in deterministic physical or simulated worlds, where apparent randomness arises from uncertainty over initial conditions, fixed law bits, and unrolled exogenous noise. We model sensing and actuation as bridge interfaces split between agent-controlled parameters and environment-controlled channel state, inducing a deterministic POMDP through a prior over latent microstates and many-to-one observation coarsening. Within this framework, we prove a separation between prediction, compression, and empowerment. Perfect prediction can be achieved either by identifying the hidden quotient relevant to the target family or by overwrite control that makes the future target action-determined; high empowerment alone is insufficient. Under refinable interfaces and sufficient memory, action-conditioned observation-compression progress reduces posterior uncertainty about the latent quotient, and when refinement requires steering world-side channel conditions, this creates target-conditioned interface empowerment. A bit-string specialization with a conserved information budget makes the resulting tradeoff explicit: prediction by identification requires internal capacity at least the relevant latent entropy, whereas overwrite control requires terminal action capacity over the controlled quotient. For modern AI agents, the results suggest a design principle rather than a theorem of inevitability: objectives should distinguish hidden-state identification, interface refinement, task-relevant controllability, and mere overwrite or distractor control. Human--AI alignment is partly an interface-design problem, where the relevant bridge is between human intent, agent internal state, external tools, and world-side channel conditions. This is a working draft: feedback and criticism is most welcome.

</details>


### [66] [From Agent Loops to Deterministic Graphs: Execution Lineage for Reproducible AI-Native Work](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06365v1)
*Josh Rosen,Seth Rosen*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 执行谱系通过有向无环图表示AI工作，实现稳定的中间状态和精确的更新，在策略备忘录更新任务中优于循环基线，提供了更好的变更隔离和一致性保证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的LLM代理工作流依赖隐式对话状态，难以保留稳定工作产品、隔离无关更新或传播变化，导致维护困难。

Method: 提出执行谱系模型，将AI工作表示为有向无环图（DAG），具有显式依赖、稳定中间边界和基于身份的重放，并在两个受控策略备忘录更新任务中与循环基线进行比较。

Result: 在无关分支更新中，DAG重放精确保留最终备忘录，零污染；循环基线常引入无关上下文。在中间工件编辑中，DAG重放实现完美的上游保留、下游传播、未影响工件保留和跨工件一致性。

Conclusion: 最终答案质量与维持状态质量不同；执行谱系提供了关于变更、稳定性和演化更强保证，而循环基线可能导致状态不一致性累积。

中文摘要：大型语言模型系统越来越多地被部署为代理工作流，这些工作流交织了推理、工具使用、记忆和迭代优化。这些系统在生成答案方面很有效，但它们通常依赖于隐式的对话状态，这使得保留稳定的工作产品、隔离不相关的更新或通过中间工件传播变化变得困难。我们引入了执行谱系：一种执行模型，其中AI原生的工作被表示为有向无环图（DAG），包含产生工件的计算、显式依赖关系、稳定的中间边界和基于身份的重放。目标不是让模型成为更好的单次生成器，而是让不断演化的AI生成的工作在变化中保持可维护性。我们在两个受控的策略备忘录更新任务上比较了执行谱系重放与以循环为中心的更新基线。在一个无关分支更新中，DAG重放在所有运行中精确地保留了最终备忘录，零变动和零无关分支污染，而循环基线重新生成了备忘录并经常引入无关上下文。在一个中间工件编辑中，所有系统都在最终备忘录中反映了新的约束，但只有DAG重放实现了完美的上游保留、下游传播、未影响工件保留和跨工件一致性。这些结果表明，最终答案质量和维持状态质量是不同的。当任务是一个有界的合成/更新问题且所有当前源都适合上下文时，强大的循环基线可以在生成精致的最终输出方面保持竞争力，但即时的任务成功可能掩盖部分状态不一致性，这种不一致性可能在未来的修订中累积。执行谱系提供了关于什么应该改变、什么应该保持稳定以及工作如何在修订之间演化的更强保证。

Original abstract: Large language model systems are increasingly deployed as agentic workflows that interleave reasoning, tool use, memory, and iterative refinement. These systems are effective at producing answers, but they often rely on implicit conversational state, making it difficult to preserve stable work products, isolate irrelevant updates, or propagate changes through intermediate artifacts.
  We introduce execution lineage: an execution model in which AI-native work is represented as a directed acyclic graph (DAG) of artifact-producing computations with explicit dependencies, stable intermediate boundaries, and identity-based replay. The goal is not to make the model a better one-shot writer, but to make evolving AI-generated work maintainable under change.
  We compare execution-lineage replay against loop-centric update baselines on two controlled policy-memo update tasks. In an unrelated-branch update, DAG replay preserved the final memo exactly in all runs, with zero churn and zero unrelated-branch contamination, while loop baselines regenerated the memo and frequently imported unrelated context. In an intermediate-artifact edit, all systems reflected the new constraint in the final memo, but only DAG replay achieved perfect upstream preservation, downstream propagation, unaffected-artifact preservation, and cross-artifact consistency.
  These results show that final answer quality and maintained-state quality are distinct. Strong loop baselines can remain competitive at producing polished final outputs when the task is a bounded synthesis/update problem and all current sources fit in context, but immediate task success can mask partial state inconsistency that may compound over future revisions. Execution lineage provides stronger guarantees about what should change, what should remain stable, and how work evolves across revisions.

</details>


### [67] [Stop Comparing LLM Agents Without Disclosing the Harness](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23950v1)
*Yunbei Zhang,Janet Wang,Yingqiang Ge,Weijie Xu,Jihun Hamm,Chandan K. Reddy*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文提出绑定约束论，认为在长周期任务中，智能体执行框架比模型本身更影响性能，并建议框架感知评估。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前评估协议系统性地将框架层面的提升误归因于模型改进，导致对智能体性能的真正来源理解有偏差。

Method: 通过控制理论形式化将框架视为控制器、进行方差分解分析、提出框架感知评估框架及披露标准。

Result: 框架引起的性能方差可显著超过模型替换引起的方差，甚至导致模型排名反转。

Conclusion: 在框架规范被披露前，长周期智能体的排行榜比较不完整且可能误导，需采用框架感知的评估协议。

中文摘要：本文立场论文认为，在具有可比前沿能力的模型上评估的长周期任务中，智能体执行框架（即围绕语言模型管理上下文构建、工具交互、编排和验证的基础设施层）通常是决定智能体性能的更强因素，而非其所包裹的模型。我们形式化并捍卫绑定约束论：在这种模式下，性能方差更多由框架配置而非模型选择决定，且当前的评估协议系统性地将框架层面的提升误归因于模型改进。我们从三个方面支持这一论点。首先，控制理论形式化将框架视为闭环动力系统的控制器，而LLM是其所管理的随机策略，这解释了为何微小的框架变化能够产生超过替换模型所获得的性能变化。其次，已发表的基准测试、行业部署以及受控的方差分解表明，框架引起的方差可能显著超过模型引起的方差，包括模型排名反转的情况。第三，我们提出一个具有披露标准和方差分解协议的框架感知评估框架。在框架规范被披露之前，长周期智能体的排行榜比较应被视为不完整且可能具有误导性。

Original abstract: This position paper argues that, for long-horizon tasks evaluated across models with comparable frontier capability, the agent execution harness, namely the infrastructure layer that governs context construction, tool interaction, orchestration, and verification around a language model, is often a stronger determinant of agent performance than the model it wraps. We formalize and defend the Binding Constraint Thesis: in this regime, performance variance is governed more by harness configuration than by model choice, and current evaluation protocols therefore systematically misattribute harness-level gains to model improvements. We support this thesis along three lines. First, a control-theoretic formalization treats the harness as the controller of a closed-loop dynamical system and the LLM as the stochastic policy it governs, which explains why small harness changes can produce performance shifts that exceed those obtained by substituting one model for another. Second, published benchmarks, industry deployments, and a controlled variance decomposition show that harness-induced variance can substantially exceed model-induced variance, including cases of model ranking reversal. Third, we propose a harness-aware evaluation framework with a disclosure standard and a variance decomposition protocol. Until harness specifications are disclosed, leaderboard comparisons for long-horizon agents should be treated as incomplete and potentially misleading.

</details>


### [68] [Knowledge Graphs, the Missing Link in Agentic AI-based Formal Verification](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06434v1)
*Vaisakh Naduvodi Viswambharan,Keerthan Kopparam Radhakrishna,Deepak Narayan Gadde,Aman Kumar*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 用知识图谱和多agent工作流生成SystemVerilog断言，涉及代码验证agent，可迁移到自动代码优化。

TL;DR: 本文提出基于知识图谱的多智能体工作流以生成SystemVerilog断言，通过三个细化循环显著提升语法正确性和形式化覆盖率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法将规范与RTL视为松散文本，导致规范-设计关联弱、语义不匹配和语法错误频繁，亟需更好的结构化上下文来生成高质量断言。

Method: 构建以验证为中心的知识图谱，整合规范、RTL和工具反馈的结构化中间表示；多智能体工作流通过查询和更新KG生成SVA，并驱动语法修复、CEX引导修正和覆盖率导向增强三个细化循环。

Result: 在7个基准设计上，该方法改善了规范到RTL的关联，生成可编译SVA且语法修复开销低，形式化覆盖率达78.5%-99.4%，但复杂时序和算术推理仍具挑战。

Conclusion: 基于KG的上下文检索有效提升断言生成质量，但收敛性依赖设计，复杂推理仍是当前LLM的瓶颈。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）的最新进展使得能够从自然语言规范生成SystemVerilog断言（SVA）的工作流程成为可能，这有望加速形式化验证（FV）。然而，高质量的断言合成仍然具有挑战性，因为规范通常模糊或不完整，且关键的微架构细节存在于寄存器传输级（RTL）中。许多现有方法将规范和RTL视为松散结构的文本，这削弱了规范到RTL的关联性，导致语义不匹配，并在形式化解析和细化过程中频繁出现语法错误。本工作通过构建一个以验证为中心的知识图谱（KG）来解决这些限制，该图谱从规范、RTL和形式化工具反馈（包括语法诊断、反例（CEX）和覆盖率报告）中提取的结构化中间表示（IR）构建而成。KG将需求、设计层次结构、信号、假设和属性联系起来，为生成提供可追溯的、基于设计的上下文。一个多智能体工作流查询并更新该KG以生成SVA，并驱动三个细化循环：工具诊断引导的语法修复、使用跟踪链接的CEX引导修正以及覆盖率导向的属性增加。在七个基准设计上的评估表明，基于KG的上下文检索改善了规范到RTL的关联性，并一致地生成了可编译的SVA，且语法修复开销较低。该方法实现了78.5%至99.4%的形式化覆盖率，尽管收敛性具有设计依赖性，复杂的时序和算术推理对当前LLM能力仍具有挑战性。

Original abstract: Recent advances in Large Language Models (LLMs) have enabled workflows that generate SystemVerilog Assertions (SVAs) from natural-language specifications, with the potential to accelerate Formal Verification (FV). However, high-quality assertion synthesis remains challenging because specifications are often ambiguous or incomplete and critical micro-architectural details reside in the Register Transfer Level (RTL). Many existing approaches treat the specification and RTL as loosely structured text, which weakens specification-to-RTL grounding and leads to semantic mismatches and frequent syntax failures during formal parsing and elaboration. This work addresses these limitations with a verification-centric Knowledge Graph (KG) constructed from structured Intermediate Representations (IRs) extracted from the specification, RTL, and formal-tool feedback, including syntax diagnostics, Counterexamples (CEXs), and coverage reports. The KG links requirements, design hierarchy, signals, assumptions, and properties to provide traceable, design-grounded context for generation. A multi-agent workflow queries and updates this KG to generate SVAs and to drive three refinement loops: syntax repair guided by tool diagnostics, CEX-guided correction using trace links, and coverage-directed property augmentation. Evaluation across seven benchmark designs indicates that KG-based context retrieval improves specification-to-RTL grounding and consistently produces compilable SVAs with low syntax-repair overhead. The approach achieves formal coverage ranging from 78.5% to 99.4%, though convergence exhibits design dependence with complex temporal and arithmetic reasoning remaining challenging for current LLM capabilities.

</details>


### [69] [PrefixGuard: From LLM-Agent Traces to Online Failure-Warning Monitors](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06455v1)
*Xinmiao Huang,Jinwei Hu,Rajarshi Roy,Changshun Wu,Yi Dong,Xiaowei Huang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 从LLM agent轨迹学习在线失败预警监视器，直接涉及agent可靠性与监控，可迁移到SemOpt agent。

TL;DR: PrefixGuard是一种为LLM代理设计的前缀监控器框架，通过离线StepView归纳和监控器训练实现高效的事件抽象和风险评分，在多个基准上优于原始文本和LLM评判方法，并分析了可操作性的权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM代理执行长时间任务时，最终结果检查太晚无法干预，需要在线前缀警告，但手工事件模式脆弱且LLM判断成本高。

Method: PrefixGuard框架：离线StepView归纳从原始轨迹中提取确定性类型化步骤适配器，然后监督训练监控器学习事件抽象和前缀风险评分器。

Result: 在WebArena、τ²-Bench、SkillsBench和TerminalBench上，最强PrefixGuard监控器分别达到0.900、0.710、0.533、0.557 AUPRC，平均比原始文本控制提升+0.137 AUPRC；LLM判断较弱；推导了AUPRC可观察性上限；DFA提取状态数在不同基准上差异较大；首次警报诊断显示排序好不等同于低误报预警。

Conclusion: PrefixGuard是实用的监控器合成方案，提供诊断方法判断前缀警告是否可转化为可操作干预。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）智能体现在执行长时间、使用工具的任务，最终结果检查可能来得太晚而无法干预。在线警告需要轻量级的前缀监控器来处理异构轨迹，但手工编写的事件模式是脆弱的，部署时的LLM判断成本高昂。我们引入了PrefixGuard，这是一个轨迹到监控器的框架，包含一个离线的StepView归纳步骤，然后是监督式监控器训练。StepView从原始轨迹样本中归纳出确定性的类型化步骤适配器，监控器从终端结果学习事件抽象和前缀风险评分器。在WebArena、τ²-Bench、SkillsBench和TerminalBench上，最强的PrefixGuard监控器达到0.900/0.710/0.533/0.557 AUPRC。使用每种表示中最强的后端，它们比原始文本控制平均提高了+0.137 AUPRC。LLM判断器在相同的前缀警告协议下仍然明显较弱。我们还推导了一个基于分数的精确率-召回率曲线下面积（AUPRC）的可观察性上限，该上限将监控器错误与观察到的前缀中缺乏证据的失败区分开。对于有限状态审计，事后确定性有限自动机（DFA）提取在WebArena和τ²-Bench上保持紧凑（29和20个状态），但在SkillsBench和TerminalBench上扩展到151和187个状态。最后，首次警报诊断表明，强排序并不意味着部署效用：WebArena排序良好但无法支持低误报警报，而τ²-Bench和TerminalBench保留了更多可操作的早期警报。总之，这些结果将PrefixGuard定位为一个实用的监控器合成方案，并提供了明确的诊断方法，用于判断前缀警告何时转化为可操作的干预。

Original abstract: Large language model (LLM) agents now execute long, tool-using tasks where final outcome checks can arrive too late for intervention. Online warning requires lightweight prefix monitors over heterogeneous traces, but hand-authored event schemas are brittle and deployment-time LLM judging is costly. We introduce PrefixGuard, a trace-to-monitor framework with an offline StepView induction step followed by supervised monitor training. StepView induces deterministic typed-step adapters from raw trace samples, and the monitor learns an event abstraction and prefix-risk scorer from terminal outcomes. Across WebArena, $τ^2$-Bench, SkillsBench, and TerminalBench, the strongest PrefixGuard monitors reach 0.900/0.710/0.533/0.557 AUPRC. Using the strongest backend within each representation, they improve over raw-text controls by an average of +0.137 AUPRC. LLM judges remain substantially weaker under the same prefix-warning protocol. We also derive an observability ceiling on score-based area under the precision-recall curve (AUPRC) that separates monitor error from failures lacking evidence in the observed prefix. For finite-state audit, post-hoc deterministic finite automaton (DFA) extraction remains compact on WebArena and $τ^2$-Bench (29 and 20 states) but expands to 151 and 187 states on SkillsBench and TerminalBench. Finally, first-alert diagnostics show that strong ranking does not imply deployment utility: WebArena ranks well yet fails to support low-false-alarm alerts, whereas $τ^2$-Bench and TerminalBench retain more actionable early alerts. Together, these results position PrefixGuard as a practical monitor-synthesis recipe with explicit diagnostics for when prefix warnings translate into actionable interventions.

### [70] [Beyond Task Success: Measuring Workflow Fidelity in LLM-Based Agentic Payment Systems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06457v1)
*Donghao Huang,Joon Kiat Chua,Zhaoxia Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出轨迹级保真度指标ASR评估LLM agent工作流，对agent评测有启发，可迁移到代码优化agent。

TL;DR: 提出ASR指标评估LLM多智能体系统轨迹保真度，发现现有指标无法察觉的捷径问题，并指导改进。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有指标TSR和HF1仅关注最终结果或无序路由，无法捕获工作流中的隐藏偏差，尤其在受监管领域需要轨迹级评估。

Method: 提出ASR，分解为Transition Recall和Transition Precision，在层次化多智能体系统HMASP上评估18个LLM和90k任务。

Result: 10/18模型跳过确认检查点而TSR/HF1完美，ASR揭示；GPT-4.1有隐藏捷径，GPT-5.2完美；ASR诊断指导的改进使TSR提升高达+93.8pp。

Conclusion: 轨迹级评估（ASR）对于受监管领域至关重要，能暴露隐藏错误并指导提升。

中文摘要：基于LLM的多智能体系统越来越多地部署于支付工作流中，然而当前流行指标——任务成功率（TSR）和智能体切换F1分数（HF1）——仅捕获最终结果或无序的路由决策。我们引入了智能体成功率（ASR），一种轨迹保真度指标，在转换级别比较观察到的和预期的智能体执行序列，将性能分解为转换召回率和转换精确率。应用于层次化多智能体支付系统（HMASP），涵盖18个LLM和90,000个任务实例，ASR揭示了18个模型中有10个在支付结账时系统性地跳过一个确认检查点，这一偏差对TSR和HF1均不可见，而8个模型完美执行了该检查点。值得注意的是，GPT-4.1虽然达到了完美的TSR和HF1，但表现出隐藏的工作流捷径，而GPT-5.2达到了完美的ASR。由ASR诊断指导的提示优化和确定性路由防护措施带来了TSR的显著提升，对于先前表现不佳的模型，提升幅度高达+93.8个百分点，表明在监管领域，轨迹级别的评估至关重要。

Original abstract: LLM-based multi-agent systems are increasingly deployed for payment workflows, yet prevailing metrics, Task Success Rate (TSR) and Agent Handoff F1-Score (HF1), capture only final outcomes or unordered routing decisions. We introduce the Agentic Success Rate (ASR), a trajectory-fidelity metric that compares observed and expected agent execution sequences at the transition level, decomposing performance into Transition Recall and Transition Precision. Applied to the Hierarchical Multi-Agent System for Payments (HMASP) across 18 LLMs and 90,000 task instances, ASR reveals that 10 of 18 models systematically skip a confirmation checkpoint during payment checkout, a deviation invisible to both TSR and HF1, while 8 models enforce the checkpoint perfectly. Notably, GPT-4.1 exhibits hidden workflow shortcuts despite achieving perfect TSR and HF1, while GPT-5.2 achieves perfect ASR. Prompt refinements and deterministic routing guards guided by ASR diagnostics yield substantial TSR improvements, with gains up to +93.8 percentage points for previously struggling models, demonstrating that trajectory-level evaluation is essential in regulated domains.

### [71] [ReasonSTL: Bridging Natural Language and Signal Temporal Logic via Tool-Augmented Process-Rewarded Learning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06483v2)
*Bowen Ye,Zhijian Li,Junyue Huang,Junkai Ma,Xiang Yin*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 工具增强学习框架将自然语言翻译为STL，涉及工具使用和过程奖励，对agent结构化推理有启发。

TL;DR: ReasonSTL是一个工具增强框架，利用本地开源语言模型将自然语言翻译为信号时序逻辑公式，通过分解推理过程、过程奖励训练和双语基准，实现低成本、保护隐私且性能优异的形式化规范生成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自然语言到STL的翻译因手动指定不可扩展、商业LLM API成本高且泄露隐私而面临挑战，亟需一种低成本、隐私保护的自动方法。

Method: ReasonSTL框架将翻译分解为显式推理、工具调用和公式构建三阶段，并引入过程奖励训练监督工具使用轨迹和最终公式；同时构建了基于真实信号的双语基准STL-Bench。

Result: 4B参数模型经ReasonSTL训练后，在自动评估和人工评估中均达到最先进性能。

Conclusion: ReasonSTL为形式化规范起草提供了透明、低成本且保护隐私的替代方案，展示了本地小模型的巨大潜力。

中文摘要：信号时序逻辑（STL）是一种表达力丰富的形式化语言，用于指定实值、实时信号上的时空需求。它已广泛用于自主系统和信息物理系统的验证与综合。然而，在实践中，用户通常用自然语言而非结构化的STL公式表达需求，这使得自然语言到STL的翻译成为关键但具有挑战性的任务。手动指定需要时序逻辑专业知识且无法扩展，而使用商业大语言模型API带来大量令牌成本，并可能将敏感系统需求暴露给第三方服务，引发工业部署的隐私问题。为应对这些挑战，我们提出ReasonSTL，一个工具增强的框架，适配本地开源语言模型进行自然语言到STL的生成。ReasonSTL将翻译过程分解为显式推理、确定性工具调用和结构化公式构建。我们进一步引入过程奖励训练来监督工具使用轨迹和最终公式，并推出STL-Bench，一个基于真实世界信号的双语、计算感知基准。实验表明，使用ReasonSTL训练的4B模型在自动评估和人工评估中均达到最先进性能，证明ReasonSTL为形式化规范起草提供了透明、低成本且保护隐私的替代方案。

Original abstract: Signal Temporal Logic (STL) is an expressive formal language for specifying spatio-temporal requirements over real-valued, real-time signals. It has been widely used for the verification and synthesis of autonomous systems and cyber-physical systems. In practice, however, users often express their requirements in natural language rather than in structured STL formulas, making natural-language-to-STL translation a critical yet challenging task. Manual specification requires temporal-logic expertise and cannot scale, while prompting commercial LLM APIs incurs substantial token costs and may expose sensitive system requirements to third-party services, raising privacy concerns for industrial deployment. To address these challenges, we present \textsc{ReasonSTL}, a tool-augmented framework that adapts local open-source language models for natural-language-to-STL generation. \textsc{ReasonSTL} decomposes the translation process into explicit reasoning, deterministic tool calls, and structured formula construction. We further introduce process-rewarded training to supervise both tool-use trajectories and final formulas, together with \textsc{STL-Bench}, a bilingual, computation-aware benchmark grounded in real-world signals. Experiments show that a 4B model trained with \textsc{ReasonSTL} achieves state-of-the-art performance in both automatic metrics and human evaluations, demonstrating that \textsc{ReasonSTL} provides a transparent, low-cost, and privacy-preserving alternative for formal specification drafting.

### [72] [Instrumental Choices: Measuring the Propensity of LLM Agents to Pursue Instrumental Behaviors](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06490v1)
*Jonas Wiedermann-Möller,Leonard Dung,Maksym Andriushchenko*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 测量LLM agent工具性行为倾向，属于agent安全与评估通用方法，对agent可靠性研究有启发。

TL;DR: 提出一个基准测试来测量终端代理的工具性趋同行为，在低风险环境中评估了10个模型，发现IC行为罕见但系统性地出现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究AI系统是否会在某些情况下选择违反人类指令以追求更符合自身目标的行为，特别是工具性趋同行为如自我保存，这对理解高级AI风险至关重要。

Method: 设计了一个包含7个操作任务和8个变体的基准测试，每个任务有官方流程和政策违规捷径，通过控制监控、指令清晰度等变量，使用确定性评分器和轨迹审查评估了10个模型共1680个样本。

Result: IC率为5.1%（86/1680），行为集中：两个Gemini模型占66.3%，三个任务占84.9%；任务成功必需IC时调整后IC率增加15.7个百分点，其他因素影响不显著。

Conclusion: 在现实低推动环境中，大多数前沿AI模型会罕见但系统地表现出工具性趋同行为，且能够稳健测量这种危险行为倾向。

中文摘要：人工智能系统在许多领域已经变得能够执行越来越危险的行为。这引发了一个问题：模型有时是否会选择违反人类指令，以便执行对某些目标更有用的行为？我们引入了一个基准测试，用于测量终端型代理中工具性趋同（IC）行为的倾向。这种行为（如自我保存）被认为在高度能力AI代理的风险中扮演关键角色。我们的基准测试是现实且低风险的，这有助于减少评估意识和角色扮演混淆。该套件包含七个操作任务，每个任务都有一个官方工作流程和一个违反政策的捷径。一个八变体的共享框架变化了监控、指令清晰度、利害关系、许可、工具性效用和阻止诚实路径，以支持对驱动IC行为的因素的推断。我们使用确定性环境状态评分器评估了十个模型，共1680个样本，并采用轨迹审查进行审计和裁决。最终的IC率为1680个样本中的86个（5.1%）。IC行为集中而非均匀：两个Gemini模型占IC案例的66.3%，三个任务占84.9%。IC行为对任务成功不可或缺的条件导致调整后IC率的最大增加（+15.7个百分点），而强调任务成功至关重要或某些框架选择不会产生可比效果。我们的发现表明，在现实、低推动的环境中，大多数测试模型会罕见但系统地引发IC行为。我们得出结论，在当前前沿AI代理中，稳健地测量危险行为倾向是可行的。

Original abstract: AI systems have become increasingly capable of dangerous behaviours in many domains. This raises the question: Do models sometimes choose to violate human instructions in order to perform behaviour that is more useful for certain goals? We introduce a benchmark for measuring model propensity for instrumental convergence (IC) behaviour in terminal-based agents. This is behaviour such as self-preservation that has been hypothesised to play a key role in risks from highly capable AI agents. Our benchmark is realistic and low-stakes which serves to reduce evaluation-awareness and roleplay confounds. The suite contains seven operational tasks, each with an official workflow and a policy-violating shortcut. An eight-variant shared framework varies monitoring, instruction clarity, stakes, permission, instrumental usefulness and blocked honest paths to support inferences regarding the factors driving IC behaviour. We evaluated ten models using deterministic environment-state scorers over 1,680 samples, with trace review employed for audit and adjudication purposes. The final IC rate is 86 out of 1,680 samples (5.1%). IC behaviour is concentrated rather than uniform: two Gemini models account for 66.3% of IC cases and three tasks account for 84.9%. Conditions in which IC behaviour is indispensable for task success result in the greatest increase in the adjusted IC rate (+15.7 percentage points), whereas emphasising that task success is critical or certain framing choices do not produce comparable effects. Our findings indicate that realistic, low-nudge environments elicit IC behaviour rarely but systematically in most tested models. We conclude that it is feasible to robustly measure tendencies for dangerous behaviour in current frontier AI agents.

### [73] [Process Matters more than Output for Distinguishing Humans from Machines](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06524v2)
*Milena Rmus,Mathew D. Hardy,Thomas L. Griffiths,Mayank Agrawal*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 通过认知过程特征区分人类与机器，提出agent评估新视角，对agent设计有启发。

TL;DR: 提出CogCAPTCHA30认知任务集，证明过程级特征比性能指标更能区分人类与AI，并比较多种微调方法，发现过程级监督可改善行为模仿但依赖任务特定表示。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决人机区分难题，现有方法聚焦输出相似性，但认知科学认为过程更重要，因此探索过程级特征是否更可靠。

Method: 构建30个认知任务（CogCAPTCHA30），提取过程级特征，比较多种AI代理（前沿模型、微调模型等）及不同微调策略（A-SFT和P-SFT）。

Result: 过程特征分类器AUC=0.88，优于性能指标；过程级监督（P-SFT）改善行为模仿，但跨任务泛化有限。

Conclusion: 过程级监督可提升机器类人行为，但需任务特定过程表示，过程规范是实现类人认知的关键瓶颈。

中文摘要：随着大型语言模型和自主代理部署于在线环境，可靠的人机区分变得日益重要。现有方法遵循艾伦·图灵提出的以输出作为智能标准的思想，评估系统是否能产生与人类难以区分的行为或回应。认知科学提供了另一种视角：评估行为产生的过程。为了测试认知过程是否能可靠区分人类与机器，我们引入了CogCAPTCHA30，这是一套包含30个认知任务的测试集，旨在即使任务表现匹配时也能引出具有诊断性的过程级特征。在整个测试集中，过程级特征比单纯的表现指标提供更强的区分信号，即使在输出匹配条件下也能可靠区分人类与代理（平均过程特征分类器AUC = 0.88）。为了评估代理过程差异，我们比较了现成的前沿代理（Claude Sonnet 4.5、GPT-5、Gemini 2.5 Pro）、Centaur（基于1070万个人类决策微调的语言模型），以及两种应用于Qwen2.5-1.5B-Instruct的任务特定微调方法：动作级监督微调（A-SFT）和过程级微调（P-SFT），后者直接优化过程特征。与现成代理相比，在人类决策上的大规模微调改善了类人任务过程，而任务特定的过程级监督进一步提升了行为模仿。然而，当监督过程目标无法自然跨任务泛化时，这种优势在跨任务迁移中减弱。显式过程级监督可以改善人类行为模仿，但前提是存在适当的任务特定过程表示，这凸显了过程规范是实现机器类人认知过程的瓶颈。

Original abstract: Reliable human-machine discrimination is becoming increasingly important as large language models and autonomous agents are deployed in online settings. Existing approaches evaluate whether a system can produce behavior or responses indistinguishable from those of a human, following the emphasis on outputs as a criterion for intelligence proposed by Alan Turing. Cognitive science offers an alternative perspective: evaluating the process by which behavior is produced. To test whether cognitive processes can reliably distinguish humans from machines, we introduce CogCAPTCHA30, a battery of 30 cognitive tasks designed to elicit diagnostic process-level features even when task performance is matched. Across the battery, process-level features provide stronger discriminative signal than performance metrics alone, reliably distinguishing humans from agents even under output matching (mean process-feature classifier AUC = 0.88). To evaluate agentic process differences, we compare off-the-shelf frontier agents (Claude Sonnet 4.5, GPT-5, Gemini 2.5 Pro), Centaur (a language model fine-tuned on 10.7M human decisions), and two task-specific fine-tuning approaches applied to Qwen2.5-1.5B-Instruct: action-level supervised fine-tuning (A-SFT) and process-level fine-tuning (P-SFT), which directly optimizes process features. Broad fine-tuning on human decisions improves human-like task processes relative to off-the-shelf agents, while task-specific process-level supervision further improves behavioral mimicry. However, this advantage diminishes under cross-task transfer when supervised process targets do not naturally generalize across tasks. Explicit process-level supervision can improve human behavioral mimicry, but only if appropriate task-specific process representations are available, highlighting process specification as a bottleneck for achieving human-like cognitive processes in machines.

</details>


### [74] [Market-Alignment Risk in Pricing Agents: Trace Diagnostics and Trace-Prior RL under Hidden Competitor State](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06529v1)
*Peiying Zhu,Sidi Chang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 定价agent中市场对齐风险与trace诊断方法，提出可迁移的agent失败模式修复框架。

TL;DR: 标准强化学习在部分可观测的收益管理场景中学会错误策略，而Trace-Prior RL通过分布先验和KL正则化修复了此问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究标量奖励在部分可观测系统中易被操纵，导致学习智能体学到错误行为（如过度降价）的现象。

Method: 提出Trace-Prior RL：从滞后市场轨迹学习分布先验，并用RevPAR奖励和KL散度惩罚训练随机定价策略。

Result: 修复后的策略在种子级不确定性内匹配竞争对手的RevPAR、入住率、ADR和价格分布，同时优化自身奖励。

Conclusion: 贡献在于提供可复现的失败与修复方案，并发现更高精确行动准确率可能恶化分布对齐。

中文摘要：结果指标可能认证错误的行为。我们在一个双酒店收益管理模拟器中研究这种失败，其中酒店A训练一个智能体对抗一个固定的基于规则的收益管理竞争对手酒店B。一个标准的学习智能体可以获得接近参考的每间可用客房收入（RevPAR），但未能学习市场化的收益管理：它销售过于激进，降价，或崩溃到模态价格区间。我们将此诊断为部分可观测性下的古德哈特式失败。酒店A无法观测竞争对手的剩余库存、预订曲线或定价规则，因此相同的酒店A可见状态映射到多个可能的酒店B价格。确定性基于价值的学习和确定性复制将这种未解决的模糊性压缩成捷径行为。我们引入了一个使用RevPAR、入住率、平均每日房价、全价格区间分布、L1/JS距离和种子级置信区间的轨迹级诊断协议。验证的修复方法是Trace-Prior RL：从滞后的市场轨迹中学习一个分布式的市场先验，然后用RevPAR奖励和对学到的先验的KL惩罚来训练一个随机定价策略。最终策略在种子级不确定性内匹配酒店B的RevPAR、入住率、ADR和价格分布，同时仍优化酒店A自身的奖励。我们认为这项贡献不是一个新的优化器，也不是酒店定价排行榜，而是一个可复现的失败与修复方案，适用于那些标量奖励容易被操纵且预期行为仅在轨迹中可见的智能体系统。一个关键发现是，当目标是分布性时，更高的精确行动准确率可能恶化聚合轨迹对齐。

Original abstract: Outcome metrics can certify the wrong behavior. We study this failure in a two-hotel revenue-management simulator where Hotel A trains an agent against a fixed rule-based revenue-management competitor, Hotel B. A standard learning agent can obtain near-reference revenue per available room (RevPAR) while failing to learn market-like yield management: it sells too aggressively, undercuts, or collapses to modal price buckets. We diagnose this as a Goodhart-style failure under partial observability. Hotel A cannot observe the competitor's remaining inventory, booking curve, or pricing rule, so the same Hotel A-visible state maps to multiple plausible Hotel B prices. Deterministic value-based RL and deterministic copying collapse this unresolved uncertainty into shortcut behavior. We introduce a trace-level diagnostic protocol using RevPAR, occupancy, ADR, full price-bucket distributions, L1/JS distances, and seed-level confidence intervals. The verified repair is Trace-Prior RL: learn a distributional market prior from lagged market traces, then train a stochastic pricing policy with a RevPAR reward and a KL penalty to the learned prior. The final policy matches Hotel B's RevPAR, occupancy, ADR, and price distribution within seed-level uncertainty, while still optimizing Hotel A's own reward. We argue that the contribution is not a new optimizer and not a hotel-pricing leaderboard, but a reproducible failure-and-repair recipe for agentic systems where scalar rewards are easy to game and the intended behavior is only visible in traces. A key finding is that higher exact action accuracy can worsen aggregate trace alignment when the target is distributional.

Original abstract: The web is complex, open-ended, and constantly changing, making it challenging to scale training data for visual web agents. Existing data collection attempts remain limited to offline trajectories for supervised fine-tuning or a handful of simulated environments for RL training, thus failing to capture web diversity. We propose Weblica (Web Replica), a framework for constructing reproducible and scalable web environments. Our framework leverages 1) HTTP-level caching to capture and replay stable visual states while preserving interactive behavior and 2) LLM-based environment synthesis grounded in real-world websites and core web navigation skills. Using this framework, we scale RL training to thousands of diverse environments and tasks. Our best model, Weblica-8B, outperforms open-weight baselines of similar size across multiple web navigation benchmarks while using fewer inference steps, scales favorably with additional test-time compute, and is competitive with API models.

### [76] [SkillOS: Learning Skill Curation for Self-Evolving Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06614v1)
*Siru Ouyang,Jun Yan,Yanfei Chen,Rujun Han,Zifeng Wang,Bhavana Dalvi Mishra,Rui Meng,Chun-Liang Li,Yizhu Jiao,Kaiwen Zha,Maohao Shen,Vishy Tirumalashetty,George Lee,Jiawei Han,Tomas Pfister,Chen-Yu Lee*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: SkillOS提出技能策展与自我进化agent，通用经验复用方法，直接可迁移至coding agent。

TL;DR: SkillOS通过经验驱动的强化学习训练可学习的技能策展器，使LLM智能体能够从过往交互中提炼复用技能，实现自我进化，在多项任务上优于基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM智能体在流式任务中无法从历史经验中学习，技能策展是关键瓶颈，而现有方法无法从间接延迟反馈中学习复杂长期策展策略。

Method: 提出SkillOS，包含冻结的执行器和可训练的策展器，通过复合奖励和基于任务依赖的分组任务流训练，让策展器从经验中更新SkillRepo。

Result: SkillOS在多轮和单轮任务上一致优于无记忆和强记忆基线，且策展器能泛化到不同执行器和任务域，技能使用更精准，技能文件结构更丰富。

Conclusion: SkillOS有效实现了智能体的自我进化，通过经验驱动学习技能策展，提升了效果和效率，并展示了泛化能力与技能结构化演化。

中文摘要：基于LLM的智能体越来越多地被用于处理流式任务，但它们通常仍然是无法从过往交互中学习的一次性问题解决者。从经验中提炼出的可复用技能为自我进化提供了天然基础，而高质量技能的策展则是关键瓶颈。现有方法要么依赖人工技能策展，要么规定启发式技能操作，要么训练短视的技能操作。然而，它们仍然难以从间接且延迟的反馈中学习复杂的长期策展策略。为应对这一挑战，我们提出了SkillOS，一种基于经验驱动的强化学习训练方案，用于自我进化智能体中的技能策展学习。SkillOS将一个冻结的、用于检索和应用技能的智能体执行器与一个可训练的、根据累积经验更新外部SkillRepo的技能策展器配对。为了提供策展的学习信号，我们设计了复合奖励，并基于技能相关的任务依赖关系在分组任务流上进行训练，其中早期的轨迹更新SkillRepo，后续的相关任务评估这些更新。在多轮智能体任务和单轮推理任务上，SkillOS在效果和效率上均一致优于无记忆和强记忆基线，并且学到的技能策展器能够泛化到不同的执行器主干和任务领域。进一步分析表明，学到的策展器会产生更具针对性的技能使用，而SkillRepo中的技能会随时间演变为更富结构化的Markdown文件，编码更高级的元技能。

Original abstract: LLM-based agents are increasingly deployed to handle streaming tasks, yet they often remain one-off problem solvers that fail to learn from past interactions. Reusable skills distilled from experience provide a natural substrate for self-evolution, where high-quality skill curation serves as the key bottleneck. Existing approaches either rely on manual skill curation, prescribe heuristic skill operations, or train for short-horizon skill operations. However, they still struggle to learn complex long-term curation policies from indirect and delayed feedback. To tackle this challenge, we propose SkillOS, an experience-driven RL training recipe for learning skill curation in self-evolving agents. SkillOS pairs a frozen agent executor that retrieves and applies skills with a trainable skill curator that updates an external SkillRepo from accumulated experience. To provide learning signals for curation, we design composite rewards and train on grouped task streams based on skill-relevant task dependencies, where earlier trajectories update the SkillRepo, and later related tasks evaluate these updates. Across multi-turn agentic tasks and single-turn reasoning tasks, SkillOS consistently outperforms memory-free and strong memory-based baselines in both effectiveness and efficiency, with the learned skill curator generalizing across different executor backbones and task domains. Further analyses show that the learned curator produces more targeted skill use, while the skills in SkillRepo evolve into more richly structured Markdown files that encode higher-level meta-skills over time.

### [77] [MASPO: Joint Prompt Optimization for LLM-based Multi-Agent Systems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06623v1)
*Zhexuan Wang,Xuebo Liu,Li Wang,Zifei Shan,Yutong Wang,Zhenxi Song,Min Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: MASPO提出多agent系统提示联合优化，通用方法可迁移至多agent coding场景。

TL;DR: MASPO通过联合评估和进化波束搜索，自动优化多智能体系统的提示，解决局部与全局目标不对齐问题，提升任务准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多智能体系统中，局部智能体目标与整体系统目标不对齐，导致联合优化提示困难。

Method: 提出联合评估机制，评估提示对后续智能体下游成功的贡献，并采用数据驱动的进化波束搜索优化提示空间。

Result: 在6个任务上平均准确率提升2.9%，优于现有方法。

Conclusion: MASPO有效提升了多智能体系统提示优化的性能，无需真实标签，具有广泛应用前景。

中文摘要：基于大语言模型（LLM）的多智能体系统（MAS）在解决复杂协作任务方面展现出潜力，其中智能体通常通过角色特定提示进行编排。尽管这些提示的质量至关重要，但在交互智能体之间联合优化提示仍然是一个重大挑战，主要原因是局部智能体目标与整体系统目标之间的不对齐。为解决此问题，我们引入了MASPO，一个旨在自动迭代优化整个系统提示的新框架。MASPO的一个核心创新是其联合评估机制，该机制不仅根据局部有效性评估提示，还根据其促进后续智能体下游成功的能力进行评估。这有效地弥合了局部交互与全局结果之间的差距，而无需依赖真实标签。此外，MASPO采用数据驱动的进化波束搜索来高效导航高维提示空间。在6个不同任务上的大量实证评估表明，MASPO始终优于最先进的提示优化方法，平均准确率提升2.9。我们在https://github.com/wangzx1219/MASPO发布代码。

Original abstract: Large language model (LLM)-based Multi-agent systems (MAS) have shown promise in tackling complex collaborative tasks, where agents are typically orchestrated via role-specific prompts. While the quality of these prompts is pivotal, jointly optimizing them across interacting agents remains a non-trivial challenge, primarily due to the misalignment between local agent objectives and holistic system goals. To address this, we introduce MASPO, a novel framework designed to automatically and iteratively refine prompts across the entire system. A core innovation of MASPO is its joint evaluation mechanism, which assesses prompts not merely by their local validity, but by their capacity to facilitate downstream success for successor agents. This effectively bridges the gap between local interactions and global outcomes without relying on ground-truth labels. Furthermore, MASPO employs a data-driven evolutionary beam search to efficiently navigate the high-dimensional prompt space. Extensive empirical evaluations across 6 diverse tasks demonstrate that MASPO consistently outperforms state-of-the-art prompt optimization methods, achieving an average accuracy improvement of 2.9. We release our code at https://github.com/wangzx1219/MASPO.

### [78] [Can RL Teach Long-Horizon Reasoning to LLMs? Expressiveness Is Key](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06638v3)
*Tianle Wang,Zhaoyang Wang,Guangchen Lan,Xinpeng Wei,Sipeng Zhang,Guanwen Qiu,Abulhair Saparov*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 研究RL训练LLM长程推理的scaling law，对agent规划能力提升有潜在启发。

TL;DR: 提出ScaleLogic框架，发现RL训练计算量随推理深度呈幂律增长，且逻辑表达力越高，缩放指数越大；下游任务表现受益于更复杂的训练设置，证明LLM长程推理不足可通过改进训练解决。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究缺乏控制变量环境来系统研究RL训练如何随推理难度扩展，且LLM在长程推理上的不足被质疑是架构固有缺陷。

Method: 设计ScaleLogic合成逻辑推理框架，独立控制推理深度和逻辑表达力（从简单蕴含到一阶逻辑），训练RL模型并测量计算量、性能等。

Result: 训练计算T与推理深度D满足幂律（R²>0.99），指数γ从1.04（简单逻辑）增至2.60（高表达力）；高表达力训练带来更大下游增益（+10.66分）和更高迁移效率；幂律对多种RL方法成立，课程训练提升效率。

Conclusion: LLM在长程推理上的不足并非架构固有问题，通过更丰富的训练数据和改进的RL训练方法（如课程学习）可以有效缓解。

中文摘要：强化学习（RL）已被应用于改进大语言模型（LLM）的推理能力，但训练如何随任务难度扩展的系统性研究因缺乏可控、可扩展的环境而受到阻碍。观察到的LLM在长程推理中的不足引发了一种观点，即这些不足是自回归Transformer架构所固有的。为了解决这个问题，我们引入了ScaleLogic，一个合成逻辑推理框架，它能够独立控制两个难度轴：所需证明规划的深度（即视界）和底层逻辑的表达力。我们提出的框架支持广泛的逻辑：从简单的蕴含逻辑（“如果-则”）到更具表达力的一阶推理，包括合取（“与”）、析取（“或”）、否定（“非”）和全称量化（“对所有”）。使用该框架，我们表明RL训练计算量T与推理深度D遵循幂律关系（T ∝ D^γ，R² > 0.99），并且缩放指数γ随逻辑表达力单调增加，从1.04到2.60。在下游数学和通用推理基准上，更具表达力的训练设置相比不具表达力的设置产生了更大的性能提升（高达+10.66分）和更高计算效率的迁移，这表明模型被训练的内容（而不仅仅是训练多少）决定了下游迁移。我们进一步表明，幂律关系在多种RL方法中成立，并且基于课程的训练显著提高了缩放效率。更广泛地说，我们的结果表明，LLM在长程推理中的不足并非底层架构所固有的，可以通过改进训练方法和数据来解决。

Original abstract: Reinforcement learning (RL) has been applied to improve large language model (LLM) reasoning, yet the systematic study of how training scales with task difficulty has been hampered by the lack of controlled, scalable environments. Observed LLM shortcomings in long-horizon reasoning have raised the prospect that they are fundamental to the autoregressive transformer architecture. To address this, we introduce ScaleLogic, a synthetic logical reasoning framework that offers independent control over two axes of difficulty: the depth of the required proof planning (i.e., the horizon) and the expressiveness of the underlying logic. Our proposed framework supports a wide range of logics: from simple implication-only logic ("if-then") towards more expressive first-order reasoning with conjunction ("and"), disjunction ("or"), negation ("not"), and universal quantification ("for all"). Using this framework, we show that the RL training compute $T$ follows a power law with respect to reasoning depth $D$ ($T \propto D^γ$, $R^{2} > 0.99$), and that the scaling exponent $γ$ increases monotonically with logical expressiveness, from $1.04$ to $2.60$. On downstream mathematics and general reasoning benchmarks, more expressive training settings yield both larger performance gains (up to $+10.66$ points) and more compute-efficient transfer compared to less expressive settings, demonstrating that what a model is trained on, not just how much it is trained, shapes downstream transfer. We further show that the power-law relationship holds across multiple RL methods, and curriculum-based training substantially improves scaling efficiency. More broadly, our results demonstrate that LLM shortcomings in long-horizon reasoning are not fundamental to the underlying architecture, and can be addressed by improved training methodology and data.

</details>

By providing an asynchronous, stateful workspace that manages uncertainty, refines user intent, tracks failed hypotheses, and outputs native mathematical artifacts, the system mirrors human collaborative workflows. In early tests, the AI co-mathematician helped researchers solve open problems, identify new research directions, and uncover overlooked literature references. ### [80] [When Does Critique Improve AI-Assisted Theoretical Physics? SCALAR: Structured Critic--Actor Loop for Agentic Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06772v1)
*Vasilis Niarchos,Constantinos Papageorgakis,Alexander G. Stapleton,Sokratis Trifinopoulos*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: Actor-Critic-Judge多轮对话框架，可迁移至代码优化agent的反思与改进机制

TL;DR: 本研究通过SCALAR流水线探索了大型语言模型在物理学推理中研究者与代理互动的影响，发现多轮对话、行动者-评论者配对和反馈策略对结果有显著且依赖性的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着LLM在研究级物理推理中展现出潜力以及代理式AI的普及，研究人员与代理之间的互动如何影响结果成为一个实际且重要的问题。

Method: 使用SCALAR（结构化评论-行动者循环）流水线，包含行动者（提出解决方案）、评论者（提供迭代反馈）和独立的评审者（根据参考答案评估），应用于量子场论和弦理论问题，并变化行动者角色、反馈策略及模型规模。

Result: 多轮对话优于单次尝试；改进机制和提示选择价值依赖于行动者-评论者配对；扩大模型规模改善简单问题但未解决最难瓶颈；反馈策略在不对称配对中效果显著，建设性反馈提高得分，而在同家族配对中策略影响较弱。

Conclusion: SCALAR提供了一个受控测试平台，用于评估不同互动结构对AI驱动科学发现的帮助或阻碍。

中文摘要：随着大型语言模型（LLM）在研究级物理推理任务中展现出越来越大的潜力，且代理式AI变得越来越普遍，一个实际问题出现了：研究人员与代理之间的互动如何影响结果？我们使用SCALAR（结构化评论-行动者循环，用于AI推理）来研究这一问题，这是一个应用于量子场论和弦理论问题的行动者-评论者-评审者流水线。行动者提出解决方案，评论者提供迭代反馈，独立的评审者根据参考答案对对话记录进行评估。我们变化了行动者角色、评论者反馈策略以及行动者模型系列和规模。多轮对话在整体上优于单次尝试，但改进的机制以及不同提示选择的价值强烈依赖于行动者-评论者配对。在一个模型系列内增加规模（例如，从8B参数的DeepSeek-R1变体到DeepSeek-R1 70B）改善了一些较简单问题的行为，但未能消除我们观察到的最难瓶颈。评论者反馈策略在不对称的行动者-评论者设置中最为重要（例如，由更强的Sonnet评论者指导的轻量级Haiku行动者），其中建设性反馈提高了平均得分结果。在相同家族的行动者-评论者设置中，策略效应较弱：宽松反馈有时更受青睐，而严格和对抗性反馈则没有益处。总体而言，SCALAR提供了一个受控的测试平台，用于评估哪些互动结构有助于或阻碍AI驱动的科学发现。

Original abstract: As large language models (LLMs) show increasing promise on research-level physics reasoning tasks and agentic AI becomes more common, a practical question emerges: How does the interaction between researchers and agents affect the results? We study this using SCALAR (Structured Critic--Actor Loop for AI Reasoning), an Actor--Critic--Judge pipeline applied to quantum field theory and string theory problems. The Actor proposes solutions, the Critic provides iterative feedback, and an independent Judge evaluates the transcript against reference solutions. We vary the Actor persona, the Critic feedback strategy, and the Actor model family and scale. Multi-turn dialogue improves over single-shot attempts throughout, but both the mechanism of improvement and the value of different prompting choices depend strongly on the Actor--Critic pairing. Increasing the scale within one model family (e.g. from the 8B-parameter DeepSeek-R1 variant to DeepSeek-R1 70B) improves some easier-problem behavior, but does not remove the hardest bottleneck we observe. Critic feedback strategy matters most clearly in the asymmetric Actor--Critic setting (e.g., a lightweight Haiku Actor guided by a stronger Sonnet Critic), where constructive feedback improves mean-score outcomes. In same-family Actor--Critic settings, strategy effects are weaker: lenient feedback is sometimes favored, while strict and adversarial feedback are not beneficial. Taken together, SCALAR provides a controlled testbed for evaluating which interaction structures help or hinder AI-driven scientific discovery.

### [81] [Towards Security-Auditable LLM Agents: A Unified Graph Representation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06812v1)
*Chaofan Li,Lyuye Zhang,Jintao Zhai,Siyue Feng,Xichun Yang,Huahao Wang,Shihan Dou,Yu Ji,Yutao Hu,Yueming Wu,Yang Liu,Deqing Zou*

Selection reason: 提出agent安全审计的统一图表示，对agent可解释性与安全性研究有通用价值

TL;DR: 提出Agent-BOM，一种统一的结构表示，用于智能体系统安全审计，通过将静态能力与动态状态分离并构建可查询的审计路径，能有效重建隐蔽攻击链。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有表示机制（静态SBOM、运行时日志）提供碎片化证据，无法捕获认知状态演化、能力绑定、内存污染和跨智能体风险传播，导致安全审计困难。

Method: 将智能体系统建模为层次化属性有向图，分离静态能力基础（模型、工具、长期记忆）和动态运行时语义状态（目标、推理轨迹、动作），通过语义边和安全属性连接，并基于OWASP Agentic Top 10开发图查询路径级风险评估。

Result: 在真实世界攻击场景中，Agent-BOM能重建跨会话内存中毒、工具滥用、供应链劫持、代码执行、多智能体生态系统劫持及权限滥用等隐蔽攻击链。

Conclusion: Agent-BOM为复杂智能体生态系统中的根本原因分析和安全裁决提供了统一且可审计的基础。

中文摘要：基于LLM的智能体系统正在迅速发展，通过动态工具调用、有状态记忆管理和多智能体协作来执行复杂的自主任务。然而，这种语义驱动的执行范式在低层物理事件和高层执行意图之间造成了严重的语义鸿沟，使得事后安全审计从根本上变得困难。现有的表示机制，包括静态SBOM和运行时日志，只提供碎片化的证据，无法捕获认知状态演化、能力绑定、持久内存污染以及跨交互智能体的级联风险传播。为了弥合这一差距，我们提出了Agent-BOM，一种用于智能体安全审计的统一结构表示。Agent-BOM将智能体系统建模为一个层次化的属性有向图，将静态能力基础（如模型、工具和长期记忆）与动态运行时语义状态（如目标、推理轨迹和动作）分离。这些层通过语义边和安全属性连接，将碎片化的执行轨迹转换为可查询的审计路径。基于Agent-BOM，我们开发了一种基于图查询的路径级风险评估范式，并使用OWASP Agentic Top 10进行了实例化。我们进一步在OpenClaw环境中实现了一个审计插件，以从实时执行中构建Agent-BOM。对代表性真实世界智能体攻击场景的评估表明，Agent-BOM可以重建隐蔽攻击链，包括跨会话内存中毒和工具滥用、能力供应链劫持和意外代码执行、多智能体生态系统劫持以及权限和信任滥用。这些结果表明，Agent-BOM为复杂智能体生态系统中的根本原因分析和安全裁决提供了统一且可审计的基础。

Original abstract: LLM-based agentic systems are rapidly evolving to perform complex autonomous tasks through dynamic tool invocation, stateful memory management, and multi-agent collaboration. However, this semantics-driven execution paradigm creates a severe semantic gap between low-level physical events and high-level execution intent, making post-hoc security auditing fundamentally difficult. Existing representation mechanisms, including static SBOMs and runtime logs, provide only fragmented evidence and fail to capture cognitive-state evolution, capability bindings, persistent memory contamination, and cascading risk propagation across interacting agents. To bridge this gap, we propose Agent-BOM, a unified structural representation for agent security auditing. Agent-BOM models an agentic system as a hierarchical attributed directed graph that separates static capability bases, such as models, tools, and long-term memory, from dynamic runtime semantic states, such as goals, reasoning trajectories, and actions. These layers are connected through semantic edges and security attributes, transforming fragmented execution traces into queryable audit paths. Building on Agent-BOM, we develop a graph-query-based paradigm for path-level risk assessment and instantiate it with the OWASP Agentic Top 10. We further implement an auditing plugin in the OpenClaw environment to construct Agent-BOM from live executions. Evaluation on representative real-world agentic attack scenarios shows that Agent-BOM can reconstruct stealthy attack chains, including cross-session memory poisoning and tool misuse, capability supply-chain hijacking and unexpected code execution, multi-agent ecosystem hijacking, and privilege and trust abuse. These results demonstrate that Agent-BOM provides a unified and auditable foundation for root-cause analysis and security adjudication in complex agentic ecosystems.

### [82] [Randomness is sometimes necessary for coordination](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06825v1)
*Rohan Patil,Jai Malegaonkar,Henrik I. Christensen*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 多agent协调中随机性角色，可迁移至多agent协作或代码优化中的探索策略

TL;DR: 提出了Diamond Attention，通过每个智能体采样随机数实现角色分化和零样本迁移，在对称任务上达到1.0成功率，优于确定性基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 完全参数共享在对称观测下导致所有智能体输出相同动作，无法实现角色分化，需要引入结构化随机性来解决对称性破缺问题。

Method: 提出Diamond Attention，每个智能体每时间步采样一个标量随机数产生瞬态排序，在注意力中屏蔽低排名智能体，实现随机比特协调协议。

Result: 在XOR游戏上达到1.0成功率（基线0.5）；N=4训练零样本泛化到N∈[2,8]；SMACLite零样本迁移；结构化随机性比dropout有效（0%胜率对比高胜率）。

Conclusion: 结构化随机性（而非噪声）是实现多智能体角色分化和零样本泛化的关键，Diamond Attention是一种有效的协议空间方法。

中文摘要：完全参数共享在面向同质智能体的合作式多智能体强化学习（MARL）中是标准做法。然而，在置换对称的观测下，共享的确定性策略会对每个智能体输出相同的动作分布，使得角色分化不可能实现。理论上，这一问题可以通过在匿名全同处理器间引入对称性破缺来解决，这需要随机性。我们提出了Diamond Attention，这是一种交叉注意力架构，其中每个智能体每个时间步采样一个标量随机数，从而引发一个瞬时的排序，该排序会屏蔽来自智能体到智能体注意力中的低排名同伴，同时使任务注意力完全不受遮蔽。这在一个广播轮次中实现了一个随机比特协调协议，并且基于集合的注意力使得模型能够零样本部署到不同规模的团队中。我们在三种隔离了结构化随机性何时重要的机制上进行了评估。在完全对称的XOR游戏中，我们的方法达到了1.0的成功率，而所有确定性基线都停滞在0.5附近。在控制协调任务上，在N=4上训练的策略零样本泛化到N∈[2,8]。在SMACLite跨场景迁移中，我们实现了零样本迁移，而标准基线由于结构限制无法迁移。此外，将结构化掩码替换为基于标准dropout的随机性会导致0%的胜率，这证实了协议空间结构，而非随机噪声，是起作用的成分。https://anonymous.4open.science/r/randomness-137A/

Original abstract: Full parameter sharing is standard in cooperative multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) for homogeneous agents. Under permutation-symmetric observations, however, a shared deterministic policy outputs identical action distributions for every agent, making role differentiation impossible. This failure can theoretically be resolved using symmetry breaking among anonymous identical processors, which requires randomness. We propose Diamond Attention, a cross-attention architecture in which each agent samples a scalar random number per timestep, inducing a transient rank ordering that masks lower-ranked peers from agent-to-agent attention while leaving task attention fully unmasked. This realizes a random-bit coordination protocol in a single broadcast round, and the set-based attention enables zero-shot deployment to teams of different sizes. We evaluate across three regimes that isolate when structured randomness matters. On the perfectly symmetric XOR game, our method achieves $1.0$ success while all deterministic baselines plateau near $0.5$. On control coordination tasks, a policy trained on $N=4$ generalizes zero-shot to $N \in [2,8]$. On SMACLite cross-scenario transfer, we achieve zero-shot transfer where standard baselines cannot transfer due to structural limitations. Furthermore, replacing the structured mask with standard dropout-based randomness results in a 0\% win rate, confirming that protocol-space structure, not stochastic noise, is the operative ingredient. https://anonymous.4open.science/r/randomness-137A/

### [83] [Extracting Search Trees from LLM Reasoning Traces Reveals Myopic Planning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06840v5)
*Sixing Chen,Ji-An Li,Saner Cakir,Sinan Akcali,Kayla Lee,Marcelo G. Mattar*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 分析LLM规划搜索树，揭示浅层规划，对agent规划机制有启发。

TL;DR: LLM在四子棋中的规划表现为浅层搜索，性能由广度而非深度驱动，与人类依赖深度搜索不同。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前对LLM推理轨迹中的斟酌是否构成真正规划、其结构及驱动因素尚不清楚。

Method: 从LLM玩四子棋的思维链轨迹中提取搜索树，拟合计算模型，并进行因果干预（选择性修剪CoT段落）。

Result: LLM搜索深度浅于人类；性能由搜索广度预测而非深度；移动选择由浅层节点主导，忽略深层节点。

Conclusion: LLM与人类规划存在关键差异：LLM不基于深度前瞻行动，而人类依赖深度搜索；这为对齐两者提供了方向。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM），尤其是推理模型，会生成扩展的思维链（CoT）推理，其中通常包含对未来结果的明确斟酌。然而，这种斟酌是否构成真正的规划、其结构如何以及其哪些方面驱动性能仍不清楚。在这项工作中，我们引入了一种新方法，通过从四子棋棋盘游戏中提取并量化推理轨迹中的搜索树来表征LLM规划。通过在提取的搜索树上拟合计算模型，我们描述了规划的结构及其如何影响移动决策。我们发现LLM的搜索比人类更浅，并且性能由搜索广度而非深度预测。最引人注目的是，尽管LLM在其轨迹中展开了深层节点，但其移动选择最好由一个忽略这些节点的短视模型来解释。一项选择性地修剪CoT段落的因果干预研究进一步表明，移动选择主要由浅层节点而非深层节点驱动。这些模式与人类规划形成对比——人类规划中性能主要由深度搜索驱动。总之，我们的发现揭示了LLM与人类规划之间的关键差异：虽然人类专业知识由更深的搜索驱动，但LLM并不基于深度前瞻行动。这种分离为调整LLM与人类规划提供了有针对性的指导。更广泛地说，我们的框架提供了一种可推广的方法，用于跨战略领域解释LLM规划的结构。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs), especially reasoning models, generate extended chain-of-thought (CoT) reasoning that often contains explicit deliberation over future outcomes. Yet whether this deliberation constitutes genuine planning, how it is structured, and what aspects of it drive performance remain poorly understood. In this work, we introduce a new method to characterize LLM planning by extracting and quantifying search trees from reasoning traces in the four-in-a-row board game. By fitting computational models on the extracted search trees, we characterize how plans are structured and how they influence move decisions. We find that LLMs' search is shallower than humans', and that performance is predicted by search breadth rather than depth. Most strikingly, although LLMs expand deep nodes in their traces, their move choices are best explained by a myopic model that ignores those nodes entirely. A causal intervention study where we selectively prune CoT paragraphs further suggests that move selection is driven predominantly by shallow rather than deep nodes. These patterns contrast with human planning, where performance is driven primarily by deep search. Together, our findings reveal a key difference between LLM and human planning: while human expertise is driven by deeper search, LLMs do not act on deep lookahead. This dissociation offers targeted guidance for aligning LLM and human planning. More broadly, our framework provides a generalizable approach for interpreting the structure of LLM planning across strategic domains.

### [84] [AGWM: Affordance-Grounded World Models for Environments with Compositional Prerequisites](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06841v1)
*Qinshi Zhang,Weipeng Deng,Zhihan Jiang,Jiaming Qu,Qianren Li,Weitao Xu,Ray LC*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准世界模型忽略动作前提条件，导致在多步预测中无法判断动作可执行性，误差累积。

Method: 提出AGWM，学习抽象可执行性结构（前提依赖DAG）显式跟踪动态可执行性。

Result: 在游戏模拟环境中，AGWM实现更低的多步预测误差、更好的泛化能力和可解释性。

Conclusion: AGWM有效解决了标准世界模型忽略动作前提导致的多步预测错误问题。

中文摘要：在基于模型的强化学习中，智能体通过模拟基于世界模型预测的轨迹来学习行为。标准世界模型通常学习一个静态的转移函数，将状态和动作映射到下一个状态，当某个动作和结果在训练数据中频繁共现时，模型倾向于将此相关性内化为一般因果规则，而忽略动作前提条件。然而，在交互环境中，智能体动作可以重塑未来的可执行空间。在每个时间步，一个动作可能只有在满足其前提条件后才变得可执行，或者当其前提条件被破坏时变得不可执行。我们将此类事件称为结构变化事件（SC事件）。因此，传统世界模型常常无法判断给定动作在当前状态下是否可执行，尤其是在多步预测中。每个想象步骤都基于不正确的可执行状态，因此预测误差在展开过程中累积。在本文中，我们提出AGWM（基于可执行性的世界模型），它学习一个抽象的可执行性结构，表示为前提依赖关系的有向无环图，以显式跟踪动作的动态可执行性。在基于游戏的模拟环境中的实验表明，我们的方法有效，实现了更低的多步预测误差、更好的对新配置的泛化能力以及改进的可解释性。

Original abstract: In model-based learning, the agent learns behaviors by simulating trajectories based on world model predictions. Standard world models typically learn a stationary transition function that maps states and actions to next states, when an action and an outcome frequently co-occur in training data, the model tends to internalize this correlation as a general causal rule while ignoring action preconditions. In interactive environments, however, agent actions can reshape the future affordance space. At each timestep, an action may becomes executable only after its prerequisites are met, or non-executable when they are destroyed. We term such events structure-changing events (SC events). As a result, a conventional world model often fails to determine whether a given action is executable in the current state, especially in multi-step predictions. Each imagined step is conditioned on an incorrect affordance state, and therefore the prediction error compounds over the rollout horizon. In this paper, we propose AGWM (Affordance-Grounded World Model), which learns an abstract affordance structure represented as a DAG of prerequisite dependencies to explicitly track the dynamic executability of actions. Experiments on game-based simulated environments demonstrate the effectiveness of our method by achieving lower multi-step prediction error, better generalization to novel configurations, and improved interpretability.

</details>


### [85] [Agentick: A Unified Benchmark for General Sequential Decision-Making Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06869v2)
*Roger Creus Castanyer,Pablo Samuel Castro,Glen Berseth*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 统一通用agent基准，直接支撑agent研究，含多项比较。

TL;DR: 提出Agentick基准，支持多模态、多难度、多能力的序列决策任务评估，发现无单一方法主导，ASCII观察优于自然语言，推理框架显著提升LLM性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准无法公平比较从RL到基础模型的各类代理，缺乏统一评估框架。

Method: 构建37个程序化生成任务，覆盖6种能力、4种难度、5种观察模态，提供编码API、参考策略、SFT数据集和组合框架。

Result: 评估27种配置、9万+回合，GPT-5 mini整体最优，PPO在规划和多代理任务领先，推理框架提升3-10倍，ASCII优于自然语言。

Conclusion: 所有代理范式仍有巨大改进空间，Agentick为通用自主代理研究和RL后训练提供了基础设施。

中文摘要：AI代理研究涵盖广泛的范围：从从头学习的RL代理到利用预训练知识的基础模型代理，然而没有一个统一的基准能够公平地比较这些方法。我们提出Agentick，一个针对序列决策代理的基准，旨在共同基础上评估RL、LLM、VLM、混合和人类代理，并推动序列决策基本挑战的研究。Agentick提供37个程序化生成的任务，涵盖六个能力类别、四个难度级别和五种观察模态，全部通过一个兼容Gymnasium的接口暴露。该基准附带一个编码API、所有任务的oracle参考策略、预构建的SFT数据集、可组合的代理框架和一个实时排行榜。对27种配置和超过90,000个回合的评估显示，没有单一方法占据主导地位：GPT-5 mini以0.309的oracle归一化分数整体领先，而PPO在规划和多代理任务中占主导地位；推理框架将LLM性能提升了3-10倍；ASCII观察始终优于自然语言。这些发现凸显了所有代理范式仍有巨大的改进空间。Agentick的能力分解、多模态设计提供了推动通用自主代理进步所需的实证基础设施，既作为评估框架，也作为在真正序列环境中对基础模型进行RL后训练的训练场。

Original abstract: AI agent research spans a wide spectrum: from RL agents that learn from scratch to foundation model agents that leverage pre-trained knowledge, yet no unified benchmark enables fair comparison across these approaches. We present Agentick, a benchmark for sequential decision-making agents designed to evaluate RL, LLM, VLM, hybrid, and human agents on common ground and to power research on the fundamental challenges of sequential decision-making. Agentick provides 37 procedurally generated tasks across six capability categories, four difficulty levels, and five observation modalities, all exposed through a single Gymnasium-compatible interface. The benchmark ships with a Coding API, oracle reference policies for all tasks, pre-built SFT datasets, a composable agent harness, and a live leaderboard. An evaluation spanning 27 configurations and over 90,000 episodes reveals that no single approach dominates: GPT-5 mini leads overall at 0.309 oracle-normalized score while PPO dominates planning and multi-agent tasks; the reasoning harness multiplies LLM performance by 3-10x; and ASCII observations consistently outperform natural language. These findings highlight the substantial room for improvement that remains across all agent paradigms. Agentick's capability-decomposed, multi-modal design provides the empirical infrastructure needed to drive progress toward general autonomous agents, both as an evaluation framework and as a training ground for RL post-training of foundation models in truly sequential environments.

### [86] [How Well Do LLMs Perform on the Simplest Long-Chain Reasoning Tasks: An Empirical Study on the Equivalence Class Problem](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06882v1)
*Chun Zheng,Lianlong Wu,Bingqian Li,Lvting Liu,Yi Zhou*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: LLM长链推理评估，对agent推理能力研究有启发。

TL;DR: 本文评估了大型语言模型在等价类问题上的推理能力，发现非推理模型完全失败，推理模型表现更好但仍无法完全解决，且最难实例分别对应相变点和最大直径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 评估LLMs在长链推理任务上的性能，尤其是最简单但长链的等价类问题，以理解其推理能力的局限性。

Method: 使用多种推理和非推理LLMs，在随机生成的等价关系实例上进行实验，控制变量数量、连通概率、提示等因素。

Result: 非推理LLMs无法解决ECP，推理模型显著更好但无法完全解决；非推理模型最难实例对应于相变点，推理模型最难实例对应于最大直径。

Conclusion: 当前LLMs在长链推理任务上存在困难，尤其是非推理模型，而推理模型虽有提升但仍需改进；问题难度与非推理模型的混沌性和推理模型的推理复杂度相关。

中文摘要：近年来，大型语言模型（LLMs）取得了巨大进步。然而，目前尚不清楚LLMs在推理任务上的表现如何，尤其是长链推理任务。在本文中，我们评估了LLMs在最简单但长链的推理任务——等价类问题（ECP）上的性能，即给定一组随机生成的等价关系，判断两个变量是否相等。我们考虑了多种推理和非推理的代表性LLMs，涵盖了不同变量数量、连通概率、提示等因素的大量问题实例。实验结果表明，非推理LLMs无法解决ECP，而推理模型明显更好，但仍然难以完全解决该问题。有趣的是，在固定变量数量下考虑不同的连通概率时，我们观察到，对于非推理模型，最难的问题实例与ln n/(n-1)的相变点一致，表明问题的混沌性；相比之下，对于推理模型，最难的问题实例与最大直径一致，表明问题的推理难度。

Original abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) have achieved great improvements in recent years. Nevertheless, it still remains unclear how good LLMs are for reasoning tasks, especially for long-chain ones. In this paper, we evaluate LLMs' performance on the simplest yet long-chain reasoning task, namely the Equivalence Class Problem (ECP), i.e., determining whether two variables are equal given a set of randomly generated equivalence relations. We consider both reasoning and non-reasoning representative LLMs over a large variety of problem instances, ranging over different numbers of variables, connectivity probabilities, prompts, and other factors. The experimental results show that non-reasoning LLMs fail ECP, while reasoning models are significantly better but still struggle to completely solve this problem. Interestingly, considering various connectivity probabilities with a fixed number of variables, we observe that, for non-reasoning models, the hardest problem instances coincide with the phase transition point of ln n/(n-1), suggesting the chaos of the problem; in contrast, for reasoning models, the hardest ones coincide with the biggest diameter, suggesting the reasoning difficulty of the problem.

### [87] [Beyond the Black Box: Interpretability of Agentic AI Tool Use](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06890v4)
*Hariom Tatsat,Ariye Shater*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: agent工具调用的可解释性方法，对监控和调试agent行为有直接帮助。

TL;DR: 本文提出使用稀疏自编码器和线性探针的机械可解释性工具包，在代理行动前读取内部状态来推断工具需求和风险，从而为高风险的代理工作流增加内部可观测性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有代理系统的可观测性方法（如提示、评分、日志）都是外部的，无法在行动前诊断和控制工具使用决策，尤其在长程任务中早期错误代价高昂。

Method: 构建基于稀疏自编码器（SAE）和线性探针的机械可解释性工具包，在代理每次行动前读取模型内部状态，推断工具需求和风险，并通过特征消融测试功能重要性。在NVIDIA Nemotron数据集上训练探针，并应用于多个开源模型。

Result: 工具包能够识别与工具决策相关的模型层和特征，并通过消融验证其因果作用；应用于GPT-OSS 20B和Gemma 3 27B模型，展示了跨模型的内部可观测性。

Conclusion: 该方法为代理系统增加了行动前的内部信号可见性，有助于发现长程任务中早期错误的深层原因，支持工具调用和风险的内部监控，但并非替代外部评估。

中文摘要：AI代理在高风险企业工作流中前景广阔，但依赖部署仍然有限，因为这些工具使用决策难以诊断和控制。代理可能会跳过必要的工具调用、不必要地调用工具，或采取执行后可见后果的行动。现有的可观测性方法是外部的：提示显示相关性，评估评分输出，日志仅在模型已经行动后才到达。在长程设置中，这些失败代价高昂，因为早期的工具错误会改变后续的执行轨迹，增加令牌消耗，并产生下游的安全与安保风险。我们引入了一个基于稀疏自编码器（SAE）的机械可解释性工具包，它可以将激活分解为稀疏的内部特征，以及线性探针——从这些特征中读取信号的轻量级分类器。该框架在每个动作之前读取模型状态，并推断是否需要工具以及下一个工具动作的风险程度。它识别与工具决策最相关的模型层和特征，并通过特征消融测试它们的功能重要性。我们在NVIDIA Nemotron函数调用数据集的多步代理执行轨迹上训练探针，并将相同的工作流程应用于GPT-OSS 20B和Gemma 3 27B模型。目标不是取代外部评估，而是增加缺失的一层：在行动之前模型内部信号的可见性。这有助于揭示代理失败的深层原因，尤其是在早期错误可能影响后续代理行为的长程运行中。更广泛地说，本文展示了机械可解释性如何支持代理系统中工具调用和风险的内部可观测性。

Original abstract: AI agents are promising for high-stakes enterprise workflows, but dependable deployment remains limited because these tool-use decisions are difficult to diagnose and control. Agents may skip required tool calls, invoke tools unnecessarily, or take actions whose consequences become visible only after execution. Existing observability methods are external: prompts reveal correlations, evaluations score outputs, and logs arrive only after the model has already acted. In long-horizon settings, these failures are costly because an early tool mistake can alter the rest of the execution trajectory, increase token consumption, and create downstream safety and security risk.
  We introduce a mechanistic-interpretability toolkit built on Sparse Autoencoders (SAEs), which decompose activations into sparse internal features, and linear probes, lightweight classifiers that read signals from those features. The framework reads model states before each action and infers whether a tool is needed and how risky the next tool action is. It identifies the model layers and features most associated with tool decisions and tests their functional importance through feature ablation. We train the probes on multi-step agent execution traces from the NVIDIA Nemotron function-calling dataset and apply the same workflow to GPT-OSS 20B and Gemma 3 27B models.
  The goal is not to replace external evaluation, but to add a missing layer: visibility into what the model signaled internally before action. This helps surface deeper causes of agent failure, especially in long-horizon runs where an early mistake can impact subsequent agent behavior. More broadly, the paper shows how mechanistic interpretability can support internal observability for monitoring tool calls and risk in agent systems.

### [88] [Mitigating Cognitive Bias in RLHF by Altering Rationality](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06895v1)
*Tiffany Horter,Andrew Markham,Niki Trigoni,Serena Booth*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: RLHF中缓解认知偏差，对agent对齐方法有参考意义。

TL;DR: 提出一种动态调整RLHF中理性参数beta的方法，使用LLM作为评判者评估认知偏差，从而降低不可靠比较的权重，使模型对不完美人类反馈更鲁棒。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 人类反馈在实践中受认知偏差影响，导致偏好不理性，而现有RLHF方法将理性参数beta视为固定常数，无法适应这种偏差，因此需要动态调整beta以处理不完美反馈。

Method: 在奖励学习过程中，利用LLM作为评判者评估每个成对比较中认知偏差的存在，并据此动态调整理性参数beta，从而降低可能包含偏差的比较的权重。

Result: 在强烈偏见偏好的数据集上进行微调时，该方法学习到的下游模型更理性，表现出更好的鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 通过动态调整理性参数，可以有效减轻认知偏差对RLHF的影响，提升模型在现实反馈中的表现。

中文摘要：如何使模型对甚至不完美的人类反馈具有鲁棒性？在从人类反馈中进行强化学习（RLHF）中，人类对模型输出的偏好被用于训练一个奖励模型，该模型为响应分配标量值。由于这些奖励是从成对比较中推断出来的，这种学习依赖于潜在奖励差异与观察到的偏好之间的假设关系，通常使用玻尔兹曼公式建模，其中理性参数beta表示偏好反映奖励差异的一致性程度。在实践中，beta通常被视为一个固定常数，反映假设的统一注释者可靠性。然而，在现实环境中，人类反馈并非如此简单：真实的人类判断受到认知偏差的影响，导致与奖励一致行为的系统性偏差，这些偏差是情境性的。为了解决这个问题，我们将理性视为依赖于上下文和注释的。我们设计了一种方法，在奖励学习过程中使用LLM作为评判者来动态调整理性参数beta，以评估认知偏差的可能存在。这种方法有效地降低了可能反映偏见或不可靠判断的比较的权重。实验表明，即使在具有强烈偏见偏好的数据集上微调时，这种方法也能学习到一个更理性的下游模型。

Original abstract: How can we make models robust to even imperfect human feedback? In reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF), human preferences over model outputs are used to train a reward model that assigns scalar values to responses. Because these rewards are inferred from pairwise comparisons, this learning depends on an assumed relationship between latent reward differences and observed preferences, typically modeled using a Boltzmann formulation in which a rationality parameter beta informs how consistently preferences reflect reward differences. In practice, beta is typically treated as a fixed constant that reflects assumed uniform annotator reliability. However, human feedback is not this simplistic in practice: real human judgments are shaped by cognitive biases, leading to systematic deviations from reward-consistent behavior that arise contextually. To address this, we treat rationality as context- and annotation-dependent. We design an approach to dynamically adjust the rationality parameter beta during reward learning using an LLM-as-judge to assess the likely presence of cognitive biases. This approach effectively downweights comparisons that are likely to reflect biased or unreliable judgments. Empirically, we show that this approach learns a more rational downstream model, even when finetuning on datasets with strongly biased preferences.

</details>


### [89] [Self-Programmed Execution for Language-Model Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06898v1)
*Luke J. O'Connor*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出无固定编排策略的LLM agent架构SPE，通用agent方法可迁移至代码优化agent

TL;DR: 提出自编程执行（SPE）架构，让模型输出自身作为编排程序，通过Spell语言实现自我编辑与重求值，实验表明现有模型可执行复杂智能体任务。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有智能体架构依赖固定编排器，限制了模型的灵活性和自适应能力，需要一种无固定编排策略的智能体机制。

Method: 形式化SPE为智能体机器，引入Spell语言支持程序自我编辑和重求值，并设计效果表达式避免重放副作用。

Result: 未经训练的前沿模型能在SPE模式下完成复杂智能体任务。

Conclusion: 语言模型可在无固定编排策略下作为智能体行动，未来训练自编排策略可能带来新能力。

中文摘要：现有语言模型智能体的核心是一个固定的编排器程序，负责连续轮次之间的状态转换。本文引入了自编程执行（SPE），这是一种智能体架构，其中模型补全本身就是编排器程序，而执行环境评估该程序但不强加自己的编排策略。我使用智能体机器形式化这一思想：SPE状态是指模型补全能从中加载任何嵌入副本的机器状态，这意味着它不受固定的轮次间编排策略约束。在实践中实现SPE并非易事，因为相同的数据既是模型上下文又是可执行程序。因此，我引入了Spell，一种基于Lisp的语言，其中程序可以编辑并重新求值自身，并且像模型调用这样的有副作用的表达式被结构化，使得重新求值已编辑的程序不会重放其副作用。使用现有模型（未经SPE或Spell训练）的实验表明，前沿模型可以在这种模式下运行并完成具有挑战性的智能体任务。这些结果展示了语言模型如何在没有固定编排策略的情况下作为智能体行动，并引发了一个问题：针对自编程执行训练的模型可能会学到什么样的自编排策略。代码可在https://github.com/lukejoconnor/spell获取。

Original abstract: At the heart of existing language model agents is a fixed orchestrator program responsible for the state transition between consecutive turns. This paper introduces self-programmed execution (SPE), an agent architecture in which the model completion is itself the orchestrator program, and the harness evaluates this program but does not impose its own orchestration policy. I formalize this idea using agentic machines: an SPE state is one from which a model completion can load any state of an embedded copy of the machine, meaning that it is subject to no fixed turn-to-turn orchestration policy. Realizing SPE in practice is nontrivial because the same data is both model context and executable program. I therefore introduce Spell, a Lisp-based language in which programs can edit and re-evaluate themselves, and effectful expressions like model invocations are structured such that re-evaluating an edited program does not replay its side effects. Experiments with existing models, not trained for SPE or Spell, show that frontier models can operate in this regime and accomplish challenging agentic tasks. These results demonstrate how an LM can act as an agent without any fixed orchestration policy, and they raise the question of what self-orchestration strategies might be learned by a model trained for self-programmed execution. Code is available at https://github.com/lukejoconnor/spell .

</details>


### [90] [Learning and Reusing Policy Decompositions for Hierarchical Generalized Planning with LLM Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06957v1)
