### [121] [Eta Given Delta: Defining LLM Tool Efficiency With Marginal Tool Utility](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14108v1)
*Nyx Iskandar*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文提出了直接衡量LLM工具使用效率的量化指标，并利用LLM评判工具调用效用，为设计精简工具套件提供依据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究多通过准确性间接评估工具使用效率，缺乏直接衡量指标，无法有效优化工具套件。

Method: 定义工具效率和边际工具效用，通过LLM-as-a-Judge评估每个工具调用的效用符号，进行后验轨迹分析。

Result: 提出了可直接计算的量化指标，可用于识别无用工具调用，提高工具效率而不影响准确性。

Conclusion: 该工作为未来基准设计和精简工具套件工程提供了基础，推动与准确性互补的评估指标的发展。

中文摘要：本文介绍了工具效率（tool efficiency）这一新的量化指标，用于评估LLM智能体轨迹中有用工具调用的比率。为确保工具效率定义明确，我们还引入了边际工具效用（marginal tool utility）这一新的量化指标，该指标针对每个工具调用定义，指示该工具是否有用，或者是否可以安全地从工具套件中移除而不影响准确性，同时提高工具效率；在本文中，我们使用LLM作为评判者（LLM-as-a-Judge）来确定轨迹中每个工具调用的边际工具效用符号。虽然先前已有大量工作致力于开发改进LLM工具使用的技术，以及设计使用准确性作为代理间接衡量效率的评估方法，但我们的工作重点是通过本文提出的量化指标在后验轨迹分析中直接衡量效率。我们的意图是，这项工作作为未来基准设计和智能体工具工程（特别是在创建精简工具套件方面）的跳板，为LLM评估研究的前沿做出贡献，以优化与准确性互补但不同的指标。

Original abstract: This paper introduces tool efficiency, a new quantitative metric to evaluate the rate of useful tool calls in an LLM agent trajectory. To ensure that tool efficiency is well-defined, we also introduce marginal tool utility, a new quantitative metric defined per tool call indicating whether a tool is useful or whether it can be safely removed from the tool suite without affecting accuracy while increasing tool efficiency; in this paper, we determine the sign of marginal tool utility for each tool call in a trajectory using LLM-as-a-Judge. While much prior work has been done to develop techniques that improve tool use by LLMs and design evaluation methods measuring efficiency indirectly using accuracy as a proxy, our work is centered on measuring efficiency directly via the quantitative metric proposed in this paper in post hoc trajectory analyses. It is our intention that this work contributes to the frontier of LLM evaluation research as a springboard for future benchmark designs and agent harness engineering (specifically with regards to creating lean tool suites) that optimize for metrics that complement but are distinct from accuracy.

</details>

*Molood Arman,Clément Bonnafous*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 多agent认知对话框架，多agent协作方法可迁移

TL;DR: 提出了MAPS框架，通过多智能体认知差异建模实现个性化推理与语义对齐的平衡，实验验证其在保持主观性的同时支持语义一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出MAPS框架，包含领域加权轮廓、基于GRU的动态记忆和可解释的token级注意力机制，使具有认知差异的智能体在对话中保持个性化推理并逐步收敛到共享意义。

Result: 在EmpatheticDialogues、TopicalChat和MultiWOZ数据集上评估，MAPS实现了语义对齐而不丧失主观性，平衡了表达性和连贯性。

Conclusion: MAPS展示了通往认知基础、可解释对话系统的可行路径，能够平衡表达多样性与语义一致性。

中文摘要：人类对话不仅仅是信息交换，它还表达信念、情感和主观认知风格。然而，当前的人工智能对话系统常常强制语义一致性，牺牲了多样性和可解释性。我们提出了MAPS（多智能体视角空间），这是一种新颖的框架，通过领域加权轮廓、基于GRU的动态记忆和可解释的token级注意力来建模具有认知差异的智能体之间的对话。MAPS使智能体能够保持个性化推理，同时逐渐在共享意义上收敛。在EmpatheticDialogues、TopicalChat和MultiWOZ上的评估表明，MAPS支持语义对齐而不丧失主观性。我们的结果展示了一条通往认知基础、可解释的对话系统的路径，这些系统平衡了表达性和连贯性。

Original abstract: Human dialogue involves more than exchanging information; it also expresses beliefs, emotions, and subjective cognitive styles. Yet current AI dialogue systems often enforce semantic uniformity, sacrificing diversity and interpretability. We present MAPS (Multi-Agent Perspective Spaces), a novel framework that models dialogue between cognitively distinct agents through domain-weighted profiles, dynamic GRU-based memory, and interpretable token-level attention. MAPS enables agents to maintain individualized reasoning while progressively converging on shared meaning. Evaluations on EmpatheticDialogues, TopicalChat, and MultiWOZ show that MAPS supports semantic alignment without collapsing subjectivity. Our results demonstrate a path toward cognitively grounded, interpretable dialogue systems that balance expressiveness and coherence.

### [123] [Group of Skills: Group-Structured Skill Retrieval for Agent Skill Libraries](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06978v1)
*Kun Zeng,Yu Huo,Siyu Zhang,Zi Ye,Yuecheng Zhuo,Haoyue Liu,Yuquan Lu,Junhao Wen,Xiaoying Tang*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 技能库检索方法，可直接用于coding agent技能管理

TL;DR: GoSkills 将检索从扁平技能列表改为角色标记的执行组，提高了上下文可用性和性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法返回的技能缺乏明确上下文，迫使智能体推断执行细节，效率低且易出错。

Method: GoSkills 从类型化技能图构建以锚点为中心的技能组，通过组图扩展，瓶颈化为原子技能，并输出包含 Start、Support、Check、Avoid 字段的固定契约。

Result: 实验表明 GoSkills 在小预算下保持可见需求覆盖率，优于扁平基线，并常提高奖励和运行时间。

Conclusion: GoSkills 在不修改下游组件的情况下，有效为增强技能的智能体提供可用的结构化上下文。

中文摘要：增强技能的系统智能体越来越依赖于大型可重用技能库，但检索相关技能并不等同于提供可用的上下文。现有方法通常返回原子技能或具有依赖关系的包，但其内部角色仍然隐式，导致智能体需要推断执行入口点、支持技能、可见需求以及避免失败的指导。我们引入了技能组（Group of Skills, GoSkills），一种推理时组结构检索方法，它将面向智能体的检索对象从扁平技能列表变为紧凑的、标记角色的执行上下文。GoSkills 从类型化技能图构建以锚点为中心的技能组，通过组图扩展支持组，将所选组计划瓶颈化为有界原子技能负载集合，并渲染包含开始（Start）、支持（Support）、检查（Check）和避免（Avoid）字段的固定执行契约，而无需改变下游智能体、技能负载或执行环境。在 SkillsBench 和 ALFWorld 上的实验表明，GoSkills 在较小的技能预算下保持了可见需求覆盖率，优于扁平技能访问基线，并且相对于结构检索参考，经常提高奖励和仅智能体运行时。

Original abstract: Skill-augmented agents increasingly rely on large reusable skill libraries, but retrieving relevant skills is not the same as presenting usable context. Existing methods typically return atomic skills or dependency-aware bundles whose internal roles remain implicit, leaving the agent to infer the execution entry point, support skills, visible requirements, and failure-avoidance guidance. We introduce Group of Skills (GoSkills), an inference-time group-structured retrieval method that changes the agent-facing retrieval object from a flat skill list to a compact, role-labeled execution context. GoSkills builds anchor-centered skill groups from a typed skill graph, expands support groups through a group graph, bottlenecks the selected group plan into a bounded set of atomic skill payloads, and renders a fixed execution contract with Start, Support, Check, and Avoid fields, without changing the downstream agent, skill payloads, or execution environment. Experiments on SkillsBench and ALFWorld show that GoSkills preserves visible-requirement coverage under a small skill budget, improves over flat skill-access baselines, and often improves reward and agent-only runtime relative to structural retrieval references.

</details>


### [124] [Cognitive Agent Compilation for Explicit Problem Solver Modeling](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07040v1)
*Hyeongdon Moon,Carolyn Rosé,John Stamper*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 认知agent编译，可迁移至agent知识表示

TL;DR: 提出认知代理编译（CAC）框架，利用教师LLM将问题解决知识编译为显式、可检查、可编辑的目标代理，分离知识、策略和验证规则，通过小型语言模型验证设计权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM在教育中虽广泛使用但难以约束，缺乏可检查性和可编辑性，需要显式的知识状态以满足教育者与学习者的需求。

Method: 受认知架构启发，提出CAC框架：使用强教师LLM编译知识为显式目标代理，分离知识表示、问题解决策略与验证更新规则。

Result: 通过小型语言模型实现早期概念验证，揭示了显式控制与可扩展泛化之间的关键设计权衡。

Conclusion: CAC作为有界知识AI在教育应用的初步步骤，平衡了可检查性与泛化能力。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）被广泛用于辅导、反馈生成和内容创作，但其广泛的预训练使其难以约束，并且作为可控学习者的替代品表现不佳。教育系统通常需要可检查和可编辑的知识状态：教育者希望知道系统假设学习者知道什么，而学习者则受益于系统能够以显式技能、误解和策略来论证其行为。受认知架构启发，我们提出了认知代理编译（CAC）——一个使用强教师LLM将问题解决知识编译为显式目标代理的框架。CAC将（i）知识表示、（ii）问题解决策略以及（iii）验证与更新规则分离，旨在使教育环境中有限的问题解决更加可检查和可编辑。我们展示了一个早期概念验证，使用小型语言模型实现，揭示了关键的设计权衡，特别是显式控制与可扩展泛化之间的权衡，并将CAC定位为面向教育应用的有界知识AI的初步步骤。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are widely used for tutoring, feedback generation, and content creation, but their broad pretraining makes them hard to constrain and poor substitutes for controllable learners. Educational systems often require inspectable and editable knowledge states: educators want to know what a system assumes the learner knows, and learners benefit when the system can justify actions in terms of explicit skills, misconceptions, and strategies. Inspired by cognitive architectures, we propose Cognitive Agent Compilation (CAC), a framework that uses a strong teacher LLM to compile problem-solving knowledge into an explicit target agent. CAC separates (i) knowledge representation, (ii) problem-solving policy, and (iii) verification and update rules, with the goal of making bounded problem solving more inspectable and editable in educational settings. We present an early proof of concept implemented with Small Language Models that surfaces key design trade-offs, particularly between explicit control and scalable generalization, and positions CAC as an initial step toward bounded-knowledge AI for educational applications.

# cs.LG [[Back]](#toc)

### [125] [Multi-Dimensional Behavioral Evaluation of Agentic Stock Prediction Systems Using Large Language Model Judges with Closed-Loop Reinforcement Learning Feedback](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05739v3)
*Mohammad Al Ridhawi,Mahtab Haj Ali,Hussein Al Osman*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 提出用LLM judge对agent决策过程进行多维行为评估并闭环强化学习反馈，方法通用，可迁移到coding agent评估

TL;DR: 提出一种行为评估方法，通过LLM评分多维度中间决策过程，并用于强化学习奖励微调，显著提升了智能体系统的输出性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准评估仅关注最终输出，无法诊断智能体系统的中间决策过程缺陷，需要一种能评分内部行为的方法。

Method: 将行为日志分组为五天片段，由三个LLM集成沿六个维度评分；通过扰动验证维度特异性；将分数转换为惩罚加入SAC奖励，进行三次微调。

Result: 行为得分与夏普比率相关（rho=0.72）；微调后一天MAPE从0.61%降至0.54%（相对降低11.5%），在高波动期间显著。

Conclusion: 该方法可应用于任何可记录中间决策的智能体系统，为评估和改进自主决策过程提供了通用框架。

中文摘要：智能体人工智能系统通过一系列相互依赖的自主决策产生输出，然而标准评估仅评估输出本身，无法诊断底层过程。我们开发了一种行为评估方法，通过评分中间决策过程本身来补充输出级测试。在每个自主决策点记录的 behavioral traces 被分组为每五天一个片段，并由三个大语言模型（LLM）评审员组成的集成系统沿着六个领域特定维度（机制检测、路由、适应、风险校准、策略一致性、错误恢复）进行评分。一个扰动过程会破坏一个维度而保持其他五个维度不变，以确认维度特异性；模型间一致性达到 Krippendorff's alpha = 0.85。综合行为得分与实现的20天夏普比率之间的 Spearman rho 相关系数为 0.72。作为闭环，该框架将每个维度的不足得分转换为信用分配惩罚，添加到 Soft Actor-Critic 奖励中。限制在验证数据上的三个微调周期将一天 MAPE 从 0.61% 降低到 0.54%（相对降低 11.5%；p<0.001，d=0.31），在保留的2017年至2025年测试期间显著，在 Diebold-Mariano 检验下显著，并且由 Giacomini-White 定位到高波动性制度。该方法是应用无关的，适用于任何中间决策可记录的智能体系统。

Original abstract: Agentic artificial intelligence systems produce outputs through sequences of interdependent autonomous decisions, yet standard evaluation assesses outputs alone and cannot diagnose the underlying process. We develop a behavioral evaluation methodology that complements output-level testing by scoring the intermediate decision process itself. Behavioral traces logged at each autonomous decision point are grouped into five-day episodes and scored along six domain-specific dimensions (regime detection, routing, adaptation, risk calibration, strategy coherence, error recovery) by an ensemble of three large language model (LLM) judges. A perturbation procedure that corrupts one dimension while leaving the other five intact confirms dimension specificity; cross-model agreement reaches Krippendorff's alpha = 0.85. The composite behavioral score correlates at Spearman rho = 0.72 with realized 20-day Sharpe ratio. Closing the loop, the framework converts deficient per-dimension scores into a credit-assigned penalty added to the Soft Actor-Critic reward. Three fine-tuning cycles, confined to validation data, reduce one-day MAPE from 0.61% to 0.54% (11.5% relative; p<0.001, d=0.31) on the held-out 2017 to 2025 test period, significant under Diebold-Mariano and localized by Giacomini-White to the high-volatility regime. The methodology is application-agnostic and applies to any agentic system whose intermediate decisions can be logged.

</details>


### [126] [Causal Reinforcement Learning for Complex Card Games: A Magic The Gathering Benchmark](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06066v1)
*Cristiano da Costa Cunha,Ajmal Mian,Tim French,Wei Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

中文摘要：因果强化学习（RL）缺乏针对结合顺序决策、隐藏信息、大规模掩蔽动作空间和显式因果结构的复杂系统的基准测试。我们引入MTG-Causal-RL，这是一个建立在《万智牌》上的Gymnasium基准测试，具有3077维局部观测、478维掩蔽离散动作空间、五种标准竞技套牌类型、三种奖励方案以及一个手动指定的战略变量结构因果模型（SCM）。每个回合都暴露因果变量、SCM预测的干预效应以及每个因素的信用迹，使因果信用分配、留一法跨套牌类型迁移和政策可审计性成为首要指标。我们调整了一组参考基线：随机、启发式、掩蔽PPO、因果世界模型PPO变体以及一个架构匹配的标量控制。我们提出因果图因子优势PPO（CGFA-PPO）作为参考因果代理，它使用获胜概率的SCM父节点作为因子对齐的评论家目标，并带有干预校准损失。所有比较均使用配对种子、配对自助置信区间和预注册族内的Holm-Bonferroni校正。掩蔽PPO和CGFA-PPO达到具有竞争力的分布内胜率并超过随机基线；每因子校准轨迹和留一法迁移差距揭示了标量胜率单独无法的诊断结构。我们公开了基准、参考基线结果和完整评估协议。通过将策略丰富、部分可观测的领域与显式因果接口和统计协议相结合，MTG-Causal-RL为因果RL、世界模型和LLM代理研究提供了一个共享测试平台，以应对当前基准无法同时提出的问题：掩蔽动作空间下的因果信用分配、跨套牌类型的结构迁移以及基于SCM的政策可审计性。

Original abstract: Causal reinforcement learning (RL) lacks benchmarks for complex systems that combine sequential decision making, hidden information, large masked action spaces, and explicit causal structure. We introduce MTG-Causal-RL, a Gymnasium benchmark built on Magic: The Gathering with a 3,077-dimensional partial observation, a 478-action masked discrete action space, five competitive Standard archetypes, three reward schemes, and a hand-specified Structural Causal Model (SCM) over strategic variables. Every episode exposes causal variables, SCM-predicted intervention effects, and per-factor credit traces, making causal credit assignment, leave-one-out cross-archetype transfer, and policy auditability first-class metrics. We adapt a panel of reference baselines: random, heuristic, masked PPO, a causal-world-model PPO variant, and an architecture-matched scalar control. We propose Causal Graph-Factored Advantage PPO (CGFA-PPO) as a reference causal agent that uses SCM parents of win probability as factor-aligned critic targets with an intervention-calibration loss. All comparisons use paired seeds, paired-bootstrap confidence intervals, and Holm-Bonferroni correction within pre-registered families. Masked PPO and CGFA-PPO reach competitive in-distribution win rates and exceed the random baseline; per-factor calibration trajectories and leave-one-out transfer gaps expose diagnostic structure that scalar win rate alone cannot. We release the benchmark, reference-baseline results, and full evaluation protocol openly. By coupling a strategically rich, partially observed domain with an explicit causal interface and statistical protocol, MTG-Causal-RL gives causal-RL, world-model, and LLM-agent research a shared testbed for questions current benchmarks cannot pose together: causal credit assignment under masked action spaces, structural transfer across archetypes, and SCM-grounded policy auditability.

### [127] [In-Context Black-Box Optimization with Unreliable Feedback](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06187v1)
*Nicolas Samuel Blumer,Julien Martinelli,Samuel Kaski*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 上下文黑盒优化方法，可应用于程序自动调优，涉及in-context学习与反馈融合

TL;DR: 提出FICBO，一种利用预训练Transformer在测试时结合历史观测和辅助反馈进行黑箱优化，通过结构化反馈先验建模源可靠性，有效利用信息性反馈并鲁棒应对误导性源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有反馈感知BO方法一次处理一个任务，泛化能力有限；上下文内优化器仅依赖优化历史，忽略了测试时可用的辅助反馈，从而限制了优化效率。

Method: 引入结构化反馈先验，模拟反馈源在访问、相关性和扭曲程度上的差异；使用该先验预训练一个反馈感知Transformer，在测试时条件化于历史观测和当前候选集的辅助反馈，通过比较目标值与辅助信号动态估计源可靠性。

Result: 在合成和真实世界任务上，FICBO有效利用信息性反馈，同时保持对弱或误导源的鲁棒性，优于其他基线方法。

Conclusion: FICBO能够泛化到多种反馈源，通过上下文感知的源可靠性估计提升黑箱优化性能，并展示了模型的可解释性。

中文摘要：科学和工程中的黑箱优化通常伴随辅助信息：专家、模拟器、预训练预测器或启发式方法可以提示哪些候选者看起来有希望。这些信息可以加速搜索，但也可能是有偏的、依赖于输入的或误导性的。反馈感知的BO方法通常一次处理一个任务，限制了它们在多个反馈源上泛化的能力。上下文内优化器处理跨任务适应，但通常假设优化历史是测试时可用的唯一信号。我们研究了反馈感知的上下文内黑箱优化（FICBO），其中预训练优化器同时基于观测历史和当前候选集的廉价辅助反馈进行条件化。我们引入了一个结构化反馈先验，模拟反馈源在访问、相关性和相对于真实目标的扭曲程度上的变化，并用其预训练一个反馈感知的Transformer。在测试时，模型通过比较观测目标值与辅助信号来估计上下文中的源可靠性，从而改进查询选择。在合成和真实世界任务上，FICBO有效利用信息性反馈，同时保持对弱或误导源的鲁棒性，优于其他基线。实证研究进一步说明了模型如何感知测试时源，提供了对其可解释性和决策过程的见解。

Original abstract: Black-box optimization in science and engineering often comes with side information: experts, simulators, pretrained predictors, or heuristics can suggest which candidates look promising. This information can accelerate search, but it can also be biased, input-dependent, or misleading. Feedback-aware BO methods typically handle one task at a time, limiting their ability to generalize over multiple sources of feedback. In-context optimizers address cross-task adaptation, but usually assume that optimization history is the only available signal at test time. We study feedback-informed in-context black-box optimization (FICBO), where a pretrained optimizer conditions on both the observed history and cheap auxiliary feedback for the current candidate set. We introduce a structured feedback prior that models how feedback sources vary in their access, relevance, and distortion relative to the true objective, and use it to pretrain a feedback-aware transformer. At test time, the model estimates source reliability in context by comparing observed objective values with auxiliary signals, improving query selection. On synthetic and real-world tasks, FICBO effectively exploits informative feedback while remaining robust to weak or misleading sources, improving over other baselines. Empirical investigations further illustrate how the model perceives test-time sources, offering insights into its interpretability and decision-making process.

### [128] [Memory Inception: Latent-Space KV Cache Manipulation for Steering LLMs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06225v2)
*Andy Zeyi Liu,Michael Zhang,Ilana Greenberg,Adam Alnasser,Lucas Baker,John Sous*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 潜空间记忆注入方法，对agent记忆操纵有启发

TL;DR: 提出记忆注入（MI），一种无需训练的方法，通过在选定层插入文本派生的KV存储来引导LLM，在个性引导、可更新行为和结构化推理任务上均优于现有方法，并大幅降低KV存储开销。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有引导方法存在不足：指令提示控制强但缓存开销大且易杂乱；激活引导紧凑但控制弱且不支持大型结构化提示。需要一种兼顾控制力、紧凑性和灵活性的方法。

Method: 记忆注入（MI）在潜在注意力空间中选择性地插入文本派生的键值（KV）存储于特定层，作为引导隐式提醒，而非显式缓存所有引导内容。

Result: 在个性引导任务中，MI在控制-漂移权衡上优于CAA且与提示竞争；在可更新引导中实现最高转变后对齐（Qwen3）；在结构化推理（HARDMath、PHYSICS）中优于可见提示（10/12个单元格），KV存储减少高达118倍。

Conclusion: MI是一种强大的引导方法，特别适用于持久性、结构化或难以保留在可见转录中的引导场景，兼具控制力、紧凑性和可更新性。

中文摘要：引导大型语言模型（LLM）通常通过指令提示或激活引导两种方式。提示通常提供较强的控制，但会在每一层缓存引导标记，并可能使长交互变得杂乱；激活引导紧凑但通常较弱，并且不支持大型结构化提示。我们引入了记忆注入（MI），一种无需训练的方法，通过在选定层插入文本派生的键值（KV）存储来在潜在注意力空间中进行引导。MI不是在整个提示缓存中物化提醒内容，而是将引导视为选择性KV分配，仅在模型路由到的位置注入潜在槽位。在匹配的个性引导任务中，MI提供了最佳的整体控制-漂移权衡，与提示相比保持竞争力，同时始终优于CAA。在可更新引导方面，MI支持无需重写可见转录的会话中行为转变，在Qwen3上实现了最高的转变后对齐。在结构化推理方面，MI在HARDMath和PHYSICS上优于可见提示（10/12个主题×模式单元格），作为可验证域中结构化推理的代理，同时将内容匹配的KV存储减少高达118倍。这些结果将MI定位为一种强大的引导方法，当引导是持久性、结构化或难以保持在可见转录中时。

Original abstract: Steering large language models (LLMs) is usually done by either instruction prompting or activation steering. Prompting often gives strong control, but caches guidance tokens at every layer and can clutter long interactions; activation steering is compact but typically weaker and does not support large structured reminders. We introduce memory inception (MI), a training-free method that steers in latent attention space by inserting text-derived key-value (KV) banks only at selected layers. Rather than materializing reminder content throughout the prompt cache, MI treats steering as selective KV allocation, injecting latent slots only where the model routes to them. On matched personality-steering tasks, MI gives the best overall control--drift trade-off, remaining competitive with prompting while consistently outperforming CAA. On updateable guidance, MI supports mid-conversation behavior shifts without rewriting the visible transcript, achieving the highest post-shift alignment on Qwen3. On structured reasoning, MI outperforms visible prompting on HARDMath and PHYSICS (10/12 subject$\times$mode cells), serving as proxies for structured reasoning in verifiable domains, while cutting content-matched KV storage by up to 118$\times$. These results position MI as a powerful steering method when guidance is persistent, structured, or expensive to keep in the visible transcript.

### [129] [Is Escalation Worth It? A Decision-Theoretic Characterization of LLM Cascades](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06350v1)
*Dylan Bouchard*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: LLM级联的决策理论分析，对coding agent的模型选择与defer策略有借鉴。

TL;DR: 通过约束优化框架分析模型级联的成本-质量边界，发现成对包络线优于固定链，而轻量级路由器因避免廉价模型生成成本而更优。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法将转交阈值视为经验超参数，缺乏对成本-质量边界几何特性的理论指导，因此需要更系统的框架。

Method: 基于约束优化和对偶理论，建立双模型级联的分段凹性边界，推广到k模型级联，并推导一阶条件；通过五个基准测试验证。

Result: 确定性阈值级联中，成对包络线优于完全固定链；轻量级预生成路由器在多数数据集上超过最佳级联，原因是避免了不必要的生成成本。

Conclusion: 级联性能受限于结构成本（必须先支付廉价模型），而非中间阶段短缺。

中文摘要：模型级联（Model cascades）是一种在低置信度查询时由廉价LLM转交昂贵LLM处理的技术，广泛用于在部署中平衡成本与质量。现有方法大多将转交阈值视为经验超参数，对于模型池中所得成本-质量边界曲线的几何特性指导有限。我们开发了一个基于约束优化和对偶理论的决策框架。对于双模型级联，我们建立了在置信度支持度递减收益区域上的成本-质量边界曲线的分段凹性，并通过互易影子价格联系了预算约束和质量约束的公式。给定一个包含k个模型的池，我们描述了确定性双模型阈值级联所能达到的边界曲线，它是由\binom{k}{2}个成对级联的逐点包络线，并在切换点处最优对发生变化。对于k模型级联，我们推导出一阶条件，其中单个影子价格在阶段边界上均衡了边际质量-成本比。我们在五个基准测试（MATH、MMLU、TriviaQA、SimpleQA、LiveCodeBench）上使用来自五个提供商的八个模型验证了该框架。在确定性阈值级联类中，完全固定链的性能低于成对包络线，而优化的子序列级联并未带来实际意义上的保持集外增益。一个轻量级的预生成路由器在五个数据集中的四个上超过了最佳级联策略，主要原因是它避免了廉价模型在直接发送到大模型的查询上的生成成本，而非由于更强的路由信号。这些结果表明，级联性能主要受限于结构成本，因为级联在任何升级决策之前都会支付廉价模型的成本，而非由于中间阶段的短缺。

Original abstract: Model cascades, in which a cheap LLM defers to an expensive one on low-confidence queries, are widely used to navigate the cost-quality tradeoff at deployment. Existing approaches largely treat the deferral threshold as an empirical hyperparameter, with limited guidance on the geometry of the resulting cost-quality frontier over a model pool. We develop a decision-theoretic framework grounded in constrained optimization and duality. For a two-model cascade, we establish piecewise concavity of the cost-quality frontier on decreasing-benefit regions of the confidence support, with reciprocal shadow prices linking the budget- and quality-constrained formulations. Given a pool of $k$ models, we characterize the frontier achievable by deterministic two-model threshold cascades as the pointwise envelope over $\binom{k}{2}$ pairwise cascades, with switching points where the optimal pair changes. For $k$-model cascades, we derive first-order conditions in which a single shadow price equalizes marginal quality-per-cost across stage boundaries. We validate the framework on five benchmarks (MATH, MMLU, TriviaQA, SimpleQA, LiveCodeBench) across eight models from five providers. Within the deterministic threshold-cascade class, full fixed chains underperform the pairwise envelope, and optimized subsequence cascades do not deliver practically meaningful held-out gains over it. A lightweight pre-generation router exceeds the best cascade policy on four of five datasets, mainly because it avoids the cheap model's generation cost on queries sent directly to a larger model rather than because of a stronger routing signal. These results suggest that cascade performance is limited primarily by structural cost, since cascades pay the cheap model before any escalation decision, rather than by a shortage of intermediate stages.

*Apurva Gandhi,Satyaki Chakraborty,Xiangjun Wang,Aviral Kumar,Graham Neubig*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Original abstract: We introduce Recursive Agent Optimization (RAO), a reinforcement learning approach for training recursive agents: agents that can spawn and delegate sub-tasks to new instantiations of themselves recursively. Recursive agents implement an inference-time scaling algorithm that naturally allows agents to scale to longer contexts and generalize to more difficult problems via divide-and-conquer. RAO provides a method to train models to best take advantage of such recursive inference, teaching agents when and how to delegate and communicate. We find that recursive agents trained in this way enjoy better training efficiency, can scale to tasks that go beyond the model's context window, generalize to tasks much harder than the ones the agent was trained on, and can enjoy reduced wall-clock time compared to single-agent systems.

### [131] [Verifier-Backed Hard Problem Generation for Mathematical Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06660v1)
*Yuhang Lai,Jiazhan Feng,Yee Whye Teh,Ning Miao*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: setter-solver-verifier三方自对抗生成难题，可迁移至代码优化benchmark生成

TL;DR: 提出VHG框架，通过三方自博弈引入独立验证器，有效生成有效且高难度的问题，显著优于基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有问题生成方法依赖昂贵人工或朴素自博弈，后者因奖励破解产生无效问题。

Method: 采用三方自博弈，引入独立验证器评估问题有效性，与求解者评估的难度共同决定设定者奖励。具体实例化了硬符号验证器和软LLM验证器。

Result: 在不定积分任务和一般数学推理任务上，VHG在所有基线方法上取得显著优势。

Conclusion: VHG框架能有效生成有效、有挑战性的问题，提升LLM问题生成能力。

中文摘要：大语言模型（LLMs）在解决科学和数学问题方面表现出强大的能力，但在生成有效、有挑战性且新颖的问题方面仍然存在困难——而这是推进LLM训练和实现自主科学研究的关键组成部分。现有问题生成方法要么依赖于昂贵的人类专家参与，要么采用朴素的自博弈范式，后者由于奖励破解常常产生无效问题。本文提出VHG，一种基于三方自博弈的验证器增强的难题生成框架。通过将独立的验证器整合到传统的设定者-求解者二元结构中，我们的设计约束设定者的奖励由问题有效性（由验证器评估）和难度（由求解者评估）共同决定。我们实例化了两种验证器变体：硬符号验证器和软基于LLM的验证器，并在不定积分任务和一般数学推理任务上进行了评估。实验结果表明，VHG在所有基线方法上明显优于它们，优势显著。

Original abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) demonstrate strong capabilities for solving scientific and mathematical problems, yet they struggle to produce valid, challenging, and novel problems - an essential component for advancing LLM training and enabling autonomous scientific research. Existing problem generation approaches either depend on expensive human expert involvement or adopt naive self-play paradigms, which frequently yield invalid problems due to reward hacking. This work introduces VHG, a verifier-enhanced hard problem generation framework built upon three-party self-play. By integrating an independent verifier into the conventional setter-solver duality, our design constrains the setter's reward to be jointly determined by problem validity (evaluated by the verifier) and difficulty (assessed by the solver). We instantiate two verifier variants: a Hard symbolic verifier and a Soft LLM-based verifier, with evaluations conducted on indefinite integral tasks and general mathematical reasoning tasks. Experimental results show that VHG substantially outperforms all baseline methods by a clear margin.

</details>


### [132] [Distributional Process Reward Models: Calibrated Prediction of Future Rewards via Conditional Optimal Transport](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06785v2)
*Rachel Ma,Dylan Hadfield-Menell,Kristjan Greenewald*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 过程奖励模型校准，可用于agent评估与推理时扩展，但直接相关性较低

TL;DR: 首次使用条件最优传输校准过程奖励模型（PRM），改善校准效果并集成到实例自适应扩展框架中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: PRM通常校准不良且高估成功概率，需要更好的校准方法。

Method: 修改条件最优传输映射学习，估计基于PRM隐藏状态的条件单调分位数函数，用于校准成功概率。

Result: 在MATH-500和AIME基准上，方法显著改善校准，并在Best-of-N IAS任务上提升性能。

Conclusion: 条件最优传输是PRM校准的有原则且实用的方法，提供结构保证和灵活的不确定性估计。

中文摘要：推理时扩展方法依赖于过程奖励模型（PRM），这些模型通常校准不良且高估成功概率。我们提出了据我们所知首次使用条件最优传输来校准PRM的方法，修改条件OT（CondOT）映射学习\cite{bunne2022supervised}以估计一个单调的条件分位数函数，该函数基于PRM估计的成功概率，并以PRM隐藏状态为条件。这产生了结构上有效的分位数估计，并能够在任意水平上高效提取置信界，我们将其整合到\cite{park2025know}的实例自适应扩展（IAS）框架中。我们在涵盖中等难度问题（MATH-500）和更难分布外问题（AIME）的数学推理基准上进行了评估。对于具有可靠排名信号的PRM，我们的方法比未校准的PRM和分位数回归显著改善了校准。在下游的Best-of-N IAS性能上，我们的方法通常优于未校准的PRM。这些结果确立了条件最优传输作为另一种有原则且实用的PRM校准方法，提供了结构保证和灵活的不确定性估计。

Original abstract: Inference-time scaling methods rely on Process Reward Models (PRMs), which are often poorly calibrated and overestimate success probabilities. We propose, to our knowledge, the first use of conditional optimal transport for calibrating PRMs, modifying conditional OT (CondOT) map learning \cite{bunne2022supervised} to estimate a monotonic conditional quantile function over success probabilities estimated by the PRM, conditioned on PRM hidden states. This yields structurally valid quantile estimates and enables efficient extraction of confidence bounds at arbitrary levels, which we integrate into the instance-adaptive scaling (IAS) framework of \cite{park2025know}. We evaluate on mathematical reasoning benchmarks spanning moderate-difficulty problems (MATH-500) and harder out-of-distribution problems (AIME). For PRMs with reliable ranking signals, our method substantially improves calibration over both uncalibrated PRMs and quantile regression. On downstream Best-of-N IAS performance, our method generally improves over uncalibrated PRMs. These results establish conditional optimal transport as another principled and practical approach to PRM calibration, offering structural guarantees and flexible uncertainty estimation.

### [133] [Path-Coupled Bellman Flows for Distributional Reinforcement Learning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08253v2)
*Boyang Xu,Qing Zou,Siqin Yang,Hao Yan*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 分布强化学习方法，对RL agent训练有潜在启发。

TL;DR: 提出路径耦合贝尔曼流（PCBF），一种连续时间分布强化学习方法，通过源一致的贝尔曼耦合路径和共享噪声来学习回报分布，减少边界匹配和高方差问题，实验表明改进的分布保真度和稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有分布强化学习方法存在有限支撑方法依赖投影、基于流的方法遭受边界不匹配或高方差自举问题，需要更稳定且保真度更高的方法。

Method: 提出路径耦合贝尔曼流（PCBF），采用连续时间流匹配，使用源一致的贝尔曼耦合路径：当前路径从基础先验开始，达到贝尔曼目标，并与后继流保持路径仿射关系；通过共享基础噪声耦合当前和后继流，并用λ参数化控制变量目标平衡偏差和方差。

Result: 在解析可处理的MRP、OGBench和D4RL实验上，PCBF展示了改进的分布保真度和训练稳定性，以及具有竞争力的离线RL性能。

Conclusion: PCBF通过路径耦合和共享噪声有效缓解了边界不匹配和高方差问题，为分布强化学习提供了一种稳定且保真度高的新方法。

中文摘要：分布强化学习（DRL）建模完整的回报分布，但现有的有限支撑或基于分位数的方法依赖于投影，而最近的基于流的方法可能遭受流源处的边界不匹配，或当当前噪声和后继噪声独立时面临高方差的自举。我们提出了路径耦合贝尔曼流（PCBF），这是一种连续时间DRL方法，通过使用源一致的贝尔曼耦合路径进行流匹配来学习回报分布：当前路径从t=0所需的基础先验开始，在t=1达到贝尔曼目标，并在中间时间保持与后继流的路径仿射关系（不需要时间t边际分布对所有t满足分布贝尔曼不动点）。PCBF通过共享基础噪声耦合当前和后继回报流，并使用λ参数化的控制变量目标：λ=0恢复无偏样本贝尔曼目标，而λ>0以受控偏差换取方差减少。在解析可处理的MRP、OGBench和D4RL上的实验显示了改进的分布保真度和训练稳定性，以及具有竞争力的离线强化学习性能。

Original abstract: Distributional reinforcement learning (DRL) models the full return distribution, but existing finite-support or quantile-based methods rely on projections, while recent flow-based approaches can suffer from \emph{boundary mismatch} at the flow source or from \emph{high-variance} bootstrapping when current and successor noises are independent. We propose Path-Coupled Bellman Flows (PCBF), a continuous-time DRL method that learns return distributions with flow matching using \textbf{source-consistent Bellman-coupled paths}: the current path starts from the required base prior at $t{=}0$, reaches the Bellman target at $t{=}1$, and maintains a pathwise affine relation to the successor flow at intermediate times (without requiring time-$t$ marginals to satisfy a distributional Bellman fixed point for all $t$). PCBF couples current and successor return flows through shared base noise and uses a $λ$-parameterized control-variate target: $λ{=}0$ recovers an unbiased sample Bellman target, while $λ{>}0$ trades controlled bias for variance reduction. Experiments on analytically tractable MRPs, OGBench, and D4RL show improved distributional fidelity and training stability, and competitive offline RL performance.

</details>


### [134] [Same Signal, Opposite Meaning: Direction-Informed Adaptive Learning for LLM Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06908v1)
*Ziming Li,Jiatan Huang,Xiaoguang Guo,Guilin Wang,Chuxu Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 提出自适应计算分配方法DIAL用于LLM agent，通用agent推理改进

TL;DR: 提出DIAL方法，通过信号无关的反事实探索学习状态特征的效用方向，解决了固定方向门控在异质设置中的不可靠问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法假设门控信号到计算价值方向固定，但实际中这种对齐不稳定，导致性能恶化。

Method: DIAL是一种稀疏门控，训练时使用信号无关的反事实探索来学习每个(环境,骨干网络)的状态特征效用方向。

Result: 在六个环境和三个骨干网络上，DIAL实现了比固定方向基线更强的成功-成本权衡。

Conclusion: 固定方向门控不可靠，DIAL通过学习效用方向提高了自适应测试时计算的性能。

中文摘要：自适应测试时计算对于LLM智能体旨在只在提升性能时调用额外计算。现有方法通常使用基于置信度、不确定性或难度的门控，假设从门控信号通过计算需求到计算价值的方向是固定的。这使得门控成为一个效用校准问题：门控信号应与额外计算相比基础策略是否改善最终结果相一致。我们表明这种对齐是不稳定的：相同的信号在一个设置中预测展开有益，在另一个中预测展开有害，即使在任务固定时，跨环境和骨干网络也会出现反转。因此，错误方向的门控可能通过精确选择有害状态而恶化性能。这种反转反映了计算需求和计算适用性之间的更深层次区别：高不确定性信号可能指示决策困难的状态，其中展开有助于比较替代方案，或者指示不适合干预的状态，其中当前上下文不支持基于展开的有用改进。在这种双源模型下，固定方向的门控在异质设置中不可靠。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了DIAL（方向感知自适应学习），一种稀疏门控，通过信号无关的反事实探索进行训练，以学习每个（环境，骨干网络）的状态特征的效用方向。在六个环境和三个骨干网络上，DIAL相比固定方向基线实现了更强的总体成功-成本权衡。

Original abstract: Adaptive test-time compute for LLM agents aims to invoke extra computation only when it improves performance. Existing methods typically use confidence-, uncertainty-, or difficulty-based gates, assuming a fixed direction from the gating signal through compute need to the value of computation. This makes gating a utility-calibration problem: gating signals should align with whether extra computation improves the final outcome over the base policy. We show that this alignment is unstable: the same signal predicts rollout benefit in one setting and rollout harm in another, with reversals across environments and backbones even when the task is fixed. Wrong-direction gates can therefore worsen performance by precisely selecting harmful states. This reversal reflects a deeper distinction between compute need and compute suitability: a high uncertainty signal may indicate decision-difficult states where rollouts help compare alternatives, or intervention-unsuitable states where the current context does not support useful rollout-based improvement. Under this two-source model, fixed-direction gates are unreliable across heterogeneous settings. To address this, we propose DIAL (Direction-Informed Adaptive Learning), a sparse gate trained from signal-agnostic counterfactual exploration to learn the utility direction of state features per (environment, backbone). Across six environments and three backbones, DIAL yields a stronger overall success-cost trade-off than fixed-direction baselines.

</details>


### [135] [Delulu: A Verified Multi-Lingual Benchmark for Code Hallucination Detection in Fill-in-the-Middle Tasks](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07024v1)
*Mahdi Erfanian,Nelson Daniel Troncoso,Aashna Garg,Amabel Gale,Xiaoyu Liu,Pareesa Ameneh Golnari,Shengyu Fu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了Delulu基准测试，用于评估代码生成模型在FIM任务中的幻觉问题，发现最强模型仅84.5% pass@1，幻觉是任务固有挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 代码生成模型在FIM任务中经常产生看似合理但错误的完成，导致运行时错误，而现有基准未能充分暴露这一挑战。

Method: 通过对抗性流程构建1,951个多语言FIM样本，包括LLM生成幻觉、多模型评估、嵌入聚类、Docker验证和人工审查，形成高质量基准Delulu。

Result: 11个开源FIM模型中，最强模型仅84.5% pass@1，最大编辑相似度0.77，所有家族在非平凡样本上产生幻觉对齐的完成。

Conclusion: Delulu暴露的困难是FIM任务固有的，而非模型家族特有，表明需要更好的方法解决代码生成中的幻觉问题。

中文摘要：大型语言模型在填充中间（FIM）任务中频繁产生幻觉——看似合理但错误的完成，例如虚构的API方法、无效参数、未定义变量或不存在的导入。这些失败通过表面审查却引入运行时错误。我们提出了Delulu，一个经过验证的多语言基准测试，包含跨7种语言和4种幻觉类型的1,951个FIM样本。样本通过对抗性流程构建：前沿LLM生成看似合理的幻觉，四个不同的判别模型对其进行评估，基于嵌入的聚类挖掘逐渐困难的样本，自包含Docker容器验证黄金完成能编译而幻觉变体产生预期的运行时错误，最后经过人类专家审查移除任何剩余的有偏见或可简单判别的样本。我们评估了来自五个家族的11个开源FIM模型，参数规模从0.5B到32B：包括一个六点Qwen2.5-Coder缩放系列，以及一个跨家族系列（CodeLlama、DeepSeek-Coder-V2、StarCoder2）。最强模型仅达到84.5%的pass@1，没有家族超过0.77的编辑相似度，并且每个家族都在非平凡的样本份额上产生与幻觉对齐的完成，证实了Delulu暴露的困难是任务固有的而非家族特有的。我们在https://github.com/microsoft/delulu发布了该基准测试、容器和评估框架。

Original abstract: Large Language Models for code generation frequently produce hallucinations in Fill-in-the-Middle (FIM) tasks -- plausible but incorrect completions such as invented API methods, invalid parameters, undefined variables, or non-existent imports. These failures pass superficial review yet introduce runtime errors. We introduce Delulu, a verified multi-lingual benchmark of 1,951 FIM samples across 7 languages and 4 hallucination types. Samples are curated through an adversarial pipeline: a frontier LLM generates plausible hallucinations, four diverse judge models evaluate them, embedding-based clustering mines progressively harder examples, self-contained Docker containers verify that golden completions compile while hallucinated variants produce the expected runtime error, and a final human-expert review removes any remaining biased or trivially decidable samples. We evaluate 11 open-weight FIM models from five families spanning 0.5B-32B parameters: a six-point Qwen2.5-Coder scaling slate, plus a cross-family slate (CodeLlama, DeepSeek-Coder-V2, StarCoder2). The strongest model reaches only 84.5% pass@1, no family exceeds 0.77 Edit Similarity, and every family produces hallucination-aligned completions on a non-trivial share of samples, confirming that the difficulty exposed by Delulu is task-intrinsic rather than family-specific. We release the benchmark, containers, and evaluation framework at https://github.com/microsoft/delulu.

### [136] [A Systematic Investigation of RL-Jailbreaking in LLMs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07032v2)
*Montaser Mohammedalamen,Kevin Roice,Reginald McLean,Alyssa Lefaivre Škopac*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: RL越狱分析，可迁移至agent安全

TL;DR: 本文首次系统分解RL越狱框架，发现环境形式化（密集奖励和延长回合长度）是越狱成功的主要驱动因素。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解强化学习越狱框架为何成功的内在机制尚不完整，需要系统性分析以揭示其结构决定因素。

Method: 对RL越狱框架进行系统分解，分为问题形式化（奖励函数、动作空间、回合长度）和算法措施（RL算法、训练数据、奖励塑造），通过实验识别对抗成功的结构决定因素。

Result: RL越狱成功攻破了所有目标模型和安全防护措施；环境形式化（尤其是密集奖励和延长回合长度）是越狱成功的主要驱动因素。

Conclusion: 本研究提供了改进RL越狱效率的工具，并最终有助于增强生成模型对基于RL的攻击的防御能力。

中文摘要：生成模型从下一个标记预测器到复杂系统自主引擎的进化需要严格的安全加固。对抗性越狱，即通过策略性操纵模型以引发有害输出，仍然是安全部署的主要威胁。虽然强化学习（RL）将通过顺序优化的多步骤攻击框架化越狱问题，但该框架为何成功的内在机制理解仍不完整。为填补这一空白，我们首次对RL越狱进行了系统分解。我们将该框架解构为问题形式化（奖励函数、动作空间、回合长度）和算法措施（RL算法、训练数据、奖励塑造），以识别对抗成功的结构决定因素。我们的结果显示，RL越狱成功攻破了所有目标模型和安全防护措施。通过这一首次分析，我们证明环境形式化，特别是密集奖励和延长回合长度，是越狱成功的主要驱动因素。这项工作提供了改进RL越狱效率的工具，并最终增强生成模型对基于RL的攻击的抵抗力。

Original abstract: The evolution of generative models from next-token predictors to autonomous engines of complex systems necessitates rigorous safety hardening. Adversarial jailbreaking, the strategic manipulation of models to elicit harmful output, remains a primary threat to safe deployment. While Reinforcement Learning (RL) frames jailbreaking as a multi-step attack through sequential optimization, a mechanistic understanding of why the framework succeeds remains incomplete. To fill this gap, we present the first systematic decomposition of RL jailbreaking. We deconstruct the framework into problem formalization (reward function, action space, episode length), and algorithmic measures (RL algorithm, training data, reward-shaping) to identify the structural determinants of adversarial success. Our results reveal that the RL-jailbreaker successfully compromised all targeted models and safeguards. Through this first-of-its-kind analysis, we demonstrate that environment formalization, specifically dense rewards and extended episode lengths, is the primary driver of jailbreaking success. This work provides a tool for improving RL-jailbreaker efficiency and, ultimately, harden generative models resistant to RL-based attacks.

### [137] [Towards Differentially Private Reinforcement Learning with General Function Approximation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07049v1)
*Yi He,Xingyu Zhou*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 差分隐私RL理论，可迁移至agent安全

TL;DR: 本文首次为具有一般函数逼近的差分隐私在线强化学习提供了理论保证，遗憾界达到$\widetilde{O}(K^{3/5})$，并揭示了线性情况下的差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有差分隐私在线强化学习的研究局限于表格和线性设置，缺乏对更一般函数逼近的理论保证。

Method: 将批量策略更新方案与指数机制相结合，进行了新颖的遗憾分析。

Result: 在一般函数逼近下，差分隐私无模型设置的遗憾与线性情况下的最先进水平匹配，为$\widetilde{O}(K^{3/5})$，并首次建立了基于覆盖性复杂度的批处理更新遗憾界。

Conclusion: 填补了差分隐私在线强化学习在一般函数逼近方面的理论空白，并澄清了线性函数逼近私有RL的研究现状。

中文摘要：我们首次提出了具有一般函数逼近的差分隐私在线强化学习（RL）的理论保证，超越了先前局限于表格和线性设置的工作。我们的方法结合了批量策略更新方案与指数机制，以及新颖的遗憾分析。我们表明，即使在一般的函数逼近下，差分隐私下无模型设置中的遗憾与线性情况下的最新技术相匹配，缩放为$\widetilde{O}(K^{3/5})$，其中$K$表示情节数。作为一个重要的副产品，我们还建立了批处理更新的在线RL的第一个遗憾界，该界依赖于标准复杂性度量——覆盖性，补充了基于新引入的Eluder-Condition类的现有结果。此外，我们揭示了最近关于线性函数逼近的私有RL结果中的基本差距，从而澄清了其前景。

Original abstract: We present the first theoretical guarantees for differentially private online reinforcement learning (RL) with general function approximation, extending beyond prior work restricted to tabular and linear settings. Our approach combines a batched policy update scheme with the exponential mechanism, together with a novel regret analysis. We show that, even under general function approximation, the regret in the model-free setting under differential privacy matches the state of the art for the linear case, scaling as $\widetilde{O}(K^{3/5})$, where $K$ denotes the number of episodes. As an important by-product, we also establish the first regret bound for online RL with batch update that depends on the standard complexity measure of coverability, complementing existing results based on a newly introduced Eluder-Condition class. In addition, we uncover fundamental gaps in recent results for private RL with linear function approximation, thereby clarifying its landscape.

</details>

### [138] [OBLIQ-Bench: Exposing Overlooked Bottlenecks in Modern Retrievers with Latent and Implicit Queries](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06235v2)
*Diane Tchuindjo,Devavrat Shah,Omar Khattab*

Main category: cs.IR

Selection reason: 潜隐式查询检索基准，可迁移至agent检索增强与信息获取

TL;DR: 本文提出斜交查询概念，揭示检索与验证的不对称性，并发布OBLIQ-Bench以推动能捕获潜在模式的检索架构研究。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有检索基准饱和，但高效搜索仍未解决，尤其是缺乏对寻找隐含模式文档（斜交查询）的研究。

Method: 定义斜交查询及其三种产生机制，构建包含五个真实长尾语料库的OBLIQ-Bench基准，对比检索与LLM验证表现。

Result: 发现推理LLM在给定相关文档时能可靠识别潜在相关性，但检索管道无法召回大多数相关文档，存在不对称性。

Conclusion: 斜交查询的挑战未被解决，需要发展能捕捉隐式信号的新检索架构，OBLIQ-Bench可推动相关研究。

中文摘要：检索基准日益饱和，但我们认为高效搜索远非一个已解决的问题。我们识别出一类称为“斜交查询”的查询，它们寻找实例化潜在模式的文档，例如找到所有表达隐含立场推文、展示特定故障模式的聊天记录，或匹配抽象场景的转录文本。我们研究了斜交性可能产生的三种机制，并介绍了OBLIQ-Bench，这是一个由五个真实长尾语料库上的斜交搜索问题组成的套件。OBLIQ-Bench暴露了检索与验证之间被忽视的不对称性：当相关文档被呈现时，推理LLM能可靠地识别潜在相关性，但即使是最复杂的检索管道也首先无法找出大多数相关文档。我们希望OBLIQ-Bench将推动能够高效捕获大规模语料库中潜在模式和隐式信号的检索架构的研究。

Original abstract: Retrieval benchmarks are increasingly saturating, but we argue that efficient search is far from a solved problem. We identify a class of queries we call oblique, which seek documents that instantiate a latent pattern, like finding all tweets that express an implicit stance, chat logs that demonstrate a particular failure mode, or transcripts that match an abstract scenario. We study three mechanisms through which obliqueness may arise and introduce OBLIQ-Bench, a suite of five oblique search problems over real long-tail corpora. OBLIQ-Bench exposes an overlooked asymmetry between retrieval and verification, where reasoning LLMs reliably recognize latent relevance whenever relevant documents are surfaced, but even sophisticated retrieval pipelines fail to surface most relevant documents in the first place. We hope that OBLIQ-Bench will drive research into retrieval architectures that efficiently capture latent patterns and implicit signals in large corpora.

</details>


### [139] [ADEPT: An Entropy-Driven Dual-Strategy Agent for Interactive Video Retrieval](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28326v1)
*Ke Chen,Shengyuan Han,Yongfeng Huang,Yujin Zhu,Jingwei Xiong,Liang Xu,Jundong Liu*

Main category: cs.IR

Selection reason: 提出entropy-driven双策略agent用于交互式视频检索，其策略决策可迁移至一般agent设计。

TL;DR: 提出ADEPT框架，使用熵驱动决策引擎动态选择交互策略，解决视频检索中的意图-查询鸿沟，显著超越现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 用户查询模糊导致单轮检索性能瓶颈，缺乏反馈机制处理复杂意图，根本在于意图-查询鸿沟。

Method: 提出ADEPT，一种无需训练的智能体，通过熵驱动决策引擎动态选择ASK（主动询问）或REFINE（细化查询）策略来引导多轮对话。

Result: 在两个挑战性数据集上，ADEPT显著优于所有非交互式、启发式和Video-LLM基线方法。

Conclusion: 核心贡献是高效且可解释的熵驱动交互策略，为交互式视频检索设立了新基准。

中文摘要：本研究旨在解决由模糊用户查询导致的海量数据集视频检索挑战。主流单轮检索范式面临性能瓶颈，因为它们缺乏有效的反馈机制来处理复杂的搜索意图。其根本原因是“意图-查询鸿沟”，即用户的意图无法通过简单的文本查询捕获。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了ADEPT框架：一个无需训练的智能体，它首创了一种熵驱动的决策引擎，通过动态选择ASK和REFINE策略来高效引导对话。在两个具有挑战性的数据集上的实验表明，ADEPT显著优于所有非交互式、启发式和Video-LLM基线。这项工作的核心贡献是一种高效且可解释的熵驱动交互策略，为交互式视频检索领域设立了新的性能基准。

Original abstract: This research aims to solve the challenge of video retrieval from massive datasets, caused by ambiguous user queries. Prevailing single-round retrieval paradigms face a performance bottleneck, as they lack effective feedback mechanisms to handle complex search intentions. The root cause is the "Intent-Query Gap", where users' intent cannot be captured by a simple text query. To solve this, we propose the ADEPT framework: a training-free agent that pioneers an entropy-driven decision engine to efficiently guide dialogue by dynamically selecting between ASK and REFINE strategies. Experiments on two challenging datasets demonstrate that ADEPT significantly outperforms all non-interactive, heuristic, and Video-LLM baselines. The core contribution of this work is an efficient and interpretable entropy-driven interactive strategy that sets a new performance benchmark for the field of interactive video retrieval.

</details>


### [140] [Superintelligent Retrieval Agent: The Next Frontier of Agentic Retrieval](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06647v2)
*Zeyu Yang,Qi Ma,Jason Chen,Anshumali Shrivastava*

Main category: cs.IR

Selection reason: 检索agent压缩多轮搜索为单步，其检索策略可启发代码搜索agent

TL;DR: 提出SIRA，通过单步检索压缩多轮搜索，无需微调，在多个基准上取得最佳性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有检索增强智能体将检索视为黑箱，导致多轮探索、延迟和低召回，缺乏专家般的先验知识利用。

Method: SIRA：离线用LLM丰富文档缺失词汇；查询时预测缺失证据词汇；利用语料统计过滤无效词；最后执行加权BM25单步检索。

Result: 在10个BEIR基准上平均检索性能最佳，超越稠密检索器等；在NQ和HotpotQA上检索覆盖超过RL问答系统；在BrowseComp-Wikipedia上Recall@1达9.70%，优于Perplexity。

Conclusion: SIRA通过单次语料区分检索有效替代多轮探索，无需标签或微调，显著提升检索效率与性能。

中文摘要：检索增强智能体正逐渐成为大型知识库的接口，然而大多数智能体将检索视为黑箱：它们发出探索性查询、检查片段并重新表述，直到证据出现。这类似于新手搜索不熟悉数据库的方式，而非专家利用术语和可能证据的强先验知识进行导航的方式，导致了额外的检索轮次、延迟和低召回率。我们引入了超智能检索智能体（SIRA），它将检索中的超智能定义为将多轮探索性搜索压缩为一次语料区分的检索动作。SIRA不仅仅询问哪些术语相关；它询问哪些术语将目标证据与语料级别的混淆项区分开。离线时，大语言模型为每个文档丰富缺失的搜索词汇；查询时，它预测查询忽略的证据词汇；语料统计信息作为工具调用，过滤掉不存在的、过于常见或不太可能产生检索余量的术语。最后一步是结合查询与验证后的扩展进行一次加权BM25调用。在十个BEIR基准测试中，SIRA在我们比较中取得了最强的平均检索性能，击败了稠密检索器、学习型稀疏检索器和LLM搜索智能体基线，且未使用任何相关性标签或检索器微调。在下游问答任务中，仅靠检索的答案覆盖率就超过了近期在NQ和HotpotQA上经过RL训练的智能代理问答系统。我们还引入了BrowseComp-Wikipedia，一个包含232个BrowseComp派生查询、涵盖25,587,229篇文档的维基百科索引的硬搜索基准。即使没有索引时增强，仅使用基于维基百科类别的接地信息，SIRA在每种预算下都优于多轮Perplexity智能体，达到了9.70%的Recall@1、15.27%的Recall@10和36.14%的Recall@100。

Original abstract: Retrieval-augmented agents are increasingly the interface to large knowledge bases, yet most treat retrieval as a black box: they issue exploratory queries, inspect snippets, and reformulate until evidence emerges. This resembles how a newcomer searches an unfamiliar database rather than how an expert navigates it with strong priors about terminology and likely evidence, causing extra retrieval rounds, latency, and poor recall.
  We introduce \textit{Superintelligent Retrieval Agent} (SIRA), which casts \emph{superintelligence} in retrieval as compressing multi-round exploratory search into a single corpus-discriminative retrieval action. SIRA does not merely ask which terms are relevant; it asks which terms separate the desired evidence from corpus-level confusers. Offline, an LLM enriches each document with missing search vocabulary; at query time, it predicts evidence vocabulary the query omits; and corpus statistics serve as tool calls that filter terms that are absent, overly common, or unlikely to create retrieval margin. The final step is a single weighted BM25 call combining the query with the validated expansion.
  Across ten BEIR benchmarks, SIRA achieves the strongest average retrieval performance in our comparison, beating dense retrievers, learned sparse retrievers, and LLM search-agent baselines while using no relevance labels or retriever fine-tuning. On downstream QA, its retrieval-only answer coverage exceeds recent RL-trained agentic QA systems on NQ and HotpotQA. We also introduce \textbf{BrowseComp-Wikipedia}, a hard-search benchmark of 232 BrowseComp-derived queries over a 25,587,229-document Wikipedia index. Even without index-time enrichment, using only grounded Wikipedia categories, SIRA outperforms multi-round Perplexity agents at every budget, reaching 9.70% Recall@1, 15.27% Recall@10, and 36.14% Recall@100.

</details>

### [141] [Active Learning for Communication Structure Optimization in LLM-Based Multi-Agent Systems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05703v2)
*Huchen Yang,Xinghao Dong,Dan Negrut,Jin-Long Wu*

Main category: cs.MA

Selection reason: 多agent系统通信结构主动学习优化，提升效率与鲁棒性

TL;DR: 提出基于集成信息论的任务选择框架，主动识别最有价值的任务以优化LLM-MAS通信结构，在有限预算下提升稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有通信结构优化方法依赖随机采样任务，任务信息量不均导致优化不稳定且对训练集敏感，需主动选择有价值任务。

Method: 提出集成信息论框架，使用集成卡尔曼反演估计任务对图参数分布的影响，结合嵌入代表性选择构建紧凑候选池，并采用代理建模和批量汤普森采样提高可扩展性。

Result: 在良性设置和智能体攻击设置中验证了方法在计算预算受限下对通信结构优化的有效性。

Conclusion: 该方法能有效识别信息性任务，提升通信结构优化在有限预算下的稳定性和性能。

中文摘要：优化基于大语言模型的多智能体系统（LLM-MAS）的通信结构已被证明可以提高下游性能并减少令牌使用。现有方法通常依赖于随机采样的训练任务。然而，任务在难度和领域上可能有很大差异，因此它们对于更新通信结构的信息量并不相等，这使得在有限训练预算下的优化往往不稳定且对特定训练集高度敏感。为了主动识别最有价值的任务以优化通信结构，我们提出了一个基于集成信息论的任务选择框架。所提出方法通过候选任务改变图参数分布的程度来估计任务信息量，并使用集成卡尔曼反演作为相应贝叶斯更新的高效且无导数的近似。得到的估计器特别适合黑盒和噪声多智能体系统。为了增强可扩展性，我们通过基于嵌入的代表性选择构建紧凑的候选池，并将信息性选择与代理建模和批量汤普森采样相结合。我们在良性设置和存在智能体攻击的设置中验证了我们的方法，展示了其在计算预算受限条件下优化通信结构的有效性。

Original abstract: Optimizing the communication structure of large language model based multi-agent systems (LLM-MAS) has been shown to improve downstream performance and reduce token usage. Existing methods typically rely on randomly sampled training tasks. However, tasks may differ substantially in difficulty and domain, and thus they are not equally informative for updating communication structure, making optimization under limited training budgets often unstable and highly sensitive to the particular training set. To actively identify the most valuable tasks for communication-structure optimization, we propose an ensemble-based information-theoretic task selection framework. The proposed method estimates task informativeness by how much a candidate task changes the distribution over graph parameters, using ensemble Kalman inversion as an efficient and derivative-free approximation of the corresponding Bayesian update. The resulting estimator is especially suitable for black-box and noisy multi-agent systems. To enhance scalability, we construct a compact candidate pool through embedding-based representative selection and combine the informative selection with surrogate modeling and batch Thompson sampling. We validate our method in both benign settings and settings with agent attacks, demonstrating its effectiveness for communication-structure optimization under constrained computational budgets.

</details>


### [142] [Auto Research with Specialist Agents Develops Effective and Non-Trivial Training Recipes](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05724v1)
*Jingjie Ning,Xiaochuan Li,Ji Zeng,Hao Kang,Chenyan Xiong*

Main category: cs.MA

Selection reason: 多agent自动研究系统，自主编写代码、运行实验并吸收反馈，可迁移至自动代码优化

TL;DR: 提出并验证了一个由外部测量驱动的自动研究闭环，通过谱系反馈使代理自主改进代码和配方，无需人工干预。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自动研究缺乏可审计的轨迹和闭环反馈机制，无法将失败经验转化为后续改进。

Method: 构建封闭经验循环，包含专业代理、谱系共享和实验轨迹记录；代理根据评估反馈进行程序级配方编辑。

Result: 在三个任务上取得显著改进：参数高尔夫验证bpb降低0.81%，NanoChat-D12 CORE提升38.7%，CIFAR-10 Airbench96耗时减少4.59%。

Conclusion: 该闭环能够自主编写代码、应用已知技术并改进公开的起始配方，未来可拓展至更复杂场景。

中文摘要：我们研究了自动研究作为由外部测量驱动的封闭经验循环。每次提交的实验都携带一个假设、一个可执行的代码编辑、一个评估者拥有的结果以及反馈，该反馈为下一次提案塑形。输出不是生成的论文或单一的模型检查点，而是一个可审计的提案、代码差异、实验、分数和失败标签的轨迹。我们通过专业代理实例化这个循环，这些代理分割配方表面并在实验间共享测量的谱系。中心实证发现是，谱系反馈让代理能够将评估结果（包括崩溃、预算超支、大小失败和准确率门槛未达标）转化为后来的程序级配方编辑，而非一次性建议。在一次性设置和启动后的1,197个头条运行实验加上600个参数高尔夫控制实验中，人类在搜索过程中没有选择提案、编辑配方、覆盖分数或修复失败的实验。在三个头条运行中，相同的提交实验循环将参数高尔夫验证bpb降低了0.81%，将NanoChat-D12 CORE提升了38.7%，并将CIFAR-10 Airbench96的挂钟时间减少了4.59%，每个任务由各自的外部评估器和合法性检查衡量。轨迹包括对157个头条运行提交的严格架构域审计和程序重写，例如NanoChat注意力核路径更改。在此范围内，该循环自主编写代码、提交实验、吸收反馈、在每个环境中应用和组合已知技术，并改进公开的起始配方。

Original abstract: We study auto research as a closed empirical loop driven by external measurement. Each submitted trial carries a hypothesis, an executable code edit, an evaluator-owned outcome, and feedback that shapes the next proposal. The output is not a generated paper or a single model checkpoint, but an auditable trajectory of proposals, code diffs, experiments, scores, and failure labels. We instantiate this loop with specialist agents that partition recipe surfaces and share measured lineage across trials. The central empirical finding is that lineage feedback lets agents turn evaluator outcomes, including crashes, budget overruns, size failures, and accuracy-gate misses, into later program-level recipe edits rather than one-shot suggestions. Across 1,197 headline-run trials plus 600 Parameter Golf control trials after one-time setup and launch, humans did not choose proposals, edit recipes, override scores, or repair failed trials during the search. In the three headline runs, the same submitted-trial loop reduces Parameter Golf validation bpb by $0.81\%$, raises NanoChat-D12 CORE by $38.7\%$, and reduces CIFAR-10 Airbench96 wallclock by $4.59\%$, with each task measured by its own external evaluator and legality checks. The trace includes a strict architecture-domain audit of 157 headline-run submissions and program rewrites such as a NanoChat attention-kernel path change. Within this scope the loop autonomously writes code, submits experiments, absorbs feedback, applies and combines known techniques inside each environment, and improves public starting recipes.

</details>


### [143] [Improving the Efficiency of Language Agent Teams with Adaptive Task Graphs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06320v1)
*Elizabeth Mieczkowski,Alexander Ku,Tiwalayo Eisape,Dilip Arumugam,John Matters,Katherine M. Collins,Ilia Sucholutsky,Thomas L. Griffiths*

Main category: cs.MA

Selection reason: 提出LATTE框架用于语言agent团队协调，使用自适应任务图，直接贡献于多agent协作方法。

TL;DR: LATTE是一种受分布式系统启发的LLM团队协调框架，通过动态维护共享协调图来减少资源浪费和协调失败，同时保持或提升准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM团队协调方法要么高度结构化（固定角色、流水线、先验分解），要么完全无结构（导致错误传播、冲突、资源浪费），缺乏平衡效率和适应性的方案。

Method: 提出LATTE框架，智能体协作构建和维护一个共享的、演化的协调图，该图编码子任务依赖、智能体分配和进度状态，允许动态分配工作、调整协调和发现新任务。

Result: 在多个协作任务和多种基础模型上，LATTE降低了令牌使用、挂钟时间、通信和协调失败（如文件冲突和冗余输出），同时准确性匹配或超过MetaGPT、去中心化团队、Leader-Worker层级和静态分解等标准方法。

Conclusion: LATTE是一种有效的LLM团队协调框架，能够在保持一致性的同时提高效率并减少失败。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）正越来越多地被部署在团队中，然而现有的协调方法往往占据两个极端。高度结构化的方法依赖于事先分配好的固定角色、流水线或任务分解。相比之下，完全无结构的团队能够实现适应性和探索，但存在效率低下的问题，如错误传播、智能体间冲突以及资源浪费（以时间、令牌或文件操作衡量）。我们引入了用于任务演化的语言智能体团队（LATTE），这是一个受分布式系统启发的协调LLM团队的框架，其中处理器必须在部分可观测性和通信约束下运行。在LATTE中，一组智能体协作构建和维护一个共享的、不断演化的协调图，该图编码了子任务依赖关系、个体智能体分配以及子任务进度的当前状态。该协议在保持一致性的同时，赋予智能体动态分配工作、调整协调和发现新任务的能力。在多个协作任务和各种基础模型上，我们展示了LATTE如何减少令牌使用、挂钟时间、通信和协调失败（例如文件冲突和冗余输出），同时匹配或超过标准设计的准确性，包括MetaGPT、去中心化团队、自上而下的领导者-工作者层级结构以及静态分解。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly deployed in teams, yet existing coordination approaches often occupy two extremes. Highly structured methods rely on fixed roles, pipelines, or task decompositions assigned a priori. In contrast, fully unstructured teams enable adaptability and exploration but suffer from inefficiencies such as error propagation, inter-agent conflicts, and wasted resources (measured in time, tokens, or file operations). We introduce Language Agent Teams for Task Evolution (LATTE), a framework for coordinating LLM teams inspired by distributed systems, where processors must operate under partial observability and communication constraints. In LATTE, a team of agents collaboratively construct and maintain a shared, evolving coordination graph which encodes sub-task dependencies, individual agent assignment, and the current state of sub-task progress. This protocol maintains consistency while empowering agents to dynamically allocate work, adapt coordination, and discover new tasks. Across multiple collaborative tasks and a variety of base models, we demonstrate how LATTE reduces token usage, wall-clock time, communication, and coordination failures (e.g. file conflicts and redundant outputs) while matching or exceeding the accuracy of standard designs including MetaGPT, decentralized teams, top-down Leader-Worker hierarchies, and static decompositions.

</details>


### [144] [Coordination Matters: Evaluation of Cooperative Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06557v1)
*Maria Ana Cardei,Matthew Landers,Afsaneh Doryab*

Main category: cs.MA

Selection reason: 合作多智能体强化学习的协调评估，提出过程级诊断方法，可迁移至多agent系统。

TL;DR: 提出协调感知评估视角，通过STAT测试平台分析发现，相似回报下不同MARL方法的协调机制存在差异，强调过程级诊断的必要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有MARL基准仅关注回报等聚合指标，无法揭示智能体协调过程，尤其在规模组合爆炸时，因此需要补充过程级诊断。

Method: 使用受承诺约束的空间任务分配测试平台STAT，系统改变智能体、任务和环境规模，评估六种基于值的MARL方法（不同集中化程度）。

Result: 相似回报趋势可能对应不同的协调机制（如冗余分配、分配多样性、任务完成效率差异）；性能受分配压力、稀疏决策机会和冗余选择影响，而不仅是动作空间大小。

Conclusion: 协调感知评估是回报基准的必要补充，能揭示MARL方法在规模下的真实协调行为。

中文摘要：合作多智能体强化学习（MARL）基准测试通常强调总体结果，如回报、成功率或完成时间。虽然这些指标至关重要，但它们往往无法揭示智能体如何协调，特别是在智能体、任务和联合分配选择组合规模呈组合爆炸增长的场景中。我们提出了一种协调感知的评估视角，用过程级诊断补充回报。我们通过STAT实例化这一视角，STAT是一个受承诺约束的空间任务分配测试平台，该系统在保持观察访问和任务规则不变的情况下，系统地改变智能体、任务和环境规模。我们评估了六种具有代表性的基于值的MARL方法，涵盖不同程度的集中化。我们的结果表明，相似的回报趋势可能反映不同的协调机制，包括冗余分配、分配多样性和任务完成效率的差异。我们发现，在受承诺约束的任务分配中，规模下的性能不仅受名义动作空间大小的影响，还受分配压力、稀疏决策机会以及相互依赖的智能体之间的冗余选择的影响。我们的发现激励将协调感知评估作为合作MARL中基于回报的基准测试的必要补充。

Original abstract: Cooperative multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) benchmarks commonly emphasize aggregate outcomes such as return, success rate, or completion time. While essential, these metrics often fail to reveal how agents coordinate, particularly in settings where agents, tasks, and joint assignment choices scale combinatorially. We propose a coordination-aware evaluation perspective that supplements return with process-level diagnostics. We instantiate this perspective using STAT, a controlled commitment-constrained spatial task-allocation testbed that systematically varies agents, tasks, and environment size while holding observation access and task rules fixed. We evaluate six representative value-based MARL methods across varying levels of centralization. Our results show that similar return trends can reflect distinct coordination mechanisms, including differences in redundant assignment, assignment diversity, and task-completion efficiency. We find that in commitment-constrained task allocation, performance under scale is shaped not only by nominal action-space size, but also by assignment pressure, sparse decision opportunities, and redundant choices among interdependent agents. Our findings motivate coordination-aware evaluation as a necessary complement to return-based benchmarking for cooperative MARL.

</details>
